	Sin-Beng7-Ki3	(5)
[1]	Mou5-se ti7 Iok-tan3 goa7, ti7 khong3-ia2 Sou2-hut tui3-bin7 e5 A-lah8-pa, chiu7-si7 ti7 Pa-lan5, To5-hut, Lah8-pan, Hap-se2-liok8, Ti2-sat-hap e5 tiong-kan, tui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3-lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  2). Tui3 Ho5-liat8 keng-ke3 Se-jiN2 soaN e5 lou7 kau3 Ka-te-su Pa-ni5-a, u7 chap8-it jit8 e5 lou7-cham7.  3). Ti7 te7 si3-chap8 ni5, chap8-it geh8 chhoe-it jit8, Mou5-se chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa it-chhe3 sou2 beng7-leng7 i e5, long2 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2.  4). Hit-si5 i i2-keng phah-iaN5 khia7-khi2 ti7 Hi-sit8-pun2 e5 A-mou5-li7 ong5 Se-hong5, kap khia7-khi2 ti7 I2-tek-lai5, A-su-tha-liok8 e5 Pa-san ong5 Gok8;  5). Mou5-se ti7 Iok-tan3 goa7 e5 Mou5-ap toe7, khi2-thau5 thoan5 chit e5 lut8-hoat kong2,  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 Ho5-liat8 hoan-hu3 lan2 kong2, Lin2 khia7-khi2 chit e5 soaN i2-keng ku2 lah;  7). tioh8 khi2-sin oat8-tng2 kau3 A-mou5-li7 lang5 e5 soaN-toe7, kap kun7-oa2 hia e5 tak8 sou2-chai7, ti7 A-lah8-pa, ti7 soaN-toe7, ti7 piN5-iuN5, ti7 lam5-hng, ian5-hai2 it-tai3, Ka-lam5 lang5 e5 toe7, kap Li7-pa-lun3, koh kau3 toa7-ho5, chiu7-si7 Pek-lah8 ho5.  8). TaN Goa2 eng7 chit e5 toe7 pai5-liat8 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5, lin2 tioh8 jip8-khi3 tit-tioh8 i lai5 choe3 giap8, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 lin2 e5 chou2, A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok, chiu3-choa7 beh siuN2-su3 in kap in e5 hou7-e3 e5 toe7.
	9). Hit-si5 goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, Lin2 e5 chek-seng5, goa2 ka-ki7 chit8-e5 tam-tng boe7 khi2.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 hou7 lin2 ke-thiN choe7-choe7, khoaN3 ah, lin2 kin-a2-jit8 chhin-chhiuN7 thiN-teng2 e5 chhiN hiah-choe7.  11). Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 liat8-chou2 e5 Siong7-te3, hou7 lin2 pi2 hian7-kim ke chheng-pe7 choe7, ia7 chiau3 I sou2 eng3-un2 lin2--e5 su3-hok lin2.  12). Lin2 e5 tang7-taN3, lin2 e5 chek-seng5, kap lin2 e5 oan-ke, goa2 ka-ki7 chit8-e5 thai2-tho2 tam-tng oe7 khi2 ah?  13). Lin2 tioh8 chiau3 tak8 chi-phai3 keng2 u7 ti3-hui7, u7 kian3-sek, u7 beng5-bong7 e5 lang5, goa2 siat-lip8 in choe3 lin2 e5 siu2-leng2.  14). Lin2 in3 goa2 kong2, Li2 sou2-kong2-e5 si7 ho2, thang kiaN5--i.  15). Goa2 chiu7 chiong lin2 tak8 chi-phai3 e5 siu2-leng2, chiu7-si7 u7 ti3-hui7, u7 beng5-bong7 e5 lang5, siat-lip8 in choe3 siu2-leng2, chiu7-si7 chhian-chong2, peh-chong2, ngou2-sip8-hu-tiong2, sip8-hu-tiong2, kap iu2-si, chiau3 lin2 e5 chi-phai3, lai5 koan2-li2 lin2.  16). Tng-si5 goa2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5 sim2-phoaN3-koaN kong2, Lin2 ti7 lin2 hiaN-ti7 tiong sim2-phoaN3, hek8-si7 lang5 kap i e5 hiaN-ti7, a2-si7 kap in tiong-kan e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, u7 saN-ko3, tioh8 chiau3 kong-to7 phoaN3-toan3;  17). sim2-phoaN3 e5 si5, m7-thang khoaN3 lang5 e5 goa7-mau7, jiok8 kap kiong5 piN5-piN5 tioh8 thiaN i; m7-thang kiaN-ui3 lang5; in-ui7 sim2-phoaN3 siok8 ti7 Siong7-te3; lin2 oh kai2-koat e5 su7, hou7 i kau3 goa2 chia, goa2 chiu7 phoaN3-toan3 i.  18). Hit-si5 goa2 chiong lin2 sou2 eng-kai kiaN5 e5 su7 long2 beng7-leng7 lin2.
	19). Lan2 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 lan2 e5, tui3 Ho5-liat8 khi2-sin, keng-ke3 lin2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 toa7 koh thang kiaN e5 khong3-ia2, lou7 tui3 A-mou5-li7 lang5 e5 soaN-toe7; lan2 chiu7 kau3 Ka-te-su Pa-ni5-a.  20). Goa2 tui3 lin2 kong2, Lin2 i2-keng kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 lan2 A-mou5-li7 lang5 e5 soaN-toe7.  21). KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, i2-keng chiong hit e5 toe7 pai5-liat8 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; li2 tioh8 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 tui3 li2 kong2 e5, chiuN7-khi3 lai5 tit-tioh8 i choe3-giap8; boh8-tit kiaN, boh8-tit lun2.  22). Hit-si5 lin2 long2 chiu7-kun7 goa2 lai5 kong2, Lan2 tioh8 chhe lang5 tai7-seng khi3, ka7 lan2 thau-khoaN3 hit e5 toe7, he5-hok lan2, khoaN3 lan2 tioh8 tui3 sim2-mih8 lou7 chiuN7-khi3, sim2-mih8 siaN5 jip8-khi3.  23). Che oe7 goa2 khoaN3 choe3-ho2; goa2 chiu7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan keng2 chap8-ji7 lang5, mui2 chi-phai3 chit8 lang5;  24). in chiu7 oat8-tng2-sin chiuN7 soaN-toe7 khi3, kau3 I2-sit8-kok e5 soaN-kok, thau-khoaN3 i.  25). In chhiu2--nih theh8 hit sou2-chai7 e5 ke2-chi2, toa3 lai5 kau3 lan2 hia, he5-hok lan2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 lan2-e5, si7 ho2 e5 thou2-toe7.
	26). Chong2-si7 lin2 m7-kheng2 chiuN7-khi3, poe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 beng7-leng7;  27). koh ti7 lin2 e5 pou3-piN5-lai7 ai-oan3 kong2, In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa oan3-hun7 lan2, sou2-i2 chhoa7 lan2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7, beh chiong lan2 kau ti7 A-mou5-li7 lang5 e5 chhiu2, chau5-biat8 lan2.  28). Lan2 beh chiuN7-khi3 toh-loh8 ah? Lan2 e5 hiaN-ti7 hou7 lan2 sit-chi3, kong2, Hia e5 peh-siN3 pi2 lan2 khah toa7 khah lo3, siaN5 khoah-toa7 koh kian-kou3, koaiN5 kau3 tu2-thiN; koh goan2 ti7-hia khoaN3-kiN3 A-lap8 chok8 e5 lang5.  29). Goa2 chiu7 tui3 lin2 kong2, Boh8-tit lun2, boh8-tit kiaN in.  30). KiaN5 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, beh thoe3 lin2 kau-chian3, chhin-chhiuN7 I ti7 Ai-kip8 ui7-tioh8 lin2 lai5 kiaN5 ti7 lin2 bak8-chiu-cheng5 it-chhe3 e5 su7;  31). koh chhin-chhiuN7 I kiaN5 ti7 khong3-ia2, ti7-hia li2 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 li2 it-chhe3 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 iang7 li2, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 iang7 i e5 kiaN2 chit8-iuN7, kau3 lin2 kau3 ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7.  32). Chong2-si7 lin2 ti7 chit e5 su7 m7-sin3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3;  33). I ti7 lou7--nih, ti7 lin2 e5 thau5-cheng5 teh kiaN5, ka7 lin2 chhe7 an-iaN5 e5 sou2-chai7; mi5-si5 eng7 he2, jit8-si5 eng7 hun5, chi2-si7 lin2 sou2 tioh8 kiaN5 e5 lou7.  34). Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3 chiah e5 oe7 e5 siaN, chiu7 siu7-khi3, chiu3-choa7 kong2,  35). Chit e5 phaiN2 se3-tai7 e5 lang5 koat-toan3 bo5 chit8-e5 oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 chiu3-choa7 siuN2-su3 lin2 liat8-chou2 e5 ho2-toe7;  36). chi2-u7 Ia5-hu-ni5 e5 kiaN2 Ka-lek8 beh tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3; koh Goa2 beh eng7 i sou2 tah8--tioh8 e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 i, kap i e5 kiaN2-sun; in-ui7 i choan-sim te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  37). Ia5-ho5-hoa ui7-tioh8 lin2 e5 ian5-kou3 ia7 siu7-khi3 goa2, kong2, Li2 ia7 boe7 tit-tioh8 jip8 hit e5 sou2-chai7;  38). kun-sui5 li2 e5, Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a, i beh jip8-khi3 hia; li2 tioh8 iong2-chong3 i e5 sim-chi3, in-ui7 i beh hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 seng5-chiap hit e5 sou2-chai7;  39). koh lin2 e5 gin2-na2, chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 kong2 beh siu7-liah8-e5, kap kin-a2-jit8 lin2 hiah-e5 boe7 hiau2 ho2-phaiN2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, beh jip8-khi3 hia; Goa2 beh chiong hit sou2-chai7 hou7 in, in beh tit-tioh8 choe3-giap8;  40). lun7-kau3 lin2, lin2 tioh8 oat8-to3-tng2 khi2-sin, tui3 Ang5-hai2 e5 lou7 khi3 khong3-ia2.
	41). Hit-si5 lin2 in3 goa2 kong2, Goan2 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; taN goan2 beh chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 it-chhe3 sou2 beng7-leng7 e5, chiuN7-khi3 kau-chian3.  Tui3 hit-tiap8 lin2 tak8-lang5 toa3 kun-khi3, sui5-pian7 chiuN7-khi3 soaN-toe7.  42). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 goa2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 ka7 in kong2, M7-thang chiuN7-khi3, ia7 m7-thang kau-chian3; in-ui7 Goa2 bo5 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan, kiaN-liau2 lin2 thai5-su tui3-tek8.  43). Goa2 chiu7 ka7 lin2 kong2; chong2-si7 lin2 m7 thiaN-than3, poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7, chu7-choan chiuN7-khi3 soaN-toe7.  44). Tiam3 ti7 soaN-nih e5 A-mou5-li7 lang5 chiu7 chhut-lai5 kong-kek lin2, chhin-chhiuN7 phang tui-koaN2 lin2 chit8-poaN, ti7 Se-jiN2 thai5-iaN5 lin2, tit8--kau3 Ho5-jiN2-ma2.  45). Lin2 chiu7 to3-tng2 lai5, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 thi5-khau3; chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa m7-thiaN lin2 e5 siaN, ia7 m7 aN3 hi7-khang ng3 lin2.  46). Lin2 chiu7 tiam3 ti7 Ka-te-su choe7-choe7 jit8, chiau3 lin2 tiam3 ti7-hia e5 jit8.

[2]	Chit-tiap8 liau2-au7, lan2 oat8-to3-tng2 khi2-sin, tui3 Ang5-hai2 e5 lou7 khi3 khong3-ia2; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 tui3 goa2 kong2--e5; lan2 seh8 Se-jiN2 soaN choe7-choe7 jit8.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 goa2 kong2,  3). Lin2 seh8 chit e5 soaN ku2 lah; tioh8 oat8-tng2 ng3 pak--si3 khi3.  4). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 peh-siN3 kong2, I2-so3 e5 kiaN2-sun lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7 tiam3 ti7 Se-jiN2; lin2 beh keng-ke3 in e5 keng2-kai3, in beh kiaN lin2; sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 put-chi2 kin2-sin7;  5). m7-thang kap in cheng-chian3 in e5 toe7, chiu7 na7 chit8 kha-jiah-ui7, Goa2 long2 bo5 hou7 lin2, in-ui7 Goa2 i2-keng chiong Se-jiN2 soaN hou7 I2-so3 choe3-giap8.  6). Lin2 tioh8 eng7 gun5 tui3 in boe2 bi2-niu5 lai5 chiah8, ia7 tioh8 eng7 gun5 tui3 in boe2 chui2 lai5 lim;  7). in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 kang, su3-hok li2; li2 kiaN5 chit e5 toa7 e5 khong3-ia2, I long2 chai; chi2 si3-chap8 ni5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kap li2 ti7-teh, li2 long2 bo5 khiam3-kheh chit8-hang7.  8). Tui3 an2-ni, lan2 li7-khui lan2 e5 hiaN-ti7 I2-so3 e5 kiaN2-sun, khia7-khi2 ti7 Se-jiN2 e5; tui3 A-lah8-pa e5 lou7 keng-ke3 I2-lah8-tha, I2-sun5-ka-piat8.
	9). Lan2 chiu7 oat8-tng2 keng-ke3 Mou5-ap khong3-ia2 e5 lou7 khi3.  Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, M7-thang kiau2-jiau2 Mou5-ap lang5, ia7 m7-thang kap in kau-chian3; in e5 toe7 Goa2 long2 bo5 beh hou7 li2 choe3-giap8; in-ui7 Goa2 i2-keng chiong A-jiN2 hou7 Lo5-tek e5 kiaN2-sun choe3-giap8.  10). (Cha2-cheng5 u7 I2-bi2 lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7-hia, peh-siN3 choe7, toa7 koh lo3, chhin-chhiuN7 A-lap8 lang5 chit8-iuN7.  11). In ia7 hou7 lang5 sng3 in choe3 Li7-hoat8-im lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 A-lap8 lang5 chit8-iuN7; chong2-si7 Mou5-ap lang5 chheng i choe3 I2-bi2 lang5.  12). Cha2-cheng5 Ho5-li7 lang5 ia7 khia7-khi2 ti7 Se-jiN2; chong2-si7 I2-so3 e5 kiaN2-sun soa3-chiap i; in ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 chau5-biat8 in, lai5 toa3 ti7 in e5 sou2-chai7, chhin-chhiuN7 I2-sek-liat8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa siuN2-su3 in choe3-giap8 e5 toe7 sou2 kiaN5 e5.)  13). TaN lin2 tioh8 khi2-lai5 ke3 Sat-liat8 khoe; tui3 an2-ni lan2 ke3 Sat-liat8 khoe.  14). Tui3 lan2 li7-khui Ka-te-su Pa-ni5-a, kau3 ke3 Sat-liat8 khoe e5 jit8, kiong7 saN-chap8-poeh ni5; kau3 hit-tai7 e5 bu2-su7 long2 si2-bo5 ti7 kun-iaN5-tiong, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 in sou2 chiu3-choa7-e5.  15). Koh Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 kong-kek in, tui3 kun-iaN5-tiong chau5-biat8 in, kau3 in long2 si2-bo5.
	16). Bu2-su7 tui3 peh-siN3-tiong long2 chau5-biat8 si2-bo5 i2-au7,  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 goa2 kong2, 18). Li2 kin-a2-jit8 tioh8 tui3 Mou5-ap e5 keng2-kai3 A-jiN2 keng-ke3;  19). kiaN5 kun7 A-bun5 lang5 e5 tui3-bin7, m7-thang kiau2-jiau2 in, ia7 m7-thang kap in cheng-chian3; in-ui7 A-bun5 lang5 e5 toe7 Goa2 bo5 hou7 lin2 choe3-giap8, in-ui7 Goa2 i2-keng siuN2-su3 Lo5-tek e5 kiaN2-sun choe3-giap8.  20). (Hit e5 toe7 ia7 sng3-choe3 Li7-hoat8-im lang5 e5 toe7; cha2-cheng5 Li7-hoat8-im lang5 tiam3 ti7-hia, A-bun5 lang5 chheng in choe3 San3-song3-beng5;  21). hiah e5 peh-siN3 choe7, toa7 koh lo3, chhin-chhiuN7 A-lap8 lang5 chit8-iuN7; chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 A-bun5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 chau5-biat8 in, in chiu7 tit-tioh8 in e5 toe7, soa3-chiap khia7-khi2;  22). chhin-chhiuN7 I ui7 I2-so3 e5 kiaN2-sun, khia7-khi2 ti7 Se-jiN2 e5, biat8 Ho5-li7 lang5 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5, in chiu7 soa3-chiap khia7-khi2 in e5 toe7 kau3 kin-a2-jit8;  23). koh u7 A-oe7 lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7 hiuN-sia7, soa3 kau3 Ka-sat e5; tui3 Ka-hui2-thok chhut-lai5 e5 Ka-hui2-thok lang5 biat8 in, lai5 khia7-khi2 ti7 in e5 ui7.)  24). TaN lin2 tioh8 khi2-lai5, khi2-sin ke3 A-lun3 e5 soaN-kok; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 i2-keng chiong A-mou5-li7 lang5 Hi-sit8-pun2 ong5 Se-hong5, kap i e5 toe7, kau ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2-thau5; li2 tioh8 khi2-chhiu2 tit-tioh8 i e5 toe7, khi3 kap i kau-chian3.  25). Tui3 kin-a2-jit8 khi2, Goa2 beh hou7 thiN-e7 ban7 peh-siN3, thiaN-kiN3 li2 e5 mia5-siaN e5, kiaN lin2, lun2 lin2; koh in-ui7 li2 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, thong3-khou2.
	26). Goa2 chiu7 tui3 Ki-ti2-bok8 e5 khong3-ia2, chhe su3-chia2 khi3 kiN3 Hi-sit8-pun2 ong5 Se-hong5, eng7 ho5-peng5 e5 oe7 kong2,  27). Kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 goa2 tui3 li2 e5 toe7 keng-ke3; goa2 beh kiaN5 toa7-lou7, bo5 phian-cho2, bo5 phian-iu7;  28). li2 theh8 goa2 e5 gun5, boe7 bi2-niu5 hou7 goa2 chiah8, theh8 goa2 e5 gun5, eng7 chui2 boe7 goa2 lim; tok8-tok8 chun2 goa2 pou7-kiaN5 ke3-khi3;  29). chhin-chhiuN7 tiam3 ti7 Se-jiN2 e5 I2-so3 e5 kiaN2-sun, kap tiam3 ti7 A-jiN2 e5 Mou5-ap lang5 khoan2-thai7 goa2 chit8-iuN7; theng3-hau7 goa2 ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5, jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 goan2 e5 toe7.  30). Chong2-si7 Hi-sit8-pun2 ong5 Se-hong5 m7-kheng2 hou7 lan2 tui3 i hia keng-ke3, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 hou7 i e5 seng3-cheng5 kou3-chip, sim ngi7, ui7-tioh8 beh chiong i kau-hu3 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2; chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 chit8-iuN7.  31). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 goa2 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, tui3 chit-tiap8 khi2, Goa2 beh chiong Se-hong5 kap i e5 toe7, kau-hu3 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 taN tioh8 tit-tioh8 i e5 toe7 choe3-giap8.  32). Hit-si5 Se-hong5 kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 chhut-lai5 ti2-tek8 lan2, kau-chian3 ti7 Nga2-chap8.  33). Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiong i kau-hu3 lan2, lan2 chiu7 phah-si2 i, kap i e5 kiaN2, i2-kip8 i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3.  34). Tng hit-si5 lan2 chhu2 i long2-chong2 e5 siaN5, chau5-biat8 u7 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 siaN5, lian5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap gin2-na2, bo5 lau5 chit8-e5;  35). tok8-tok8 cheng-siN kap sou2 chhiuN2 tak8 e5 siaN5 e5 chong-but8, long2 chhu2 lai5 choe3 ka-ki7 e5 lou7-eng7.  36). Tui3 A-lun3 soaN-kok-piN e5 A-lo5-jiN2, i2-kip8 soaN-kok tiong e5 siaN5, kau3 ti7 Ki-liat8, bo5 chit8 e5 siaN5 kian-kou3, hou7 lan2 chhu2 i bo5 tioh8; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 long2 kau-hu3 lan2;  37). chi2-u7 A-bun5 lang5 e5 toe7, Nga2-phok ho5-piN e5 toe7, kap soaN-toe7 chiah e5 siaN5, kap Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 kim3 lan2 khi3 e5 toe7, li2 long2 bo5 oa2-kun7 i.

[3]	Lan2 chiu7 oat8-tng2-sin chiuN7 Pa-san e5 lou7 khi3; Pa-san ong5 kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3 long2-chhut-lai5 ti2-tek8 lan2, chiu7 ti7 I2-tek-lai5 kau-chian3.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 goa2 kong2, Boh8-tit kiaN i, in-ui7 Goa2 i2-keng chiong i kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, kap i e5 toe7, long2 kau ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2; li2 tioh8 khoan2-thai7 i chhin-chhiuN7 khoan2-thai7 tiam3 ti7 Hi-sit8-pun2 e5 A-mou5-li7 ong5 Se-hong5 chit8-iuN7.  3). Tui3 hit-tiap8 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ia7 chiong Pa-san ong5 Gok8, kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, long2 kau ti7 lan2 e5 chhiu2; lan2 chiu7 phah-si2 in, bo5 lau5 chit8-e5.  4). Hit-si5 lan2 chhu2 i sou2 u7 e5 siaN5, bo5 chit8 e5 siaN5 bo5 hou7 lan2 chhu2 i, kiong7 lak8-chap8 e5 siaN5; che si7 A-jiN2-ko-pek e5 choan5-keng2, chiu7-si7 Gok8 e5 kok ti7 Pa-san e5.  5). Chiah-e5 long2 si7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5, u7 koaiN5 e5 chhiuN5, u7 mng5, u7 kong5; chiah-e5 i2-goa7 iau2-u7 choe7-choe7 bo5 siaN5-chhiuN5 e5 pou-thau5.  6). Lan2 it-chin7 biat8 in, chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5 khoan2-thai7 Hi-sit8-pun2 ong5 Se-hong5 chit8-iuN7, biat8 u7 lang5 khia7-khi2 e5 siaN5, lian5 hu7-jin5-lang5, kap gin2-na2;  7). tok8-tok8 it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN, kap siaN5-tiong e5 chong-but8, lan2 long2 chhu2 lai5 choe3 ka-ki7 e5 lou7-eng7.  8). Hit-si5 lan2 tui3 Iok-tan3 hit-peng5, nng7 e5 A-mou5-li7 ong5 e5 chhiu2, chhiuN2 i e5 toe7, tui3 A-lun3 e5 soaN-kok kau3 Hek-bun5 soaN.  9). (Chit e5 Hek-bun5, Se-tun3 lang5 chheng i choe3 Se-lian5; A-mou5-li7 lang5 chheng i choe3 Si7-ni5-jiN2.)  10). Lan2 chhiuN2 piN5-iuN5 tak8 e5 siaN5, Ki-liat8 choan5-toe7, Pa-san choan5-toe7, tit8-kau3 Sat-ka kap I2-tek-lai5, long2 si7 Pa-san ong5 Gok8 kok-lai7 e5 siaN5.  11). (Li7-hoat8-im lang5 sou2 lau5 e5, chi2-u7 chhun Pa-san ong5 Gok8; khoaN3 ah, i e5 bin5-chhng5 si7 thih e5 bin5-chhng5, tng5 kau2-tiu2, khoah si3-tiu2, long2 si7 eng7 lang5 e5 tiu2 choe3-pan7; hian7-kim kiam2-m7-si7 ti7 A-bun5 lang5 e5 Lah8-pa mah?)  12). Hit-si5 lan2 tit-tioh8 chit e5 toe7; tui3 A-lun3 soaN-kok piN e5 A-lo5-jiN2 khi2, i2-kip8 Ki-liat8 soaN-toe7 e5 chit8-poaN3, kap ki5-tiong e5 siaN5, goa2 long2 hou7 Liu5-pian7 lang5 kap Ka-tek lang5;  13). Ki-liat8 ki5-u5 e5 toe7, kap Pa-san choan5-toe7, Gok8 e5 kok, goa2 hou7 Ma2-na2-se e5 poaN3-chi-phai3; A-jiN2-ko-pek choan5-toe7, Pa-san choan5-toe7, che kio3-choe3 Li7-hoat8-im lang5 e5 toe7.  14). Ma2-na2-se e5 kiaN2 Gai5-jiN2 chiam3 A-jiN2-ko-pek choan5-keng2, tit8-kau3 Ki-sut8 lang5 kap Ma2-ka lang5 e5 kau-kai3; chiu7 chiau3 ka-ki7 e5 mia5 chheng Pa-san toe7 choe3 Hap-ui2-tek8-gai5-jiN2, kau3 kin-a2-jit8.  15). Goa2 koh chiong Ki-liat8 hou7 Ma2-kiat.  16). Tui3 Ki-liat8 kau3 A-lun3 e5 soaN-kok, eng7 soaN-kok choe3 kai3, tit8-kau3 A-bun5 lang5 kau-kai3 e5 Nga2-phok ho5, goa2 chiong che hou7 Liu5-pian7 lang5, kap Ka-tek lang5;  17). koh chiong A-lah8-pa, kap oa2-kun7 Iok-tan3 ho5 e5 toe7, tui3 Ki-ni5-liat8 tit8-kau3 A-lah8-pa e5 hai2, chiu7-si7 Iam5-hai2, i2-kip8 Pi2-su-ka soaN-kha tang-piN e5 toe7, long2 hou7 in.
	18). Hit-si5 goa2 hoan-hu3 lin2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 i2-keng chiong chit e5 toe7 hou7 lin2 choe3-giap8, lin2 tiong-kan oe7 kau-chian3-e5, long2 tioh8 toa3 kun-khi3, ti7 lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 ke3--khi3.  19). Chong2-si7 lin2 e5 bou2, lin2 e5 gin2-na2, lin2 e5 cheng-siN, (goa2 chai lin2 e5 cheng-siN chin choe7,) thang tiam3 ti7 goa2 sou2 hou7 lin2 tak8 e5 siaN5,  20). kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa siuN2-su3 peng5-an hou7 lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7, chhin-chhiuN7 i2-keng siuN2-su3 lin2 chit8-iuN7, koh in ia7 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, eng7 Iok-tan3 hit peng5 e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 in, jian5-au7 lin2 tak8-lang5 thang to3--lai5 goa2 siuN2-su3 lin2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7.  21). Hit-si5 goa2 hoan-hu3 Iok-su-a kong2, Li2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 tui3 chi2 nng7 e5 ong5 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 su7, Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 beh tui3 lin2 sou2 beh ke3-khi3 e5 tak8-kok an2-ni kiaN5.  22). Lin2 boh8-tit kiaN in; in-ui7 thoe3 lin2 kau-chian3 e5, si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.
	23). Hit-si5 goa2 khun2-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2,  24). Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 i2-keng khi2-thau5 hian2-chhut Li2 e5 toa7 ui-giam5, kap Li2 e5 toa7 khui3-lat8 ti7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, in-ui7 ti7 thiN--nih, ti7 toe7--nih, iau2-u7 sim2-mih8 siong7-te3 oe7 kiaN5 chhin-chhiuN7 Li2 sou2 kiaN5--e5, koh chhin-chhiuN7 Li2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5 ah?  25). Kiu5 Li2 iong5-un2 goa2 ke3-khi3, khoaN3 Iok-tan3 ho5 hit-peng5 sui2 e5 toe7, hit-e5 sui2 e5 soaN-toe7, kap Li7-pa-lun3.  26). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, in-ui7 lin2 e5 ian5-kou3, siu7-khi3 goa2, m7 thiaN goa2; Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, An2-ni li2 kau3-giah8 lah, li2 boh8-tit koh tui3 Goa2 the5-khi2 chit e5 su7.  27). Li2 tioh8 chiuN7 Pi2-su-ka e5 soaN-teng2, kiah8-bak8 ng3-sai, ng3-pak, ng3-lam5, ng3-tang, chhin-bak8 khoaN3; in-ui7 li2 koat-toan3 boe7-oe7 ke3 chit e5 Iok-tan3 ho5.  28). Chong2-si7 li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 Iok-su-a, hou7 i chong3-taN2 kian-kou3; in-ui7 i beh ti7 chit e5 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5 ke3-khi3, hou7 in seng5-chiap li2 sou2 beh khoaN3-kiN3 e5 toe7.  29). Tui3 an2-ni lan2 tiam3 ti7 Pek-pi2-jiN2 tui3-bin7 e5 soaN-kok-tiong.

[4]	I2-sek-liat8 ah, taN goa2 sou2 ka3-si7 lin2 e5 lut8-le7 hoat-tou7, lin2 tioh8 thiaN lai5 chun-than3, thang hou7 lin2 oah8-teh, jip8-khi3 lai5 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 e5 toe7.  2). Goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5 oe7, lin2 m7-thang ke-thiN, ia7 m7-thang kiam2-chio2 i; thang hou7 lin2 chip-siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 beng7-leng7, chiu7-si7 goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa in-ui7 Pa-lek8-pi2-jiN2 e5 su7 sou2 kiaN5 e5, lin2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3; in-ui7 kiN3-na7 than3 Pa-lek8-pi2-jiN2 e5 lang5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 long2 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tu5-biat8 in.  4). Tok8-tok8 lin2 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 kiat-lian5 e5, kin-a2-jit8 long2 oah8--teh.  5). KhoaN3 ah, goa2 ia7 bat eng7 lut8-le7 kap hoat-tou7 ka3-si7 lin2, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 goa2 e5, hou7 lin2 chun-than3 ti7 lin2 sou2 beh jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7.  6). Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5--i; che chiu7-si7 lin2 e5 ti3-hui7 chhang-mia5 ti7 liat8-kok e5 bin7-cheng5; in chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 che it-chhe3 e5 lut8-le7, beh kong2, Chit e5 toa7-kok chin-chiaN3 si7 u7 ti3-hui7 chhang-mia5 e5 peh-siN3.  7). Toh-loh8 chit8 e5 toa7-kok u7 siong7-te3 kap i chhin-kun7, chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3, ti7 lan2 kiN3-na7 kiu5-kio3 I e5 si5, kap lan2 chhin-kun7 ah?  8). Koh u7 sim2-mih8 toa7-kok u7 lut8-le7 kap hoat-tou7 chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 thoan5 it-chhe3 e5 lut8-hoat hiah-nih kong-gi7 ah?
	9). Sou2-i2 tioh8 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, ia7 tioh8 kin2-sin7 siu2 li2 e5 sim, bian2-tit li2 boe7-ki3-tit chhin-bak8 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 su7; koh bian2-tit chiah e5 su7 ti7 li2 oah8--teh e5 si5 li7-khui li2 e5 sim; ia7 tioh8 eng7 chit-e5 ka3-si7 lin2 hiah e5 kiaN2, hiah e5 sun.  10). Li2 ti7 Ho5-liat8 soaN khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 ka7 Goa2 chio-chip8 peh-siN3, Goa2 beh hou7 in thiaN-kiN3 Goa2 e5 oe7, hou7 in oah8 ti7 se3-kan e5 jit8, thang hak8-sip8 keng3-ui3 Goa2; koh thang ka3-si7 in e5 kiaN2-ji5.  11). Hit-si5 lin2 kun7-oa2, khia7 ti7 soaN-kha, soaN--nih u7 he2-iam7 chheng3-kau3 thiN-teng2, ia7 u7 bat8-hun5 ou-ou am3-am3.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 he2-iam7-tiong ka7 lin2 kong2-oe7; lin2 thiaN-kiN3 kong2-oe7 e5 siaN, bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8 siong7; chi2-u7 siaN na7-tiaN7.  13). I chiong sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 tioh8 siu2 e5 iok chi2-si7 lin2, chiu7-si7 chap8-tiau5-kai3; ia7 sia2 i ti7 nng7 te3 chioh8-pi.  14). Hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa koh beng7-leng7 goa2, chiong lut8-le7 hoat-tou7 ka3-si7 lin2, hou7 lin2 ti7 sou2 beh ke3-khi3 lai5 tit-tioh8 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7 chun-than3 kiaN5 i.  15). Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 tek8-piat8 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Ho5-liat8 soaN tui3 he2-tiong ka7 lin2 kong2-oe7 hit-jit8, lin2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8 heng5-siong7;  16). kiaN-liau2 lin2 pai7-hoai7 ka-ki7, ui7 ka-ki7 tiau-khek ngou2-siong7, hong2 sim2-mih8 heng5-chong7, bo5-lun7 si7 lam5 a2-si7 lu2 e5 heng5-siong7;  17). a2-si7 toe7-chiuN7 chau2-siu3 e5 siong7;  18). a2-si7 khong-tiong pe-chiau2 e5 siong7; a2-si7 toe7-chiuN7 teh so5 e5 mih8 e5 siong7; a2-si7 toe7-e7 chui2-tiong hi5-lui7 e5 siong7.  19). Koh kiaN-liau2 li2 kiah8-bak8 ng3-thiN khoaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 hun-phai3 hou7 thiN-e7 ban7-kok e5 jit8, geh8, chhiN, chiu7-si7 thiN-teng2 e5 ban7-siong7, li2 chiu7 siu7 in2-iu2, keng3-pai3 hok8-sai7 in.  20). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa toa3 lin2 chhut Ai-kip8, thoat-li7 chu3-thih e5 lou5, beh choe3 I ka-ki7 san2-giap8 e5 peh-siN3, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 e5 khoan2.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh in-ui7 lin2 e5 ian5-kou3 siu7-khi3 goa2, chiu3-choa7 m7 hou7 goa2 ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5, ia7 m7 hou7 goa2 jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8 e5 sui2 toe7;  22). goa2 tioh8 si2 ti7 chit e5 toe7; goa2 boe7-oe7 ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5; chong2-si7 lin2 beh ke3-khi3 lai5 tit-tioh8 hit e5 ho2 e5 toe7.  23). Lin2 tioh8 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, kiaN-liau2 lin2 boe7-ki3-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 kap lin2 sou2 lip8 e5 iok, ui7 ka-ki7 tiau-khek ngou2-siong7 hong2-hut sim2-mih8 mih8, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 kim3 li2 e5.  24). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiu7-si7 liat8-liat8 e5 he2, koat-toan3 m7 iong5-un2 u7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3.
	25). Au7-lai5 lin2 ku2-ku2 khia7-khi2 ti7 hit e5 toe7 siN-kiaN2 thoan5-sun, chiu7 tiau-khek ngou2-siong7, hong2 sim2-mih8 mih8 e5 siong7, phah-phaiN2 li2 e5 sim-sut8, kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 bak8-chiu-tiong khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2 e5 su7, jia2 I siu7-khi3;  26). goa2 chiu7 kin-a-jit8 kio3 thiN kio3 toe7 lai5 kan-cheng3, lin2 beh ti7 ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5 tit-tioh8 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7 kin2-kin2 biat8 kau3 chin7; lin2 e5 jit8-chi2 boe7-oe7 ti7 hit sou2-chai7 tit-tioh8 ku2-tng5, beh it-chin7 tu5-biat8.  27). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 lin2 si3-soaN3 ti7 liat8-pang; ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chhoa7 lin2 kau3 hiah e5 kok, lin2 chhun e5 lang5-giah8 chio2-chio2.  28). Ti7-hia lin2 beh hok8-sai7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 sou2 cho7 e5 siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 chha5--e5, chioh8--e5, boe7-oe7 khoaN3-kiN3, boe7-oe7 thiaN, boe7-oe7 chiah8, boe7-oe7 phiN7 e5.  29). Chong2-si7 lin2 ti7-hia na7 beh chhe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, na7 eng7 chin7-sim chin7-seng3 chhe7 I, chiu7 beh tu2-tioh8.  30). Jit8-au7 lin2 tu2-tioh8 khou2-lan7, sou2 kong2 chiah e5 su7 lim5-kau3 li2, li2 beh kui-ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 e5 Siong7-te3, lai5 thiaN I e5 siaN;  31). in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 si7 lin5-bin2 e5 Siong7-te3, I bo5 beh pang3-sak li2, bo5 beh chau5-biat8 li2, ia7 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit I kap li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5 iok.
	32). Chhi3-mng7 ke3-sin e5 si5, chiu7-si7 li2 i2-cheng5 e5 si5, tui3 Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 lang5 ti7 se3-kan hit-jit8 i2-lai5, tui3 thiN e5 chit-piN kau3 thiN e5 hit-piN, u7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit-ho7 e5 toa7-su7 mah? Bat thiaN-kiN3 u7 an2-ni mah?  33). Bat u7 sim2-mih8 peh-siN3 thiaN-kiN3 Siong7-te3 tui3 he2-tiong kong2-oe7 e5 siaN, chhin-chhiuN7 li2 thiaN-kiN3, ia7 iau2 oe7 oah8-teh mah?  34). A2-si7 bat u7 sim2-mih8 siong7-te3 chhi3 an2-ni choe3, eng7 chhi3-lian7, sin5-jiah, ki5-su7, kau-chian3, toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2-kut, kap toa7 thang kiaN e5 su7, ui7 ka-ki7 tui3 pat8-kok tiong chhu2 chit8-kok, chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 Ai-kip8 ti7 lin2 e5 bak8-chiu cheng5, ui7 lin2 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 su7 ah?  35). Eng7 che hian2-hian7 ti7 li2, hou7 li2 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa I si7 Siong7-te3, I i2-goa7 bo5 u7 pat8-e5.  36). I tui3 thiN hou7 li2 thiaN-kiN3 I e5 siaN, ui7-tioh8 beh ka3-si7 li2, koh ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 hou7 li2 khoaN3-kiN3 I e5 toa7-he2, koh li2 thiaN-kiN3 I e5 oe7 tui3 he2-tiong chhut.  37). In-ui7 I thiaN3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2, sou2-i2 keng2-soan2 in e5 hou7-e3, eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 chhin-sin toa3 li2 chhut Ai-kip8;  38). beh tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut pi2 li2 khah-toa7 khah-beng2 e5 kok-bin5, beh chhoa7 li2 jip8-khi3, eng7 in e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 lin2 choe3-giap8, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 chit8-iuN7.  39). Sou2-i2 kin-a2-jit8 li2 tioh8 chai, sim ia7 tioh8 siuN7, thiN-teng2 toe7-e7 chi2-u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, I si7 Siong7-te3, i2-goa7 bo5 pat8-e5.  40). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 siu2 I e5 lut8-le7 kai3-beng7, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2, hou7 li2 kap li2 e5 hou7-e3 thang tit-tioh8 hok-khi3, koh ke-thiN li2 e5 jit8-chi2 ku2-tng5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7 kau3 eng2-oan2.
	41). Hit-si5 Mou5-se ti7 Iok-tan3 goa7, ng3 jit8-chhut e5 sou2-chai7 hun-piat saN e5 siaN5;  42). hou7 thai5-si2 lang5 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 peng5-sou3 bo5 kiat-oan3, chho3-gou7 thai5-si2 i e5 chhu3-piN e5, thang to5-chau2 ti7-hia; i2-keng chau2-jip8 chiah e5 siaN5 e5 chit8-e5, chiu7 tit-tioh8 oah8;  43). chiu7-si7 khong3-ia2 piN5-iuN5 e5 Pi2-sek, ui7-tioh8 Liu5-pian7 lang5 siat-e5; Ki-liat8 e5 Lah8-boat8, ui7-tioh8 Ka-tek lang5 siat-e5; Pa-san e5 Ko-lan5, ui7-tioh8 Ma2-na2-se lang5 siat-e5.
	44). Chit-e5 si7 Mou5-se ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 pai5-liat8 e5 lut8-hoat;  45). chiah-e5 si7 Mou5-se ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut Ai-kip8 liau2-au7, sou2 thoan5 hou7 in e5 cheng3-ku3, lut8-le7, hoat-tou7.  46). Ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5-goa7, Pek-pi2-jiN2 tui3-bin7 e5 soaN-kok-tiong, ti7 Hi-sit8-pun2 khia7-khi2 A-mou5-li7 ong5 Se-hong5 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut Ai-kip8 liau2-au7 sou2 phah--e5.  47). In tit-tioh8 i e5 toe7, kap Pa-san ong5 Gok8 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 nng7 e5 A-mou5-li7 ong5, ti7 Iok-tan3 goa7, ng3 jit8-chhut e5 sou2-chai7;  48). tui3 A-lun3 soaN-kok piN e5 A-lo5-jiN2, tit8-kau3 Se-hun5 soaN, chiu7-si7 Hek-bun5 soaN;  49). i2-kip8 Iok-tan3 goa7, tang--si3 A-lah8-pa e5 choan5-toe7, tit8-kau3 A-lah8-pa e5 hai2, oa2-kun7 Pi2-su-ka e5 soaN-kha.

[5]	Mou5-se kio3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5, tui3 in kong2, I2-sek-liat8 ah, lin2 tioh8 thiaN goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 thoan5 hou7 lin2 thiaN e5 lut8-le7 hoat-tou7, hou7 lin2 thang hak8-sip8 i, chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 in.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 Ho5-liat8 kap lan2 lip8-iok.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 kap lan2 e5 liat8-chou2 lip8 chit e5 iok, si7 kap lan2 chiah-e5, chiu7-si7 kap lan2 kin-a2-jit8 it-chhe3 oah8 ti7-chia e5 lang5 lip8-e5.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 soaN-teng2, tui3 he2-tiong bin7-tui3-bin7, kap lin2 kong2-oe7.  5). (Hit-si5 goa2 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap lin2 e5 tiong-kan, beh chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 thoan5 hou7 lin2, in-ui7 lin2 ui7-tioh8 hit e5 he2 lai5 kiaN, bo5 chiuN7 soaN.)  6). Chu2 kong2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, bat chhoa7 li2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7, tui3 choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke chhut-lai5 e5.
	7). Goa2 i2-goa7 li2 m7-thang u7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3.
	8). M7-thang ui7 ka-ki7 tiau-khek ngou2-siong7, put-lun7 thiN-teng2, toe7-e7, kap toe7-e7 chui2-lai7 sou2-u7 e5 mih8, long2 m7-thang chng in e5 siong7;  9). m7-thang kui7-pai3 in, ia7 m7-thang hok8-sai7 in; in-ui7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, toan3-toan3 m7 iong5-un2 eng7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 phit-phoe3 Goa2; oan3-hun7 Goa2 e5, Goa2 kui-kiu7 i e5 choe7, tui3 pe7 kau3 kiaN2, kau3 saN-si3 tai7;  10). thiaN3 Goa2, siu2 Goa2 kai3-beng7 e5, Goa2 si-un hou7 i, tit8-kau3 chheng-tai7.
	11). M7-thang lam7-sam2 chheng Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5; in-ui7 lam7-sam2 chheng I e5 mia5 e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak bo5 liah8 i choe3 bo5-choe7.
	12). Tioh8 siu2 an-hioh-jit8, liah8 i choe3-seng3, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5;  13). lak8-jit8-lai7 tioh8 tioh8-boa5 choe3 li2 it-chhe3 e5 kang;  14). tok8-tok8 te7-chhit jit8, chiu7-si7 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 lai5 siu2 e5 an-hioh, chit-jit8, li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, gu5, lu5, cheng-siN, i2-kip8 tiam3 ti7 li2 tiong-kan e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, it-chhe3 e5 kang long2 m7-thang choe3; hou7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, thang chhin-chhiuN7 li2 an-hioh.  15). Li2 ia7 tioh8 ki3-tit li2 cheng5 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 choe3 lou5-pok8, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, chhun--chhut-lai5 e5 chhiu2-kut, chhoa7 li2 tui3 hia chhut-lai5; in-ui7 an2-ni, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beng7-leng7 li2 siu2 an-hioh-jit8.
	16). Tioh8 hau3-keng3 li2 e5 lau7-pe7, li2 e5 lau7-bu2, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, hou7 li2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7-hng, jit8-chi2 ku2-tng5, lai5 hiong2-siu7 hok-khi3.
	17). M7-thang thai5-si2 lang5.
	18). Ia7 m7-thang kiaN5 kan-im5.
	19). Ia7 m7-thang thau-theh8.
	20). Ia7 m7-thang choe3 ke2 e5 kan-cheng3, ham7-hai7 li2 e5 chhu3-piN.
	21). Ia7 m7-thang tham li2 e5 chhu3-piN e5 bou2, ia7 m7-thang tham li2 e5 chhu3-piN e5 chhu3, kap i e5 chhan5-hng5, i e5 lou5-pok8, i e5 lu2-pi7, i e5 gu5, i e5 lu5, kap li2 e5 chhu3-piN it-chhe3 sou2 u7 e5.
	22). Chiah e5 oe7 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 soaN-teng2, tui3 he2-tiong hun5-tiong ou-am3-tiong, toa7-siaN hoan-hu3 lin2 choan5-hoe7 e5; ia7 bo5 koh ke-thiN.  I ia7 sia2 in ti7 nng7 te3 chioh8-pi, kau-tai3 goa2.  23). Hit-tiap8 he2-iam7 sio ti7 soaN--nih, lin2 thiaN-kiN3 hit e5 tui3 ou-am3-tiong chhut-lai5 e5 siaN, lin2 e5 chi-phai3 long2-chong2 e5 siu2-leng2, kap lin2 e5 tiuN2-lo2 lai5 chiu7-kun7 goa2.  24). Lin2 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 hian2-beng5 I e5 eng5-kng, kap I e5 chi3-toa7, hou7 goan2 khoaN3; goan2 koh thiaN-kiN3 I e5 siaN-im tui3 he2-tiong chhut; kin-a2-jit8 goan2 ia7 chai Siong7-te3 kap lang5 kong2-oe7, lang5 iau2 oe7 oah8.  25). TaN goan2 mih-sai2 tioh8 si2 ah? In-ui7 chit e5 toa7-he2 beh sio-biat8 goan2; goan2 na7 koh thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 Siong7-te3 e5 siaN, chiu7 oe7 si2.  26). In-ui7 kiN3-u7 jiok8-the2 e5, chi7-chui7 chhin-chhiuN7 goan2 thiaN-kiN3 eng2-oah8 Siong7-te3 tui3 he2-tiong kong2-oe7 e5 siaN, iau2 oe7 oah8--teh ah?  27). Li2 tioh8 chin3-cheng5 khi3, thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7; chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 tui3 li2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, li2 tioh8 tui3 goan2 kong2; goan2 beh thiaN ia7 beh kiaN5 i.  28). Lin2 tui3 goa2 kong2-oe7, Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3 lin2 kong2-oe7 e5 siaN, Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Goa2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 peh-siN3 kong2-oe7 e5 siaN, chiu7-si7 in sou2 tui3 li2 kong2 e5; in sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 long2 ho2.  29). Goan7 in chun5 chit-ho7 sim, lai5 keng3-ui3 Goa2, siong5-siong5 siu2 Goa2 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, hou7 in kap in e5 kiaN2-sun eng2-oan2 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  30). Li2 khi3 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 choe3 lin2 to3-khi3 lin2 e5 pou3-piN5.  31). Lun7-kau3 li2, li2 tioh8 khia7 ti7 Goa2 chia, Goa2 beh chiong li2 sou2 tioh8 ka3-si7 in it-chhe3 kai3-beng7, lut8-le7, hoat-tou7, ka7 li2 kong2, hou7 in ti7 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 in choe3-giap8 e5 toe7 kiaN5 i.  32). Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5, tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 i; m7-thang phian ti7 cho2, phian ti7 iu7.  33). Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5 lou7, lin2 long2 tioh8 kiaN5 i, hou7 lin2 oah8-teh, tit-tioh8 hok-khi3; ia7 hou7 lin2 e5 jit8-chi2, ti7 lin2 sou2 beh seng5-chiap e5 toe7, tit-tioh8 ku2-tng5.

[6]	Che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 ka3-si7 lin2 e5 kai3-beng7, lut8-le7, hoat-tou7, hou7 lin2 ti7 lin2 sou2 beh ke3-khi3 tit-tioh8 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7 lai5 kiaN5 i;  2). thang hou7 li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2-kiaN2 sun-sun, it-seng keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, chip-siu2 I it-chhe3 e5 lut8-le7, kai3-beng7, chiu7-si7 goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, hou7 li2 e5 jit8-chi2 tit-tioh8 ku2-tng5.  3). I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 tioh8 thiaN, tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 i; hou7 li2 thang ti7 hit-e5 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7, tit-tioh8 hiong2-hok, lang5-giah8 ke-thiN kek8-ki5 choe7; chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 liat8-chou2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 eng3-un2 li2 e5.
	4). I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 tioh8 thiaN; Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3, si7 tok8-it e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  5). li2 tioh8 chin7-sim, chin7-seng3, chin7-lat8, thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3.  6). Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 chiah e5 oe7, tioh8 ki3 ti7 li2 e5 sim;  7). ia7 tioh8 eng7 che khun5-khun5 ka3-si7 li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, bo5-lun7 li2 che7 ti7 chhu3-lai7 kiaN5 ti7 lou7--nih, khun3 a2-si7 khi2-lai5, long2 tioh8 kang2-lun7;  8). ia7 tioh8 pak8 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2 choe3 ki3-ho7, ti3 ti7 li2 nng7 lui2 bak8-chiu e5 tiong-ng choe3 ki3-liam7;  9). koh tioh8 sia2 ti7 li2 e5 chhu3 e5 mng5-khia7, i2-kip8 li2 e5 mng5.
	10). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chhoa7 li2 jip8 I tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2, A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok, chiu3-choa7 beh hou7 li2 e5 toe7; ti7-hia u7 siaN5 toa7 koh sui2, m7-si7 li2 sou2 khi2-cho7 e5;  11). ia7 u7 chhu3 chek-chu7 moa2-moa2 e5 ho2-mih8, m7-si7 li2 sou2 chek-chu7 e5; ia7 u7 khui-pian7 e5 chui2-chiN2, m7-si7 li2 sou2 khui e5;  12). ia7 u7 phu5-to5-hng5, kaN-na2-chhiu7, m7-si7 li2 sou2 chai-cheng3 e5; li2 chiah8 kau3 pa2, hit-si5 li2 tioh8 kin2-sin7, bian2-tit li2 boe7-ki3-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 chhoa7 li2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7, choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke, chhut-lai5 e5.  13). Li2 tioh8 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, hok8-sai7 I, chi2 I e5 mia5 chiu3-choa7;  14). m7-thang than3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 lin2 si3-ui5 peh-siN3 hiah e5 siong7-te3.  15). In-ui7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, toan3-toan3 bo5 iong5-un2 eng7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 phit-phoe3 I; si7 kiaN-liau2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 toa7 siu7-khi3 li2, tui3 toe7-chiuN7 tu5-biat8 li2.
	16). Lin2 m7-thang chhi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 ti7 Ma2-sat chhi3 I chit8-iuN7.  17). Tioh8 ti3-i3 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 kai3-beng7, kap I sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5 cheng3-ku3, lut8-le7.  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 khoaN3-choe3 cheng3-tit8, choe3 ho2 e5, li2 tioh8 kiaN5 i, hou7 li2 thang hiong2-hok, koh thang jip8-khi3 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5 ho2-toe7;  19). beh tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut li2 long2-chong2 e5 tui3-tek8 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2 e5.
	20). Chiong-lai5 li2 e5 kiaN2 mng7 li2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 chiah e5 cheng3-ku3, lut8-le7, hoat-tou7, si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3 ah?  21). Li2 tioh8 ka7 li2 e5 kiaN2 kong2, Cheng5 goan2 ti7 Ai-kip8 choe3 Hoat-lo2 e5 lou5-chai5, Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, chhoa7 goan2 chhut Ai-kip8.  22). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 goan2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, eng7 toa7 koh li7-hai7 e5 sin5-jiah ki5-su7, kiaN5 ti7 Ai-kip8 kap Hoat-lo2, i2-kip8 i e5 choan5-ke;  23). tui3 hia chhoa7 goan2 chhut-lai5, beh chhoa7 goan2 jip8-khi3, chiong I tui3 lan2 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 lan2.  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa beng7-leng7 lan2 kiaN5 chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 lut8-le7, lai5 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3, hou7 lan2 siong5-siong5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3, tit-tioh8 I po2-choan5 lan2 e5 siN3-mia7, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 e5 khoan2.  25). Lan2 na7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7-e5, ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 chiau3 I it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7 lai5 kiaN5, che chiu7-si7 lan2 e5 gi7.

[7]	Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chhoa7 li2 jip8 li2 sou2 beh khi3 tit-tioh8 e5 toe7, tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut choe7-choe7 pang-kok, chiu7-si7 Hek lang5, Kek-ka-sat lang5, A-mou5-li7 lang5, Ka-lam5 lang5, Pi2-li7-se2 lang5, Hi-bi7 lang5, Ia5-pou3-su lang5, kiong7 chhit-kok, long2 pi2 li2 khah-toa7 khah-beng2;  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiong in kau-hu3 li2, hou7 li2 phah-iaN5 i, hit-si5 li2 tioh8 it-chin7 biat8 in, m7-thang kap in lip8-iok, ia7 m7-thang lin5-bin2 in;  3). m7-thang kap in kiat-chhin, li2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 m7-thang ke3 hou7 i e5 kiaN2, ia7 m7-thang ka7 li2 e5 kiaN2 chhoa7 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  4). In-ui7 i beh hou7 li2 e5 kiaN2 oat8-tng2 bo5 te3 Goa2, khi3 hok8-sai7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3; ti3-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa toa7 siu7-khi3 lin2, kin2-kin2 biat8 lin2.  5). Chong2-si7 lin2 tioh8 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 in; thiah-hui2 in e5 che3-toaN5, phah-chhui3 in tiau-khek e5 thiau7, chho3 in e5 A-sai3-lim5, eng7 he2 sio in sou2 chng e5 ngou2-siong7.  6). In-ui7 lin2 choe3 seng3-kiat e5 peh-siN3, kui ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3.  Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 tui3 toe7-chiuN7 ban7 peh-siN3-tiong keng2 li2, tek8-piat8 choe3 I ka-ki7 e5 peh-siN3.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN3 lin2, keng2 lin2, m7-si7 in-ui7 lin2 e5 lang5-giah8 pi2 pat8-kok khah-choe7; in-ui7 lin2 e5 lang5-giah8 si7 ban7-kok-tiong te7-it chio2-e5;  8). si7 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN3 lin2, koh in-ui7 beh kiaN5 I tui3 lin2 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa chiah eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2 chhoa7 lin2 chhut-lai5, tui3 choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke kiu3-siok8 lin2, thoat-li7 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2.  9). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, I si7 Siong7-te3, si7 sin3-sit8 e5 Siong7-te3, ui7-tioh8 thiaN3 I siu2 I kai3-beng7 e5 lang5, kiaN5 I e5 iok kap chu5-ai3, tit8-kau3 chheng-tai7.  10). KiN3-na7 oan3-hun7 I e5 lang5, I beh tng-bin7 po3-eng3 lai5 biat8 in; oan3-hun7 I e5 lang5, I beh tng-bin7 po3-eng3 i, bo5 beh ian5-chhian5.  11). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 chip-siu2 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5 kai3-beng7, lut8-le7, hoat-tou7, lai5 kiaN5 i.
	12). Au7-lai5 lin2 na7 thiaN chiah e5 hoat-tou7, chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 i, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 in-ui7 an2-ni beh ka7 li2 kiaN5 I tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5 iok kap chu5-ai3.  13). I beh thiaN3 li2, su3-hok li2, hou7 li2 heng-ong7; ia7 beh ti7 I tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7, su3-hok li2 e5 thai sou2-siN-e5, li2 e5 toe7 sou2-chhut-e5, kap li2 e5 ngou2-kok, li2 e5 chiu2, li2 e5 iu5, i2-kip8 li2 e5 gu5-a2, kap li2 e5 iuN5-a2-kiaN2.  14). Li2 beh tit-tioh8 su3-hok iaN5-ke3 ban7 peh-siN3; lin2 tiong-kan e5 lam5-lu2 bo5 chit8-e5 boe7 seng-iong2; lin2 tiong-kan e5 cheng-siN bo5 chit8-chiah boe7 siN-thoaN3.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 it-chhe3 e5 piN7-cheng3 li7-khui li2; li2 sou2 chai Ai-kip8 tak8-iuN7 e5 phaiN2 cheng3-thau5, I bo5 hou7 li2 tu2-tioh8 chit8-hang7; si7 beh hou7 it-chhe3 oan3-hun7 li2 e5 lang5 tu2-tioh8.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh kau-hu3 li2 e5 peh-siN3, li2 tioh8 long2 biat8 in; li2 e5 bak8-chiu m7-thang kho2-lin5 in, li2 ia7 m7-thang hok8-sai7 in e5 siong7-te3; in-ui7 che beh choe3 hai7 li2 e5 lo5-bang7.
	17). Li2 na7 sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2, Chiah e5 kok pi2 goa2 khah-toa7, goa2 thai2-tho2 oe7 koaN2-tiok8 in ah?  18). Li2 m7-bian2 kiaN in; tek-khak tioh8 ki3-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ng3 Hoat-lo2 kap Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7 sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7;  19). chiu7-si7 li2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 toa7 chhi3-lian7, sin5-jiah, ki5-su7, kap toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, kap chhun-chhut-lai5 e5 chhiu2-kut, long2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 eng7 lai5 chhoa7 li2 chhut--e5; Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ia7 beh an2-ni kiaN5 ti7 li2 sou2 kiaN it-chhe3 e5 peh-siN3.  20). Koh Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh chhe toa7 chiah phang, pe--kau3 in tiong-kan, tit8-kau3 in sou2 chhun lai5 siam2-bih-e5, biat8 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  21). Li2 m7-bian2 kiaN in; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 si7 toa7 koh thang kiaN e5 Siong7-te3, ti7 lin2 tiong-kan.  22). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chiam7-chiam7 tu5-biat8 chiah e5 kok; li2 m7-thang kin2-kin2 biat8 i kau3-chin7, kiaN-liau2 ia2-siu3 ke-thiN choe7-choe7 lai5 hai7 li2.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh chiong in kau-hu3 li2, hou7 in toa7-kiaN jiau2-loan7, tit8-kau3 in biat8-bo5;  24). koh beh eng7 in hiah e5 ong5 kau ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, li2 beh tu5-biat8 in e5 mia5 ti7 thiN-e7; tek-khak bo5 chit8-lang5 oe7 khia7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, tit8-kau3 li2 biat8-bo5 in.  25). In sou2 tiau-khek in e5 siong7-te3 e5 siong7, lin2 tioh8 eng7 he2 sio i; i e5 sin-chiuN7 e5 kim-gun5 li2 m7-thang tham, ia7 m7-thang theh8 i choe3 ka-ki7-e5; kiaN-liau2 li2 ui7 chit-e5 ham7-loh8 lo5-bang7; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 iam3-ouN3-e5 .  26). KiN3-na7 thang iam3-ouN3 e5 mih8, li2 m7-thang toa3-jip8 li2 e5 chhu3, kiaN-liau2 li2 ia7 chiaN5-choe3 thang chiu3-chou2--e5, kap hiah e5 mih8 chit8-iuN7; li2 tioh8 kek8-ki5 thong3-hun7, kek8-ki5 iam3-ouN3; in-ui7 si7 thang chiu3-chou2--e5.

[8]	Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, lin2 tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 i, hou7 lin2 thang oah8, lang5-giah8 ke-thiN choe7-choe7, thang jip8-khi3 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 e5 toe7.  2). Li2 ia7 tioh8 ki3-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chi2 si3-chap8 ni5 chhoa7 li2 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5 lou7, si7 beh hou7 li2 khiam-pi lai5 chhi3-giam7 li2, beh chai li2 e5 sim-lai7 chaiN2-iuN7, kheng2 siu2 I e5 kai3-beng7 a2-bo5.  3). I hou7 li2 khiam-pi, hou7 li2 iau-go7, eng7 li2 sou2 m7-bat, li2 e5 liat8-chou2 ia7 m7-bat, e5 ma2-na2 iuN2-chhi7 li2; hou7 li2 chai lang5 m7-si7 kan-ta oa2-kho3 piaN2 lai5 oah8, lang5 si7 oa2-kho3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhui3 sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7 lai5 oah8.  4). Chi2 si3-chap8 ni5 li2 e5 saN-khou3 bo5 phoa3, li2 e5 kha ia7 bo5 phong3-pha7.  5). Li2 e5 sim tioh8 chai, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kau3-tok li2, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 kau3-tok i e5 kiaN2 chit8-iuN7;  6). koh li2 tioh8 chip-siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 kai3-beng7, lai5 kiaN5 I e5 to7-lou7, lai5 keng3-ui3 I.  7). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chhoa7 li2 jip8 hit e5 sui2 e5 toe7; hit e5 toe7 u7 khoe, u7 chui2-choaN5, u7 chhim-ian, tui3 soaN-kok kap soaN lau5--chhut-lai5;  8). si7 chhut sio2-beh8, toa7-beh8, phu5-to5-chhiu7, bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7, siah8-liu5-chhiu7 e5 toe7, ia7 chhut kaN-na2-chhiu7 kap bit8 e5 toe7.  9). Li2 ti7 hit sou2-chai7 chiah8 mih8 chhiong-chiok, ti7-hia li2 ia7 bo5 khiam3 chit8-hang7; hit sou2-chai7 e5 chioh8-thau5 si7 thih, ti7 i e5 soaN thang kut8 tang5;  10). li2 beh chiah8 kau3 pa2, chiu7 ui7-tioh8 I sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 sui2 toe7, lai5 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3.  11). Li2 tioh8 kin2-sin7, bian2-tit li2 boe7-ki3-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, bo5 siu2 I e5 kai3-beng7, hoat-tou7, lut8-le7, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5;  12). kiaN-liau2 li2 i2-keng chiah8-pa2, i2-keng khi2 sui2 e5 chhu3 lai5 khia7-khi2;  13). li2 e5 gu5 iuN5 ke-thiN, li2 e5 kim-gun5 ke-thiN, li2 sou2-u7-e5 long2 ke-thiN,  14). hit-si5 li2 e5 sim chu7-ko, boe7-ki3-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 chhoa7 li2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7, choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke, chhut-lai5 e5.  15). I chhoa7 li2 keng-ke3 hit e5 toa7 koh thang kiaN e5 khong3-ia2, hia u7 he2-choa5, giat-a2-thang5, ta-so3 bo5 chui2 e5 toe7; I bat ui5-tioh8 li2 hou7 chui2 tui3 teng7 e5 chioh8-poaN5 lau5--chhut-lai5.  16). Koh ti7 khong3-ia2, chiong li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 m7-bat e5 ma2-na2 iuN2-chhi7 li2, si7 beh hou7 li2 khiam-pi, chhi3-giam7 li2, hou7 li2 kau3-be2 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3;  17). kiaN-liau2 li2 sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2, Tit-tioh8 chit e5 toa7 e5 ki-giap8 si7 tui3 goa2 e5 khui3-lat8, goa2 e5 chhiu2 e5 leng5-lek8.  18). Chong2-si7 li2 tioh8 ki3-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3; in-ui7 li2 tit-tioh8 toa7 ki-giap8 e5 khui3-lat8, si7 I hou7 li2, beh chiaN5 I sou2 tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 e5 iok, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 e5 khoan2.  19). Chiong-lai5 li2 na7 boe7-ki3-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 than3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 hok8-sai7 i, keng3-pai3 i, goa2 kin-a2-jit8 giam5-giam5 keng2-kai3 lin2, lin2 tek-khak biat8-bo5.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 biat8-bo5 hiah e5 kok, lin2 ia7 beh an2-ni biat8-bo5; in-ui7 lin2 m7 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7.

[9]	I2-sek-liat8 ah, tioh8 thiaN; li2 kin-a2-jit8 beh ke3 Iok-tan3, jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap hiah e5 pi2 li2 khah-toa7, khah-beng2 e5 kok, tit-tioh8 khoah-toa7 koh kian-kou3 kau3 tu2-thiN e5 siaN5;  2). hit e5 peh-siN3, toa7 koh lo3, si7 A-lap8 e5 chok8, lin2 sou2 chai e5, ia7 bat thiaN-kiN3 u7 lang5 chi2 in kong2, Chi7-chui7 ti7 A-lap8 chok8 e5 bin7-cheng5 khia7-oe7-tiau5 ah?  3). Kin-a2-jit8 li2 tioh8 chai, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 choe3 li2 e5 thau5-cheng5 ke3-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 liat8-liat8 e5 he2; I beh biat8-bo5 in, hou7 in toa7-toa7 thai5-su ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5; lin2 tioh8 koaN2 in chhut, hou7 in kin2-kin2 biat8-bo5, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 tui3 lin2 kong2 e5.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut in liau2-au7, li2 sim-lai7 m7-thang siuN7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa chhoa7 goa2 jip8-lai5 seng5-chiap chit e5 toe7 si7 in-ui7 goa2 e5 gi7; ki5-sit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 ui7-tioh8 hiah e5 kok e5 phaiN2, chiah tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2 in chhut.  5). Li2 jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap in e5 toe7, peng7 m7-si7 in-ui7 li2 e5 gi7, ia7 m7-si7 in-ui7 li2 e5 sim cheng3-tit8; chiu7-si7 in-ui7 chiah e5 kok e5 phaiN2, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiah tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2 in chhut-khi3; koh in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh kian-kou3 I tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok, sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5 oe7.  6). Li2 tioh8 chai, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 eng7 sui2 e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 lin2 choe3-giap8, m7-si7 in-ui7 li2 e5 gi7, in-ui7 li2 si7 am7-kun2 ngi7 e5 peh-siN3.  7). Li2 tioh8 ki3-tit, m7-thang boe7-ki3-tit, li2 ti7 khong3-ia2 jia2-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 siu7-khi3; tui3 lin2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 hit-jit8, kau3 lin2 lai5 kau3 chit e5 sou2-chai7, lin2 siong5-siong5 poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  8). Lin2 ti7 Ho5-liat8 soaN koh jia2 Ia5-ho5-hoa siu7-khi3, ti3-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa siu7-khi3 lin2, beh biat8-bo5 lin2.  9). Tng-si5 goa2 chiuN7-soaN, beh nia2-siu7 chioh8-pi, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap lin2 lip8-iok e5 pi; hit-si5 goa2 tiam3 ti7 soaN--nih si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5, bo5 chiah8-piaN2, bo5 lim-chui2.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 nng7 te3 chioh8-pi kau-tai3 goa2, si7 Siong7-te3 eng7 chng2-thau5-a2 sia2 e5; hi2 teng2-bin7 sou2 sia2 e5, si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 toa7-hoe7 e5 jit8, ti7 soaN-teng2, ti7 he2-tiong, tui3 lin2 sou2 kong2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7.  11). Si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 hit nng7 te3 chioh8-pi, chiu7-si7 iok-pi, kau-tai3 goa2.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 khi2-lai5, kin2-kin2 tui3 chia loh8-khi3; in-ui7 li2 e5 peh-siN3, li2 tui3 Ai-kip8 chhoa7-chhut--lai5 e5, i2-keng pai7-hoai7 ka-ki7; in khoai3-khoai3 phian-oai Goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 e5 lou7; in-ui7 in ui7 ka-ki7 chu3 chit8 sian ngou2-siong7.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh hoan-hu3 goa2 kong2, Goa2 khoaN3 chit e5 peh-siN3, khoaN3 ah, si7 am7-kun2 ngi7 e5 peh-siN3.  14). Li2 chhut-chai7 Goa2, Goa2 beh biat8 in, tui3 thiN-e7 chhat-biat8 in e5 mia5; Goa2 beh hou7 li2 chiaN5-choe3 chit8-kok pi2 in khah-kiong5 khah-toa7.  15). Goa2 chiu7 oat8-tng2-sin loh8-soaN, soaN hou7 he2 sio-toh8, nng7 te3 iok-pi ti7 goa2 nng7 ki chhiu2--nih;  16). goa2 chit8-e7 khoaN3, lin2 i2-keng tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, ui7 ka-ki7 chu3 chit8 chiah gu5-a2, kin2-kin2 oai-chhoah8 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5 lou7.  17). Goa2 eng7 hit nng7 te3 pi tui3 goa2 e5 siang-chhiu2 hiat--loh8-khi3, phah-chih8 ti7 lin2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5.  18). Goa2 phak ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5 e5 khoan2, si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5, bo5 chiah8-piaN2, bo5 lim-chui2; in-ui7 lin2 sou2 hoan7 it-chhe3 e5 choe7, kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2 e5 su7, jia2 I e5 siu7-khi3.  19). Hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa toa7 m7 kam-goan7, siu7-khi3 lin2, goa2 chiu7 chin kiaN, in-ui7 I siu7-khi3 beh biat8 lin2; chong2-si7 hit-pai2 Ia5-ho5-hoa koh thiaN goa2.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 siu7-khi3 A-lun5, beh biat8 i, siang5 hit-si5 goa2 ia7 thoe3 A-lun5 ki5-to2.  21). Hit-si5 goa2 eng7 lin2 hoan7-choe7 e5 mih8, chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 chu3 e5 gu5-a2, eng7 he2 sio i, koh tui5 i, geng2 kau3 iu3-iu3, iu3 kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 thou5-hun2; goa2 eng7 chit e5 thou5-hun2 ia7 ti7 tui3 soaN-teng2 lau5--loh8-lai5 e5 khoe.
	22). Lin2 ia7 ti7 Tha-pi7-lah8, ti7 Ma2-sat, ti7 Ki-phok-lo5-hap-tha-oa2, koh kek-khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe lin2 li7-khui Ka-te-su Pa-ni5-a kong2, Lin2 chiuN7-khi3 seng5-chiap Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 e5 toe7; hit-si5 lin2 ui5-poe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 beng7-leng7, m7-sin3 I, ia7 m7 thiaN I e5 oe7.  24). Tui3 goa2 bat lin2 e5 jit8, lin2 siong5-siong5 poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	25). Goa2 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 beh biat8 lin2, chiu7 phak ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, phak-teh si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5.  26). Goa2 ki5-to2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 boh8-tit biat8-bo5 Li2 e5 peh-siN3, Li2 e5 san2-giap8, chiu7-si7 Li2 eng7 toa7 khui3-lat8 siok8-hoe5 e5, eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2 chhoa7-chhut Ai-kip8 e5;  27). kiu5 Li2 tioh8 ki3-tit Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok; boh8-tit ki3-liam7 chit e5 peh-siN3 e5 ngi7-sim kap in e5 phaiN2, in e5 choe7;  28). kiaN-liau2 Li2 chhoa7 goan2 chhut-lai5 hit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa in-ui7 boe7-oe7 chhoa7 in jip8 I sou2 eng3-un2 in e5 toe7, koh oan3-hun7 in, sou2-i2 chhoa7 in chhut-khi3, beh biat8 in ti7 khong3-ia2.  29). M7-ku2 in si7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3, Li2 e5 san2-giap8, si7 Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5, eng7 Li2 chhun--chhut-lai5 e5 chhiu2, sou2 chhoa7-chhut-lai5 e5.

[10]	Hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 goa2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 phah nng7 te3 chioh8-pi, chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5 e5 khoan2, chiuN7-soaN lai5 Goa2 chia; koh tioh8 choe3 chit8 e5 chha5 e5 kui7.  2). Li2 cheng5 sou2 phah-chih8 hiah e5 pi, hit teng2-bin7 e5 oe7, Goa2 beh sia2 ti7 chiah e5 pi e5 teng2-bin7; li2 tioh8 he7 in ti7 kui7-lai7.  3). Goa2 chiu7 eng7 cho7-kiap-chha5 choe3 chit8 e5 kui7, koh phah nng7-te3 chioh8-pi chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5 e5 khoan2; goa2 chhin-chhiu2 theh8 chi2 nng7-te3 pi chiuN7-soaN.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiong I ti7 toa7-hoe7 e5 jit8, ti7 soaN-teng2, tui3 he2-tiong ka7 li2 kong2 e5 chap8-kai3, chiau3 cheng5 sou2 sia2 e5 khoan2, sia2 ti7 hiah e5 pi--nih; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 chiong hiah-e5 kau-tai3 goa2.  5). Goa2 oat8-tng2-sin loh8-soaN, chiong hiah e5 pi he7 ti7 goa2 sou2 choe3 e5 kui7, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7; kau3-taN iau2 ti7-hia.  6). (I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 Pi2-lo5-pi2-ni5-a-kan khi2-sin, kau3 Mou5-se-lah8; A-lun5 si2 ti7-hia, chiu7 bai5-chong3 ti7-hia; i e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat soa3-chiap i tam-tng che3-si e5 chit.  7). In tui3 hia khi2-sin, kau3 Kok-ko-tai7, koh tui3 Kok-ko-tai7 kau3 Iok-pa-tha, chiu7-si7 u7 khoe-chui2 e5 toe7;  8). hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa hun-piat Li7-bi7 chi-phai3, kng Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 iok-kui7, khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 lai5 hok8-sai7 I, hong7 I e5 mia5 lai5 chiok-hok, kau3 kin-a2-jit8;  9). sou2-i2 Li7-bi7 ti7 i e5 hiaN-ti7-tiong bo5-hun7 bo5-giap8, Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 i e5 san2-giap8, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 tui3 i kong2 e5.)  10). Goa2 koh chhin-chhiuN7 thau5-pai2 tiam3 ti7 soaN-teng2 si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5; hit-pai2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 thiaN goa2, Ia5-ho5-hoa m7-kam biat8 li2.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 goa2 kong2, Li2 khi2-lai5 choe3-thau5 kiaN5 ti7 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5, hou7 in jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap Goa2 sou2 tui3 in e5 liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 beh hou7 in e5 toe7.
	12). I2-sek-liat8 ah, taN Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ai3 li2 sim2-mih8 ah? Kiam2-m7-si7 tok8-tok8 ai3 li2 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, kiaN5 I it-chhe3 e5 to7-lou7, thiaN3 I, chin7-sim chin7-seng3 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3;  13). siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiah e5 kai3-beng7, kap I e5 lut8-le7, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, ui7-tioh8 beh hou7 li2 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3 mah?  14). KhoaN3 ah, thiN kap chiah e5 thiN e5 thiN, toe7 kap toe7-chiuN7 sou2-u7-e5, long2 siok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa tok8-tok8 hoaN-hi2 li2 e5 liat8-chou2, thiaN3 in, keng2 in e5 hou7-e3 ti7 ban7 peh-siN3 tiong, chiu7-si7 lin2 chiah-e5, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 chiu7-si7.  16). Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 ka7 lin2 e5 sim kiaN5 kat-le2, m7-thang ngi7 lin2 e5 am7-kun2.  17). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, I si7 chiah e5 siong7-te3 e5 Siong7-te3, chiah e5 chu2 e5 Chu2.  I si7 chi3-toa7 e5 Siong7-te3, u7 leng5-lek8 koh thang kiaN-ui3-e5; bo5 eng7 goa7-mau7 chhu2--lang5, ia7 bo5 siu7 pou3-lou7.  18). I ui7-tioh8 kou-ji5 kap koaN2-hu7 phoaN3-toan3; koh thiaN3 chhut-goa7 lang5, hou7 i chiah8-chheng7;  19). sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 thiaN3 chhut-goa7 lang5, in-ui7 lin2 ia7 bat chhut-goa7 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7.  20). Li2 tioh8 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, hok8-sai7 I, kiat-lian5 I, ki2 I e5 mia5 lai5 chiu3-choa7.  21). I si7 li2 sou2 o-lo2 e5, si7 li2 e5 Siong7-te3, ui7-tioh8 li2 choe3 hit e5 toa7 koh thang kiaN e5 su7, si7 li2 chhin-bak8 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3-e5.  22). Li2 e5 liat8-chou2 chhit-chap8 lang5 loh8 Ai-kip8, taN Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 hou7 li2 chhin-chhiuN7 thiN-teng2 e5 chhiN hiah--nih choe7.

[11]	Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, siong5-siong5 siu2 I sou2 hoan-hu3 li2 siu2 e5, kap I e5 lut8-le7, hoat-tou7, kai3-beng7.  2). Lin2 kin-a2-jit8 tioh8 chai, in-ui7 goa2 m7-si7 kap lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 kong2, in m7-chai, ia7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 kau3-tok, ui-giam5, toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, kap chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2-kut;  3). i2-kip8 I e5 sin5-jiah, I e5 sou2 choe3, kiN3-na7 ti7 Ai-kip8 tiong tui3 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2, kap i e5 choan5-toe7, sou2 kiaN5 e5;  4). ia7 I chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 Ai-kip8 e5 kun-peng, kap in e5 be2, in e5 chhia; in tui-jip lin2 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa chaiN2-iuN7 hou7 Ang5-hai2 e5 chui2 im--in, biat8-bo5 in kau3 kin-a2-jit8;  5). koh I ti7 khong3-ia2 chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 lin2, kau3 lin2 lai5 chit e5 sou2-chai7;  6). koh I chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun I2-li7-ap e5 kiaN2, Tai7-tan, A-pi2-lan5; toe7 chaiN2-iuN7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan khui-chhui3 thun in, kap in e5 ke-koan3, i2-kip8 in e5 pou3-piN5, kap it-chhe3 kun-te3 in e5 oah8-mih8;  7). chi2-u7 lin2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 toa7-su7.  8). Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 siu2 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, hou7 lin2 chong3-taN2, oe7 jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap lin2 sou2 beh ke3-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7;  9). ia7 hou7 lin2 e5 jit8-chi2 ku2-tng5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kap lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 siuN2-su3 in kap in e5 hou7-e3 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 hit-ho7 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7.  10). In-ui7 li2 beh jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7, m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 chhut-lai5 e5 Ai-kip8 toe7, li2 ti7-hia ia7-cheng2, eng7 kha tah8 lai5 koan3-ak, chhin-chhiuN7 chhai3-hng5;  11). tok8-tok8 lin2 sou2 beh jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 u7 soaN, u7 soaN-kok, lai5 seng5-siu7 thiN e5 hou7-chui2 e5 toe7;  12). si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 koan3-kou3 e5 toe7, tui3 ni5-thau5 kau3 ni5-be2; Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bak8-chiu siong5-siong5 khoaN3 i.
	13). Lin2 na7 liu5-sim thiaN-than3 goa2 e5 kai3-beng7, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5, thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, chin7-sim chin7-seng3 hok8-sai7 I,  14). chiu7 Goa2 beh chiau3-si5 loh8 li2 e5 toe7 sou2 khiam3-eng7 e5 hou7, chiu7-si7 cheng5 e5 hou7, au7 e5 hou7, hou7 li2 thang siu-seng5 li2 e5 gou7-kak, li2 e5 chiu2, li2 e5 iu5;  15). ia7 hou7 li2 e5 chhan5-ia2 hoat-chhau2, chhi7 li2 e5 cheng-siN, li2 ia7 beh tit-tioh8 pa2-chiok.  16). Lin2 tioh8 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, bian2-tit lin2 e5 sim siu7 be5, ti3-kau3 lin2 oai-chhoah8, khi3 hok8-sai7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, lai5 keng3-pai3 i;  17). ti3-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa toa7 siu7-khi3 lin2, hou7 thiN koaiN-bat8 bo5 loh8 hou7, toe7 ia7 bo5 chhut-san2; lin2 chiu7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 e5 sui2 toe7 kin2-kin2 biat8-bo5.  18). Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 eng7 goa2 chiah e5 oe7 ki3 ti7 lin2 e5 sim, lin2 e5 nau2; ia7 tioh8 pak8 ti7 lin2 e5 chhiu2 choe3 ki3-ho7, ti3 ti7 lin2 nng7 lui2 bak8-chiu e5 tiong-ng choe3 ki3-liam7;  19). ia7 tioh8 eng7 che ka3-si7 lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, bo5-lun7 li2 che7 ti7 chhu3-lai7, kiaN5 ti7 lou7--nih, khun3 a2-si7 khi2-lai5, long2 tioh8 kang2-lun7;  20). koh tioh8 sia2 ti7 li2 e5 chhu3 e5 mng5-khia7, i2-kip8 li2 e5 mng5;  21). hou7 lin2 e5 jit8-chi2, kap lin2 e5 kiaN2-sun e5 jit8-chi2, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 lin2 e5 liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 siuN2-su3 in e5 toe7, tit-tioh8 ke-thiN choe7-choe7, chhin-chhiuN7 thiN kham3-toe7 e5 jit8 hiah ku2.  22). Lin2 na7 chu3-i3 chip-siu2 goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, lai5 kiaN5 i, thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, kiaN5 I it-chhe3 e5 lou7, kiat-lian5 ti7 I,  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 beh tui3 lin2 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut che it-chhe3 e5 kok, lin2 ia7 beh tit-tioh8 pi2 lin2 khah-toa7 khah-kiong5 e5 kok.  24). KiN3-na7 lin2 e5 kha-chiuN2 sou2 tah8 e5 toe7, long2 beh kui hou7 lin2, tui3 khong3-ia2 kap Li7-pa-lun3, tui3 hit e5 ho5, chiu7-si7 Pek-lah8 ho5, kau3 sai-peng5 e5 hai2, long2 beh choe3 lin2 e5 keng2-kai3;  25). beh bo5 chit8-lang5 oe7 khia7-tiau5 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5; Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh hou7 lin2 sou2 tah8 e5 choan5-toe7 long2 kiaN lin2, lun2 lin2, chiau3 I sou2 tui3 lin2 kong2 e5.
	26). KhoaN3 ah, goa2 kin-a2-jit8 chiong chiok-hok kap chiu3-chou2 pai5 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  27). lin2 na7 than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 kai3-beng7, goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5, chiu7-si7 chiok-hok;  28). lin2 na7 m7-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 kai3-beng7, oai-chhoah8 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5 lou7, khi3 than3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, lin2 peng5-sou3 sou2 m7-bat e5, chiu7-si7 chiu3-chou2.
	29). Chiong-lai5 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chhoa7 li2 kau3 li2 sou2 beh jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7, li2 tioh8 he7 hit e5 chiok-hok ti7 Ki-li7-sim soaN, he7 hit e5 chiu3-chou2 ti7 I2-pa-lou7 soaN.  30). Chit nng7 e5 soaN kiam2-m7-si7 ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5 hit-peng5, jit8-loh8 e5 lou7 e5 au7-bin7, ti7 khia7-khi2 A-lah8-pa e5 Ka-lam5 lang5 e5 toe7, kap Kiat-kah saN-tui3, oa2-kun7 Mou5-li7 siong7-chhiu7 mah?  31). In-ui7 lin2 beh ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5, jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7, lin2 beh ti7-hia khia7-khi2.  32). Lin2 tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 pai5-liat8 it-chhe3 e5 lut8-le7 hoat-tou7.

[12]	Lin2 ti7 se3-kan it-seng e5 jit8, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 liat8-chou2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 choe3-giap7 e5 toe7, tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 e5 lut8-le7 hoat-tou7, chiu7-si7 chiah-e5.  2). Lin2 sou2 beh koaN2 lai5 seng5-chiap e5 liat8-kok, kiN3-na7 in hok8-sai7 in hiah e5 siong7-te3 e5 sou2-chai7, bo5-lun7 ti7 koaiN5-soaN, ti7 sio2-soaN, ti7 long2-chong2 chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhiu7-kha, long2 tioh8 hui2-hoai7 in;  3). lin2 ia7 tioh8 thiah-hui2 in e5 che3-toaN5, phah-chhui3 in tiau-khek e5 thiau7, eng7 he2 sio in e5 A-sia3-lim5, chho3 in sou2 tiau-khek e5 siong7-te3 e5 siong7, ia7 tioh8 tui3 hit sou2-chai7 tu5-biat8 in e5 mia5;  4). lin2 m7-thang chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni lai5 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  5). Tok8-tok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiong-lai5 tui3 lin2 cheng3 chi-phai3 tiong sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7, thang ti7-hia an-ti3 I e5 mia5, chiu7-si7 I khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, lin2 tioh8 khi3 hia chhe7 I;  6). chiong lin2 e5 sio-che3 kap pat8-ho7 e5 che3, chap8-hun7 chhu2 chit8-hun7 e5 mih8, kap chhiu2--nih e5 ku2-che3, i2-kip8 sia7-goan7 e5 che3, kam-sim hian3 e5 che3, i2-kip8 gu5-kun5 iuN5-kun5 tiong thau5-chui2-siN--e5, long2 tioh8 toa3 kau3 hia;  7). ti7-hia lin2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 ui7-tioh8 lin2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 su3-hok e5, lin2 kap lin2 e5 ke-koan3 long2 tioh8 lim-chiah8 hoaN-hi2.  8). Lan2 kin-a2-jit8 ti7-chia sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7, si7 tak8-lang5 kiaN5 i ka-ki7 khoaN3-choe3 tioh8-e5, lin2 chiong-lai5 m7-thang an2-ni kiaN5.  9). In-ui7 lin2 hian7-kim iau2-be7 u7 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 an-hioh kap san2-giap8.  10). Chong2-si7 lin2 ke3 Iok-tan3, tit-tioh8 khia7-khi2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 lin2 seng5-chiap e5 toe7, koh hou7 lin2 thoat-li7 si3-ui5 long2-chong2 e5 tui3-tek8, tit-tioh8 an-hioh, lai5 an-un2 khia7-khi2;  11). chiu7 beh u7 chit8 sou2-chai7, si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 keng2 lai5 an-ti3 I e5 mia5 e5, kiN3-na7 goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5, chiu7-si7 lin2 e5 sio-che3, kap pat8-ho7 e5 che3, chap8-hun7 chhu2 chit8-hun7 e5 mih8, kap chhiu2--nih e5 ku2-che3, i2-kip8 li2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 he7-goan7 kek8-ho2 e5 mih8, long2 tioh8 toa3 kau3 hia.  12). Lin2 kap lin2 e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, long2 tioh8 hoaN-hi2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5; Li7-bi7 lang5 tiam3 ti7 lin2 e5 mng5-lai7-e5 ia7 si7 an2-ni, in-ui7 in ti7 lin2 tiong-kan bo5-hun7 bo5-giap8.  13). Li5 tioh8 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, m7-thang ti7 li2 khoaN3 kah-i3 e5 sou2-chai7 hian3 lin2 e5 sio-che3;  14). tok8-tok8 ti7 li2 chiah e5 chi-phai3 tiong e5 chit8-e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7, lin2 ti7-hia tioh8 hian3 li2 e5 sio-che3; koh ti7-hia kiaN5 goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5.  15). Chong2-si7 li2 ti7 li2 tak8 e5 mng5-lai7, thang chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 hok-hun7, chiau3 li2 e5 sim sou2 ai3, thai5 cheng-siN chiah8-bah; bo5-lun7 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5, bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5, long2 thang chiah8 i, chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8 leng5-iong5 kap lok8 chit8-poaN.  16). Chong2-si7 huih m7-thang chiah8, tioh8 piaN3 ti7 toe7--nih, chhin-chhiuN7 piaN3-chui2 chit8-iuN7.  17). Li2 e5 ngou2-kok, chiu2, iu5, chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7, hek8-si7 gu5-kun5 iuN5-kun5 tiong thau5-chui2 siN-e5, hek8-si7 li2 he7-goan7 hian3-e5, kam-sim hian3-e5, hek8-si7 chhiu2--nih e5 ku2-che3, long2 m7-thang ti7 li2 e5 mng5-lai7 chiah8 i;  18). tok8-tok8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 chiah8 i, chiu7-si7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7, li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2, li2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, i2-kip8 tiam3 ti7 li2 mng5-lai7 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5, long2 tioh8 chiah8 i; kiN3-na7 li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 e5, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, thang hoaN-hi2.  19). Li2 tioh8 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, ti7 li2 e5 toe7-hng, chit8-si3-lang5 m7-thang pang3-sak Li7-bi7 lang5.
	20). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiau3 I sou2 eng3-un2 li2 e5, khui-khoah li2 e5 keng2-kai3 e5 si5, li2 e5 sim ai3 chiah8-bah, sou2-i2 kong2, Goa2 beh chiah8-bah, chiu7 thang chiau3 li2 e5 sim sou2-ai3 e5 lai5 chiah8-bah.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 keng2 beh an-ti3 I e5 mia5 e5 sou2-chai7, na7 li7-khui li2 chin-hng7, chiu7 thang chiau3 goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa siuN2-su3 li2 e5 gu5, iuN5, chhu2 lai5 thai5 i, thang chiau3 sim sou2-ai3 e5, ti7 li2 e5 mng5-lai7 chiah8 i.  22). Li2 chiah8 i, chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8 leng5-iong5 kap lok8 chit8-poaN; bo5 chheng-khi3 kap chheng-khi3 e5 lang5 piN5-piN5 thang chiah8;  23). tok8-tok8 li2 tioh8 koat-i3, m7-thang chiah8 huih, in-ui7 huih si7 oah8-mia7; li2 m7-thang chiah8 bah, soa3 chiah8 i e5 oah8-mia7;  24). m7-thang chiah8 i, tioh8 piaN3 ti7 toe7--nih8, chhin-chhiuN7 piaN3 chui2 chit8-iuN7;  25). m7-thang chiah8 i; an2-ni li2 kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 khoaN3-choe3 tioh8 e5 su7, li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2-sun chiu7 oe7 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  26). Tok8-tok8 li2 sou2 u7 e5 seng3-mih8, kap li2 sou2 he7-goan7 e5, tioh8 toa3 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7.  27). Li2 e5 sio-che3, bah kap huih, tioh8 hian3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 toaN5-teng2; li2 che3-mih8 e5 huih, tioh8 piaN3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 toaN5; hit e5 bah, li2 thang chiah8.  28). Li2 tioh8 chip-siu2, thiaN-than3 goa2 beng7-leng7 li2 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 khoaN3-choe3 ho2 choe3-tioh8 e5 su7; an2-ni li2 kap li2 e5 hou7-e3 chiu7 thang eng2-oan2 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.
	29). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tu5-biat8 li2 sou2 beh khi3 seng5-chiap e5 kok, li2 seng5-chiap i, lai5 khia7-khi2 i e5 toe7;  30). hit-si5 li2 tioh8 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, m7-thang ti7 in tui3 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tu5-biat8 liau2-au7, ham7-loh8 in e5 lo5-bang7, lai5 te3 in; ia7 m7-thang tham3-thiaN in e5 siong7-te3 e5 su7, kong2, Chiah e5 kok chaiN2-iuN7 hok8-sai7 in e5 siong7-te3, goa2 ia7 beh an2-ni kiaN5.  31). Li2 m7-thang tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 an2-ni kiaN5; in-ui7 in tui3 in e5 siong7-te3 kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa it-chhe3 sou2 thong3-hun7 iam3-ouN3 e5 su7; sim7-chi3 eng7 in e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 eng7 he2 sio, hian3 hou7 in e5 siong7-te3.
	32). KiN3-na7 goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5, lin2 long2 tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5; li2 m7-thang ke-thiN, ia7 m7-thang kiam2-chio2.

[13]	Lin2 tiong-kan na7 u7 sian-ti, a2-si7 bang7-kiN3 bang7-e5 khi2-lai5, tui3 lin2 hian2-chhut sin5-jiah, ki5-su7, chiu7 tui3 lin2 kong2,  2). Lan2 lai5-khi3 than3 li2 peng5-sou3 sou2 m7-bat e5 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, lai5 hok8-sai7 in, i sou2 hian2-beng5 e5 sin5-jiah ki5-su7, chiu7 na7 eng3-giam7,  3). li2 ia7 m7-thang thiaN hit e5 sian-ti, a2-si7 hit e5 bang7-kiN3--e5 e5 oe7; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 teh chhi3 lin2, ai3 chai lin2 si7 chin7-sim chin7-seng3 thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 a2-bo5.  4). Lin2 tioh8 sun7-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, keng3-ui3 I, siu2 I e5 kai3-beng7, thiaN I e5 oe7, hok8-sai7 I, kiat-lian5 I.  5). Hit e5 sian-ti, a2-si7 hit e5 bang7-kiN3 bang7-e5, i2-keng eng7 oe7 poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 chhoa7 lin2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7, siok8-hoe5 lin2 thoat-li7 choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke e5, in an2-ni beh puih8 lin2 li7-khui Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 kiaN5 e5 lou7, li2 chiu7 tioh8 hou7 i si2; an2-ni tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tu5-khi3 hit e5 phaiN2.
	6). Na7 si7 li2 tang5-bu2 e5 hiaN-ti7, a2-si7 li2 e5 kiaN2, li2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, a2-si7 li2 sim-hoai5-tiong e5 bou2, a2-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 li2 siN3-mia7 e5 peng5-iu2, am3-chiN7 in2-iu2 li2, kong2, Lan2 lai5-khi3 hok8-sai7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 li2 kap li2 e5 liat8-chou2 peng5-sou3 m7-bat-e5;  7). si7 li2 si3-ui5 chiah e5 kok e5 siong7-te3, li7-khui lin2 kun7, a2 li7-khui lin2 hng7, tui3 chit e5 toe7-kek8 kau3 hit e5 toe7-kek8 e5,  8). li2 m7-thang than3 i, m7-thang thiaN i, bak8-chiu m7-thang sioh i, li2 m7-thang kho2-lin5 i, ia7 m7-thang khng3-bat8 i;  9). li2 tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2; li2 tioh8 choe3-thau5 he7 chhiu2 beh hou7 i si2, jian5-au7 cheng3 peh-siN3 ia7 he7 chhiu2;  10). li2 tioh8 eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 hou7 i si2; in-ui7 i siuN7 beh puih8 li2 li7-khui Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 chhoa7 li2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7, choe3 lou5-chai5 e5 ke e5.  11). Chiu7 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 beh thiaN-kiN3 lai5 kiaN; bo5 koh kiaN5 chit-ho7 phaiN2-tai7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan.
	12). Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 khia7-khi2 chiah e5 siaN5 e5 chit8-e5, li2 na7 thiaN-kiN3 kong2,  13). U7 hui2-lui7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan chhut, puih8 khia7-khi2 in e5 siaN5 e5 lang5, kong2, Lan2 lai5-khi3 hok8-sai7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, lin2 cheng5 sou2 m7-bat e5;  14). li2 chiu7 tioh8 tham3-thiaN, chha5-kho2, siong5-se3 mng7; khoaN3 ah, ko2-jian5 si7 chin, chun2-chun2 u7 chit-e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 kiaN5 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan;  15). li2 tek-khak tioh8 eng7 to thai5-si2 khia7-khi2 hit e5 siaN5 e5 peh-siN3, chiong i i2-kip8 i sou2-u7-e5, i e5 cheng-siN, it-chin7 eng7 to biat8 i;  16). li2 tioh8 eng7 sou2 chhiuN2 hit e5 siaN5 e5 mih8, thiap8 ti7 koe-chhi7--nih, eng7 he2 sio hit e5 siaN5 kap sou2 chhiuN2 it-chhe3 e5 mih8, hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3; hit e5 siaN5 eng2-eng2 choe3 thou5-tui, bo5 thang koh khi2.  17). Hit e5 eng-kai hui2-biat8 e5 mih8, long2 m7-thang chit8-tiam2-a2 tiau5 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2; hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa soah I e5 toa7 siu7-khi3, un-tian2 li2, lin5-bin2 li2, hou7 li2 ke-thiN lang5-giah8, chiau3 I tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5;  18). in-ui7 li2 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, siu2 I it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, lai5 kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 khoaN3-choe3 ho2-e5.

[14]	Lin2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 kiaN2-ji5, m7-thang ui7-tioh8 si2-lang5 koah ka-ki7 e5 seng-khu, ia7 m7-thang ti7 li2 nng7-lui2 bak8-chiu e5 tiong-ng thi3 kng-kng;  2). in-ui7 li2 choe3 seng3 e5 peh-siN3, lai5 siok8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3; Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 toe7-chiuN7 ban7 peh-siN3 tiong, lai5 keng2 li2 choe3 I tek8-piat8 e5 peh-siN3.
	3). KiN3-na7 kho2-ouN3 e5 mih8, li2 long2 m7-thang chiah8.  4). Li2 sou2 thang chiah8 e5 cheng-siN chiu7-si7 chiah-e5; gu5, mi5-iuN5, soaN-iuN5;  5). lok8, kap leng5-iong5, sio2-lok8, ia2-soaN-iuN5, bi5-lok8, chhiah-iuN5, kiuN.  6). Cheng-siN tiong, kiN3-na7 pun-toe5, toe5 thiah choe3 nng7-peng5 e5, hoan-chhau2 e5 cheng-siN, lin2 long2 thang chiah8 i.  7). Chong2-si7 hiah e5 hoan-chhau2 e5, a2-si7 thiah-toe5 e5, e5 tiong-kan, lin2 m7-thang chiah8-e5, chiu7-si7 chiah-e5; lok8-to5, thou3, sa-hoan, in-ui7 i si7 hoan-chhau2, bo5 pun-toe5, tui3 ti7 lin2 si7 bo5 chheng-khi3.  8). Ti, in-ui7 i u7 pun-toe5 ia7 bo5 hoan-chhau2, tui3 ti7 lin2 si7 bo5 chheng-khi3; in e5 bah lin2 m7-thang chiah8; si2-e5 ia7 m7-thang bong.
	9). Ti7 chui2-tiong lin2 sou2 thang chiah8-e5, si7 chiah-e5;  10). kiN3 u7-sit8 u7-lan5 e5, lin2 long2 thang chiah8; kiN3 bo5-sit8 bo5-lan5 e5, lin2 long2 m7-thang chiah8; tui3 ti7 lin2 chiu7 bo5 chheng-khi3.
	11). KiN3 chheng-khi3 e5 chiau2, lin2 long2 thang chiah8 i;  12). m7-thang chiah8-e5 chiu7-si7 eng, hiau, tiau;  13). chian, sio2-eng, ian kap i e5 lui7;  14). it-chhe3 e5 ou-a kap i e5 lui7,  15). to5-chiau2, kang e5 to5-chiau2, hi5-eng, chhiok-eng kap i e5 lui7;  16). am3-kong-chiau2, kou-ng5, niau-thau5-eng,  17). the5-ou5, chhau3-thau5-eng, lou5-chi5,  18). hoh8, peh8-leng7-si kap i e5 lui7, ti3-ke3-chiau2, pian2-hok.  19). KiN3 u7 sit8 oe7 so5 e5 mih8, tui3 ti7 lin2 chiu7 bo5 chheng-khi3, lin2 long2 m7-thang chiah8 i;  20). kiN3 oe7 pe chheng-khi3 e5 mih8, lin2 long2 thang chiah8.
	21). KiN3 ka-ki7 si2 e5 mih8, lin2 long2 m7-thang chiah8; thang hou7 lin2 mng5-lai7 kia3-kha e5 lang5 chiah8, a2-si7 boe7 hou7 goa7-kok lang5 chiah8; in-ui7 li2 si7 seng3 e5 peh-siN3, siok8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3.  Chu2 soaN-iuN5-a2, m7-thang eng7 i e5 bu2 e5 lin.
	22). Li2 tioh8 chiong li2 ia7-cheng2 sou2 chhut-san2 e5, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 chhan5-hng5 tak8-ni5 sou2 chhut e5, chap8-hun7 thiu chit8-hun7.  23). Li2 e5 ngou2-kok, chiu2, iu5, chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7, kap gu5 iuN5 thau5-chui2 siN-e5, li2 tioh8 chiah8 i ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7-si7 I sou2 beh keng2 lai5 an-ti3 I e5 mia5 e5 sou2-chai7; hou7 li2 hak8-sip8 siong5-siong5 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3.  24). Tng Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 su3-hok li2 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh keng2 an-ti3 I e5 mia5 e5 sou2-chai7, na7 li7-khui li2 thai3-hng7, hit tiau5 lou7 thai3-tng5, ti3-kau3 li2 boe7-oe7 toa3 chiah e5 mih8 kau3 hia;  25). li2 chiu7 thang oaN7 gun5, chiong gun5 pau--khi2-lai5, nih8 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2-lai7, khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7;  26). li2 eng7 chit e5 gun5 chiau3 sim sou2 ai3 boe2 i, hek8-si7 gu5, hek8-si7 iuN5, hek8-si7 chiu2, hek8-si7 kau7-chiu2, kiN3-na7 li2 e5 sim sou2 i3-ai3 e5; ti7-hia li2 kap li2 e5 ke-koan3, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiah8 lai5 hoaN-hi2;  27). tiam3 ti7 li2 mng5-lai7 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5 li2 m7-thang pang3-sak i, in-ui7 i ti7 lin2 tiong-kan bo5 hun7 bo5 giap8.
	28). Tak8-pai2 kau3 saN-ni5 moa2, li2 tioh8 chiong hit-ni5 e5 thou2-san2 chap8-hun7 thiu chit8-hun7, khng3 ti7 li2 e5 mng5-lai7;  29). in-ui7 Li7-bi7 lang5 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan bo5 hun7 bo5 giap8, i kap chhut-goa7 lang5, i2-kip8 kou-ji5, koaN2-hu7, tiam3 ti7 lin2 mng5-lai7 e5, long2 thang lai5 chiah8 kau3 pa2; ti3-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 li2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, su3-hok li2.

[15]	Tak8-pai2 kau3 chhit-ni5 e5 lou7-be2, li2 tioh8 kiaN5 thau2-pang3.  2). Thau2-pang3 e5 le7, chiu7-si7 an2-ni; hoan7-na7 che3-chu2 chioh chhu3-piN-e5, tioh8 thau2-pang3; m7-thang tui3 li2 e5 chhu3-piN kap hiaN-ti7 tui-tho2; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 thau2-pang3 i2-keng soan-pou3 lah.  3). Na7-si7 goa7-kok lang5 li2 thang ka7 i tui-tho2 sou2 khiam3 e5; tok8-tok8 li2 e5 mih8 ti7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 e5, li2 e5 chhiu2 tioh8 thau2-pang3 i.  4,5). Li2 na7 liu5-sim thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 che it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, chiu7 beh ti7 lin2 tiong-kan bo5 song3-hiong lang5; in-ui7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh toa7-toa7 su3-hok li2.  6). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh chiau3 I sou2 eng3-un2 su3-hok li2; li2 beh chioh hou7 choe7-choe7 kok, ia7 li2 m7-bian2 chioh; li2 beh koan2-hat choe7-choe7 kok, ia7 in boe7 koan2-hat li2.
	7). Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7, na7 ti7 li2 chit8 e5 siaN5-mng5-lai7, li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 tiong, u7 chit8 e5 song3-hiong lang5 kap li2 ti7-teh, chiu7 m7-thang tui3 li2 song3-hiong e5 hiaN-ti7 ngi7 li2 e5 sim, kiu li2 e5 chhiu2;  8). tek-khak tioh8 tui3 i khui li2 e5 chhiu2, chiau3 i sou2 khiam3-eng7 e5 chioh i, pou2 i e5 bo5-kau3.  9). Li2 tioh8 ka-ki7 kin2-sin7, kiaN-liau2 li2 sim-lai7 u7 phaiN2 liam7-thau5, kong2, Te7-chhit ni5, thau2-pang3 e5 ni5, kun7 lah, li2 chiu7 gin5 li2 song3-hiong e5 hiaN-ti7, long2 m7 hou7 i, ti3-kau3 i ui7-tioh8 li2 kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 chiu7 u7-choe7;  10). li2 tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i; hou7 i e5 si5, sim-lai7 m7-thang hoan5-lo2; in-ui7 tui3 chit e5 su7, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh ti7 li2 it-chhe3 sou2 kiaN5 e5, kap li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 e5, su3-hok li2.  11). In-ui7 ti7 hit sou2-chai7, song3-hiong lang5 eng2 boe7 tng7; sou2-i2 goa2 beng7-leng7 li2 kong2, Ti7 li2 e5 keng2-lai7, tek-khak tioh8 tui3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7, song3-hiong e5, khiam3-kheh e5, lai5 khui li2 e5 chhiu2.
	12). Li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 tiong, na7 u7 chit8-e5 Hi-pek-lai5 e5 ta-pou-lang5, a2-si7 Hi-pek-lai5 e5 cha-bou2-lang5, boe7 hou7 li2, hok8-sai7 li2 lak8-ni5; kau3 te7-chhit ni5, chiu7 thau2-pang3 i khi3 chu7-iu5.  13). Li2 thau2-pang3 i khi3 chu7-iu5 e5 si5, m7-thang hou7 i khang-chhiu2 khi3;  14). tioh8 tui3 li2 e5 iuN5-kun5, gou7-kak-tiuN5, chiu2-khut tiong, choe7-choe7 hou7 i; chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 su3-hok li2 e5, lai5 hou7 i.  15). Tioh8 ki3-tit li2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 choe3 lou5-chai5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kiu3-siok8 li2; in-ui7 an2-ni, goa2 kin-a2-jit8 beng7-leng7 li2 chit e5 su7.  16). I na7 tui3 li2 kong2, Goa2 bo5 beh li7-khui li2, in-ui7 i thiaN3 li2 kap li2 e5 ke-koan3, koh in-ui7 tiam3 li2 hia khia7 chin-ho2;  17). li2 tioh8 eng7 chng3-a2 tui3 mng5--nih kng3 i e5 hi7-a2, i chiu7 eng2-eng2 choe3 li2 e5 lou5-pok8.  Li2 khoan2-thai7 li2 e5 lu2-pi7 ia7 si7 an2-ni.  18). Li2 thau2-pang3 i khi3 chu7-iu5 e5 si5, m7-thang liah8-choe3 khek-khui, in-ui7 i hok8-sai7 li2 lak8-ni5, pi2 chhiaN3-kang-e5 teng5-pe7 tat8; Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh ti7 li2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, su3-hok li2.
	19). KiN3-na7 gu5-kun5 iuN5-kun5, thau5-chui2-siN--e5, kang-e5, li2 tioh8 hun-piat choe3-seng3, kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3; gu5-kun5 thau5-chui2-siN--e5, m7-thang choe3-kang; iuN5-kun5 thau5-chui2-siN--e5, m7-thang chian2 i e5 mng5.  20). Li2 kap li2 e5 ke-koan3, tak8-ni5 tioh8 chiah8 i ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7-si7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7.  21). Na7 u7 phoa3-siuN3 e5, hek8-si7 pai2-kha, hek8-si7 chhiN-mi5, bo5-lun7 u7 sim2-mih8 phaiN2 e5 phoa3-siuN3, long2 m7-thang choe3-che3 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3;  22). thang ti7 li2 e5 mng5-lai7 chiah8 i; bo5 chheng-khi3 kap chheng-khi3 e5 lang5 long2 thang, chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8 leng5-iong5 kap lok8 chit8-iuN7;  23). tok8-tok8 m7-thang chiah8 i e5 huih; tioh8 piaN3 ti7 toe7--nih, chhin-chhiuN7 piaN3 chui2 chit8-iuN7.

[16]	Li2 tioh8 chu3-i3 A-pit geh8, lai5 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 poaN5-ke3-choeh; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 ti7 A-pit geh8 mi5-si5 chhoa7 li2 chhut Ai-kip8.  2). Li2 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh keng2 lai5 an-ti3 I e5 mia5 e5 sou2-chai7, tui3 li2 e5 iuN5-kun5 gu5-kun5, eng7 ju5-oat8-choeh e5 cheng-siN, hian3-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3.  3). Li2 m7-thang eng7 u7-kaN3 e5 piaN2 chham teh chiah8; chhit-jit8 ku2 li2 tioh8 eng7 bo5-kaN3 e5 piaN2 chham teh chiah8, chiu7-si7 khun3-khou2 e5 piaN2; beh hou7 li2 it-seng e5 jit8 ki3-tit li2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 jit8; in-ui7 li2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 si5 chin koaN2-kin2.  4). Ti7 li2 e5 si3-keng2-lai7, chhit-jit8 ku2 long2 m7-thang khoaN3-kiN3 kaN3; thau5-chit8-jit8 e5-hng sou2 hian3 e5 che3-bah, m7-thang lau5 chit8-tiam2-a2 kau3 thiN-kng.  5). Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 hiah e5 siaN5-mng5-lai7 li2 m7-thang hian3 poaN5-ke3-choeh e5 che3.  6). Tok8-tok8 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh keng2 choe3 an-ti3 I e5 mia5 e5 sou2-chai7, kau3 e5-hng jit8-loh8 e5 si5, chiu7-si7 li2 chhut Ai-kip8 e5 si5, tioh8 hian3 poaN5-ke3-choeh e5 che3;  7). tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7, pek lai5 chiah8 i; keh cha2-khi2 li2 oat8-to3--khi3 li2 e5 pou3-piN5.  8). Li2 tioh8 chiah8 bo5-kaN3-piaN2 lak8-jit8; te7-chhit jit8 li2 tioh8 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 giam5-siok-hoe7; long2 m7-thang choe3-kang.
	9). Li2 tioh8 ui7 ka-ki7 sng3 chhit e5 chhit-jit8; tui3 li2 khi2-thau5 eng7 liam5-a2 koah ngou2-kok e5 si5, chiu7 sng3 chhit e5 chhit-jit8.  10). Li2 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 siu2 chhit-chhit-jit8-choeh; chiong li2 e5 chhiu2 e5 le2-mih8 hong7-hian3, si7 chiau3 li2 e5 sim sou2 goan7-e5, ia7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 su3-hok li2 e5.  11). Li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, kap tiam3 ti7 li2 siaN5-mng5-lai7 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5, i2-kip8 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan kia3-kha-e5, kap kou-ji5, koaN2-hu7, long2 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh keng2 an-ti3 I e5 mia5 e5 sou2-chai7, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 hoaN-hi2.  12). Li2 tioh8 ki3-tit li2 ti7 Ai-kip8 bat choe3 lou5-chai5; li2 tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 chiah e5 lut8-le7.
	13). Gou7-kak-tiuN5 kap chiu2-khut sou2 chhut e5, li2 siu-khng3 liau2-au7, tioh8 siu2 tah chhau2-liau5-a2 choeh chhit-jit8;  14). siu2 choeh e5 si5, li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, kap tiam3 ti7 li2 siaN5-mng5-lai7 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5, i2-kip8 kia3-kha-e5, kap kou-ji5, koaN2-hu7, long2 tioh8 hoaN-hi2.  15). Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7, li2 tioh8 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 choeh chhit-jit8; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ti7 li2 it-chhe3 e5 but8-san2, kap li2 e5 chhiu2 it-chhe3 sou2 choe3 e5, beh su3-hok li2, li2 chiu7 chin toa7 hoaN-hi2.  16). Li2 it-chhe3 e5 ta-pou-teng, tioh8 ti7 tu5-kaN3-choeh, chhit-chhit-choeh, tah-liau5-a2 choeh, chit8-ni5 saN-pai2, long2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 I sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7; ia7 m7-thang khang-chhiu2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5;  17). tak8-lang5 tioh8 chiau3 i e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 hian3, chiu7-si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 hok-hun7.
	18).
