Li2 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 tak8 e5 siaN5-mng5-lai7, chiau3 li2 hiah e5 chi-phai3, ui7 ka-ki7 siat-lip8 sim2-phoaN3-koaN kap koaN-tiuN2; in tioh8 chiau3 kong-gi7 e5 phoaN3-toan3, lai5 sim2-phoaN3 peh-siN3.  19). Li2 e5 sim2-phoaN3 m7-thang oan-ong2, m7-thang khoaN3 lang5 e5 goa7-mau7, ia7 m7-thang siu7 pou3-lou7; in-ui7 pou3-lou7 oe7 hou7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5 bak8-chiu chhiN-mi5, koh oe7 hou7 gi7-lang5 e5 oe7 peng2-to3-tng2.  20). Li2 tioh8 tui-jip chi3-kong chi3-gi7, hou7 li2 oe7 oah8, seng5-chiap Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7.
	21). Li2 ui7 ka-ki7 sou2 khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 toaN5, m7-thang ti7 hi2 piN-a2 chai sim2-mih8 chhiu7-bak8, choe3 A-sia3-lah8;  22). ia7 m7-thang ui7 ka-ki7 chhai7 tiau-khek e5 thiau7; che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 oan3-hun7 e5.

[17]	KiN3-u7 phoa3-siuN3, a2-si7 u7 sim2-mih8 phaiN2-iuN7 e5 gu5 iuN5, li2 m7-thang che3-hian3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 iam3-ouN3 e5.
	2). Ti7 lin2 tiong-kan, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 hiah e5 siaN5 e5 tiong-kan, na7 tu2-tioh8 u7 lang5, hek8-si7 lam5, hek8-si7 lu2, kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2-e5, ui5-poe7 I e5 iok,  3).  khi3 hok8-sai7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 lai5 keng3-pai3 i, hek8-si7 jit8, hek8-si7 geh8, a2-si7 thiN-teng2 e5 ban7-siong7, si7 goa2 sou2 be7-bat beng7-leng7-e5;  4). na7 u7 lang5 ka7 li2 kong2, li2 ia7 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3, chiu7 tioh8 siong5-se3 tham3-thiaN; khoaN3 ah, ko3-jian5 u7-iaN2, sit8-chai7 u7 chit-e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, kiaN5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong;  5). li2 tioh8 chiong kiaN5 chit e5 phaiN2-tai7 e5 ta-pou-lang5, a2-si7 hu-jin5-lang5, thoa kau3 siaN5-mng5-goa7, eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 hit e5 ta-pou-lang5, a2-si7 hu7-jin5-lang5, hou7 i si2.  6). Tioh8 pin5 nng7 e5 kan-cheng3, a2-si7 saN e5 kan-cheng3 e5 chhui3, eng-kai si2--e5 tioh8 hou7 i si2; na7 pin5 chit8-lang5 e5 chhui3 choe3 kan-cheng3, chiu7 m7-thang hou7 i si2;  7). kan-cheng3-e5 tioh8 choe3-thau5 he7 chhiu2 tim3 i, jian5-au7 cheng3 peh-siN3 ia7 he7 chhiu2 hou7 i si2; an2-ni chiu7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tu5--khi3 hit e5 phaiN2.
	8). Li2 siaN5-mng5-lai7 na7 u7 oan-ke e5 su7, hek8-si7 in-ui7 lau5-huih, hek8-si7 in-ui7 saN-ko3, hek8-si7 in-ui7 saN-phah, si7 li2 sou2 boe7 hiau2-tit toan3 e5, li2 chiu7 tioh8 khi2-lai5, khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7;  9). kiN3 che3-si Li7-bi7 lang5, kap tng-si5 e5 sim2-phoaN3-koaN, lai5 mng7 in; in beh chiong phoaN3-su5 chi2-si7 li2;  10).  in ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7 chi2-si7 li2 e5 phoaN3-su5, li2 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5; kiN3 in sou2 ka3-si7 li2 e5, tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 i;  11). tioh8 chiau3 in sou2 beh ka3-si7 li2 hoat-tou7 e5 chong-chi2, ia7 tioh8 chiau3 in sou2 ka7 li2 kong2 e5 phoaN3-toan3 lai5 kiaN5; in sou2 chi2-si7 li2 e5 phoaN3-su5, li2 m7-thang phian-cho2 phian-iu7.  12). Na7 u7 lang5 chu7-choan kiaN5, m7-thiaN che3-si, chiu7-si7 ti7-hia khia7-teh lai5 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5, a2-si7 m7-thiaN sim2-phoaN3-koaN, chiu7 tioh8 hou7 hit-lang5 si2; an2-ni li2 chiu7 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 tiong tu5-khi3 hit e5 phaiN2;  13). peh-siN3 beh long2 thiaN-kiN3 lai5 kiaN, bo5 koh chu7-choan kiaN5.
	14). Li2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7, tit-tioh8 hit sou2-chai7 lai5 khia7-khi2 e5 si5, na7 kong2, Goa2 beh siat-lip8 ong5 choe3 goa2 e5 thau5, chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 si3-ui5 e5 liat8-kok chit8-iuN7,  15). li2 tek-khak tioh8 siat-lip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 keng2 e5 lang5 choe3-ong5, choe3 li2 e5 thau5; tui3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 tiong siat-lip8 chit8-lang5 choe3-ong5, choe3 li2 e5 thau5; goa7-kok lang5, m7-si7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 e5, li2 m7-thang siat-lip8 choe3 li2 e5 thau5.  16). Chong2-si7 ong5 m7-thang ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 ke-thiN choe7-choe7 chiah be2, ia7 m7-thang ui7-tioh8 beh ke-thiN khah-choe7 chiah be2, hou7 peh-siN3 to3-khi3 Ai-kip8, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bat beng7-leng7 lin2 kong2, Lin2 boh8 koh tui3 hit tiau5 lou7 to3-khi3.  17). I ia7 m7-thang ui7 ka-ki7 chhoa7 choe7-choe7 hou7-hui, kiaN-liau2 i e5 sim poe7-biu7; i ia7 m7-thang ui7 pun2-sin chek-chu7 choe7-choe7 kim-gun5.  18). I che7 i e5 kok-ui7 e5 si5, tioh8 eng7 chit8 pun2 chheh chhau-sia2 chit e5 lut8-hoat, tioh8 tui3 hit-pun2 chun5 ti7 che2-si Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 e5 lai5 chhau i;  19). hit-pun2 tioh8 he7 ti7 i hia, chit8-si3-lang5 tioh8 thak8 i; thang hak8-sip8 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa i e5 Siong7-te3; tioh8 chip-siu2 chit e5 lut8-hoat it-chhe3 e5 oe7, kap chiah e5 lut8-le7 lai5 kiaN5 i;  20). bian2-tit i chu7-ko lai5 khoaN3-khin hiaN-ti7; koh bian2-tit i phian-cho2 phian-iu7, lai5 li7-khui chit e5 kai3-beng7; thang hou7 i kap i e5 kiaN2-sun ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong kok-ui7 ku2-tng5.

[18]	Che3-si Li7-bi7 lang5, thong Li7-bi7 e5 chi-phai3, in ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong bo5 hun7 bo5 giap8; in sou2 beh chiah8-e5, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 he2-che3, kap I e5 giap8.  2). In ti7 in hiaN-ti7 tiong bo5 san2-giap8, Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 in e5 san2-giap8, chiau3 sou2 tui3 in kong2 e5.  3). Che3-si tui3 peh-siN3 sou2 eng-kai tit-tioh8 e5 hun7 chiu7-si7 chiah-e5; kiN3-na7 hian3 gu5 a2-si7 iuN5 choe3 che3 e5, tioh8 chiong cheng5-thui2, kap nng7 e5 chhui3-phoe2, kap tou7, hou7 che3-si.  4). Li2 e5 ngou2-kok, li2 e5 chiu2, li2 e5 iu5, khi2-thau5 siu-seng5 e5, kap khi2-thau5 chian2 e5 iuN5-mng5, long2 tioh8 hou7 i.  5). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 tui3 li2 cheng3 chi-phai3 keng2 i, hou7 i kap i e5 kiaN2-sun, hong7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, khia7-teh, hok8-sai7 I kau3 eng2-oan2.
	6). Na7 u7 Li7-bi7 lang5 bo5-lun7 kia3-kha ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong toh-loh8 chit8 cho7 siaN5-mng5-lai7, tui3 hia chhut-lai5, choan-sim i3-ai3 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh keng2 e5 sou2-chai7,  7). chiu7 i beh hong7 Ia5-ho5-hoa i Siong7-te3 e5 mia5 hok8-sai7, chhin-chhiuN7 i cheng3 hiaN-ti7 hiah-e5 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5 chit8-iuN7;  8). ti7 i boe7 chou2-kong e5 giap8 i2-goa7, i sou2 tit-tioh8 chiah8 e5 hun7-giap8 tioh8 kap in piN5.
	9). Li2 na7 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7, li2 m7-thang oh8 hiah e5 kok kho2-ouN3 e5 su7 lai5 kiaN5.  10). Lin2 tiong-kan m7-thang u7 lang5 hou7 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 keng-ke3 he2, kiaN5 sia5-sut8 e5, chiam-pok e5, khoaN3-mia7 e5, choe3 sai-kong e5;  11). ui7-hu5 e5, choe3 tang5-ki e5, kiaN5 mou5-sut8 e5, khan-bong5 e5;  12). in-ui7 kiN3-na7 kiaN5 hiah e5 su7 e5, long2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 iam3-ouN3; ia7 si7 ui7-tioh8 chiah e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 tui3 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2 in chhut.  13). Li2 tui3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, tioh8 choe3 oan5-choan5 e5 lang5.  14). In-ui7 li2 sou2 beh seng5-chiap hiah e5 kok, long2 thiaN-than3 chiam-pok e5, kiaN5 sia5-sut8 e5; lun7-kau3 li2, chiu7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 m7-chun2 li2 an2-ni kiaN5.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh tui3 lin2 tiong-kan, tui3 lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7, heng-khi2 sian-ti chhin-chhiuN7 goa2, lin2 tioh8 thiaN-than3 i.  16). Chiau3 li2 ti7 Ho5-liat8 chu7-hoe7 e5 jit8, tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 it-chhe3 sou2 kiu5-e5, kong2, Boh8-tit hou7 goa2 koh thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 siaN; ia7 boh8-tit hou7 goa2 koh khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 toa7-he2, bian2-tit goa2 si2-bo5.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tui3 goa2 kong2, In sou2 kong2-e5 si7 ho2.  18). Goa2 beh ti7 in hiaN-ti7 tiong, ka7 in heng-khi2 chit8 e5 sian-ti chhin-chhiuN7 li2, Goa2 beh chiong Goa2 e5 oe7 he7 ti7 i e5 chhui3, i beh chiong Goa2 it-chhe3 sou2 beng7-leng7-e5 tui3 in kong2.  19). I thok Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5 thoan5 Goa2 e5 oe7, lang5 na7 m7-thiaN, Goa2 beh pan7 i.  20). Chong2-si7 sian-ti chu7-choan thok Goa2 e5 mia5, kong2 Goa2 sou2 bo5 beng7-leng7 i kong2 e5 oe7, a2-si7 hong7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 e5 mia5 lai5 kong2, hit e5 sian-ti tioh8 si2.  21). Li2 e5 sim na7 siuN7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 bo5 kong2 e5 oe7, goan2 beh-thai2 oe7 chai ah?  22). Na7 u7 sian-ti thok Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 lai5 kong2--e5, hit e5 su7 na7 bo5 chiaN5, ia7 bo5 eng3-giam7, che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 bo5 kong2-e5, si7 hit e5 sian-ti chu7-choan lai5 kong2-e5, li2 boh8-tit kiaN i.

[19]	Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiong-lai5 chian2-tu5 hiah e5 kok, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 eng7 in e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 li2 e5, li2 seng5-chiap in, lai5 khia7-khi2 in e5 siaN5, kap in e5 chhu3;  2). hit-si5 li2 chiu7 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7, ka7 i hun-piat saN e5 siaN5.  3). Tioh8 chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 seng5-chiap kai3-lai7 e5 toe7, hun-choe3 saN-khu, koh ka7 i khui lou7, hou7 hiah e5 thai5-lang5-e5 long2 thang chau2-khi3 hia.  4). Thai5-si2-lang5-e5 chau2-khi3 hia, chiu7 thang tit-tioh8 oah8, hit e5 le7 chiu7-si7 an2-ni; kiN3-na7 peng5-sou3 bo5 kiat-oan3 chho3-gou7 lai5 thai5-si2 i e5 chhu3-piN;  5). chiu7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 kap i e5 chhu3-piN khi3 chhiu7-na5, beh chho3 chhiu7-bak8, chhiu2 kiah8 pou2-thau5 chit8-e7 chho3, beh chho3 hit e5 chhiu7, pou2-thau5-bah lut-khi3, siong-tioh8 i e5 chhu3-piN ti3-kau3 si2, chit e5 lang5 tioh8 chau2 kau3 hiah e5 siaN5 e5 chit8-e5, chiu7 thang oah8-teh;  6). bian2-tit po3-jin5-beng7-e5, tng i sim-he2 toh8 e5 si5, tui-jip thai5-lang5 e5 lang5, in-ui7 lou7 chin-hng7 jip-tioh8 chiu7 thai5-si2 i; ki5-sit8 i m7 eng-kai si2, in-ui7 peng5-si5 i bo5 oan3-hun7 i.  7). Sou2-i2 goa2 beng7-leng7 li2 kong2, Tioh8 ka7 i hun-piat saN e5 siaN5.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, na7 chiau3 I tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7-e5, khui-khoah li2 e5 keng2-kai3, chiong sou2 eng3-un2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 e5 choan5-toe7 hou7 li2;  9). goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, li2 na7 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 i, thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, siong5-siong5 kiaN5 I hiah e5 to7-lou7, chiu7 ti7 chi2 saN e5 siaN5 i2-goa7, tioh8 koh ui7 ka-ki7 ke-siat saN e5 siaN5;  10). bian2-tit bo5-choe7 e5 huih lau5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7, ti3-kau3 lau5-huih e5 choe7 kui ti7 li2.  11). Chong2-si7 lang5 na7 oan3-hun7 i e5 chhu3-piN, bih--teh, khi2-lai5 phah i, siong-hai7 i kau3 si2, chiu7 chau2 kau3 hiah e5 siaN5 e5 chit8-e5;  12). i e5 siaN5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 tioh8 chhe lang5, tui3 hia toa3 i chhut-lai5, kau ti7 po3-jin5-beng7 e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, hou7 i si2;  13). li2 e5 bak8-chiu m7-thang kho2-lin5 i; ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong tioh8 tu5-khi3 bo5-choe7 e5 huih, hou7 li2 thang tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.
	14). Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 seng5-chiap e5 toe7, m7-thang i5-soa2 chhu3-piN e5 kai3-chi2; hit-e5 si7 cheng5 e5 lang5 sou2 chhai7 ti7 li2 soa3-chiap e5 giap8 e5 lai7-bin7 e5.
	15). Kan-ta chit8-lang5 boe7 thang khi2-lai5 kan-cheng3 lang5 sim2-mih8 phaiN2, sim2-mih8 choe7, chiu7-si7 i kiN3 sou2 hoan7 e5 choe7; tek-khak tioh8 pin5 nng7 e5 kan-cheng3 e5 lang5 e5 chhui3, a2-si7 saN e5 kan-cheng3 e5 lang5 e5 chhui3, chiah thang teng7 i e5 an3.  16). Na7 u7 lam7-sam2 kan-cheng3 e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek bou2 lang5, kan-cheng3 i kiaN5-phaiN2,  17). chiu7 chi2 nng7-e5 saN-chiN3 e5 lang5 tioh8 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, kap tng-si5 e5 che3-si, kap sim2-phoaN3-koaN e5 bin7-cheng5.  18). Sim2-phoaN3-koaN tioh8 siong5-se3 chha5-mng7; khoaN3 ah, na7 choe3 kan-cheng3 e5 lang5, ko2-jian5 si7 ke2 kan-cheng3, eng7 ke2 kan-cheng3 beh hai7 i e5 hiaN-ti7,  19). lin2 chiu7 tioh8 khoan2-thai7 i, chhin-chhiuN7 i siuN7 beh khoan2-thai7 i e5 hiaN-ti7 e5; an2-ni tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tu5-khi3 hit e5 phaiN2.  20). Ki5-u5 e5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 long2 beh kiaN, chiu7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan bo5 koh kiaN5 chit ho7 phaiN2.  21). Li2 e5 bak8-chiu m7-thang kho2-lin5 i, tioh8 eng7 mia7 pe5 mia7, bak8-chiu pe5 bak8-chiu, chhui3-khi2 pe5 chhui3-khi2, chhiu2 pe5 chhiu2, kha pe5 kha.

[20]	Li2 chhut-khi3 kap tui3-tek8 kau-chian3 e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 be2, chhia, i2-kip8 peh-siN3 pi2 li2 khah-choe7-e5, m7-bian2 kiaN in; in-ui7 chhoa7 li2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kap li2 ti7-teh.  2). Lin2 teh-beh lim5-tin7 kau-chian3 e5 si5, che3-si tioh8 kau3 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5 soan-pou3;  3). tui3 in kong2, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ah, lin2 tioh8 thiaN; lin2 kin-a2-jit8 beh kap peh-siN3 tui3-tek8 kau-chian3, m7-thang sit-taN2, m7-thang kiaN, lai5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, ia7 m7-thang in-ui7 in lai5 lun2-neh;  4). in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiu7-si7 kap lin2 saN-kap khi3 e5, beh thoe3 lin2 kap tui3-tek8 kau-chian3 lai5 chin2-kiu3 lin2.  5). Hiah e5 koaN-tiuN2 ia7 tioh8 tui3 peh-siN3 soan-pou3, kong2, Chi7-chui7 khi2 sin-chhu3 iau2-be7 kiaN5 lok8-seng5 e5 le2 ah? i tioh8 to3-khi3 in tau, kiaN-liau2 i tin7-bong5, pat8-lang5 kiaN5 lok8-seng5 e5 le2.  6). Chi7-chui7 cheng3 phu5-to5-hng5, iau2-be7 u7 eng7-tioh8 i e5 ke2-chi2 ah? i ia7 thang to3-khi3 in tau, kiaN-liau2 i tin7-bong5, pat8-lang5 khi3 eng7 i.  7). Chi7-chui7 pheng3-tiaN7 bou2, iau2-be7 chhoa7 i ah? i ia7 thang to3-khi3 in tau, kiaN-liau2 i tin7-bong5, pat8-lang5 chhoa7 i.  8). Hiah e5 koaN-tiuN2 koh tioh8 tui3 peh-siN3 soan-pou3, kong2, Chi7-chui7 kiaN-hiaN5 sit-taN2 ah? i thang to3-khi3 in tau, kiaN-liau2 i e5 hiaN-ti7 e5 sim siau-iuN5, chhin-chhiuN7 i e5 sim chit8-iuN7.  9). Hiah e5 koaN-tiuN2 tui3 peh-siN3 soan-pou3 beng5-pek8, tioh8 siat-lip8 hiah e5 kun-tiuN2 choe3-thau5 lai5 chhoa7 peh-siN3.
	10). Li2 oa2-kun7 chit8 e5 siaN5 beh phah e5 si5, tioh8 tai7-seng tui3 i soan-pou3 ho5-peng5 e5 oe7.  11). I na7 eng7 ho5-peng5 e5 oe7 tap-hok li2, ka7 li2 khui siaN5-mng5, hi2 tiong-kan sou2 u7 e5 peh-siN3 long2 beh choe3 li2 e5 chhe-eng7, lai5 hok8-sai7 li2.  12). I na7 m7-kheng2 kap li2 ho5-ho2, hoan2-tng2 beh kap lin2 kau-chian3, lin2 chiu7 tioh8 ui5-khun3 i.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 eng7 i kau-hu3 li2, li2 chiu7 tioh8 eng7 to it-chin7 thai5-si2 i hiah e5 ta-pou-teng;  14). tok8-tok8 hu7-lu2, gin2-na2, cheng-siN, kap siaN5-lai7 it-chhe3 sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8, li2 thang chhiuN2 i lai5 choe3 ka-ki7 e5 lou7-eng7; li2 sou2 chhiuN2 li2 e5 tui3-tek8 e5 mih8, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5, li2 thang chiah8-eng7.  15). Li7-khui li2 hng7-hng7 hiah e5 siaN5, m7-si7 chiah e5 liat8-kok e5 siaN5, li2 tioh8 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 i.  16). Tok8-tok8 siok8 chiah e5 peh-siN3 e5 siaN5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 i2-keng siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8, ki5-tiong kiN3-u7 chhoan2-khui3 e5, li2 m7-thang hou7 i oah8-teh;  17). tioh8 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, chiong Hek lang5, A-mou5-li7 lang5, Ka-lam5 lang5, Pi2-li7-se2 lang5, Hi-bi7 lang5, Ia5-pou3-su lang5, it-chin7 biat8 i;  18). bian2-tit in ka3-si7 lin2 oh8 it-chhe3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 in tui3 ti7 in e5 siong7-te3 sou2 kiaN5 e5, ti3-kau3 lin2 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.
	19). Li2 na7 ku2-ku2 ui5-khun3 chit8 e5 siaN5, kong-kek beh chhu2 i, chiu7 m7-thang eng7 pou2-thau5 phah-phaiN2 chhiu7-bak8; in-ui7 li2 thang chiah8 i e5 ke2-chi2, sou2-i2 m7-thang chho3 i; chhan5-ia2 e5 chhiu7-bak8 kiam2-si7 lang5, hou7 li2 ui5-khun3 mah?  20). Tok8-tok8 li2 sou2 bat m7-si7 thang choe3 chiah8-mih8 e5 chhiu7, thang chho3 lai5 hui2-hoai7 i, eng7 i lai5 choe3 kong-siaN5 e5 khi3-ku7, kong-kek hit-e5 kap li2 kau-chian3 e5 siaN5, kau3 kong-phoa3 i.

[21]	Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7, na7 tu2-tioh8 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 to2 ti7 chhan5-ia2, m7-chai si7 chi7-chui7 thai5-si2 e5;  2). li2 e5 tiuN2-lo2 kap sim2-phoaN3-koaN tioh8 chhut-lai5 niu5 i, tui3 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 hit-tah, tit8-kau3 si3-ui5 hiah e5 siaN5,  3). khoaN3 toh-loh8 chit8 e5 siaN5 li7-khui siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 te7-it kun7; chiu7 hit e5 siaN5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 tioh8 tui3 gu5-kun5 tiong chhu2 chit8-chiah be7-bat eng7 i lai5 choe3-kang, be7-bat koa3-taN e5 gu5-cheng2-a2;  4). hit e5 siaN5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 tioh8 khan gu5-cheng2-a2 kau3 u7 tng5-lau5-chui2 e5 soaN-kok, bo5 cheng3 bo5 choh-e5, ti7 hit e5 soaN-kok kong3-chih8 gu5-cheng2-a2 e5 am7-kun2.  5). Che3-si7 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 kiaN2-sun tioh8 kun7-oa2, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 keng2 in lai5 hok8-sai7 I, thok Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 chiok-hok; sou2 u7 saN-ko3, saN-phah e5 su7, long2 tioh8 chiau3 in e5 oe7 lai5 gi2-toan3.  6). Hit e5 siaN5 e5 cheng3 tiuN2-lo2, chiu7-si7 li7-khui siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 te7-it kun7-e5, tioh8 ti7 hit e5 soaN-kok tiong, sou2 kong3-chih8 am7-kun2 e5 gu5-cheng2-a2 e5 teng2-bin7 lai5 soe2 chhiu2;  7). ia7 beh in3 lai5 kong2, Goan2 e5 chhiu2 be7-bat lau5 chit e5 huih, goan2 e5 bak8-chiu ia7 be7-bat khoaN3-kiN3.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 sia3-bian2 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8, Li2 sou2 siok8-hoe5 e5, boh8-tit hou7 bo5-choe7 e5 huih kui ti7 Li2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8.  9). An2-ni lau5 hit e5 huih e5 choe7 kap i bo5 kan-siap8; an2-ni chiu7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tu5-khi3 lau5 bo5-choe7 e5 huih e5 choe7; si7 li2 u7 kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3-choe3 ho2-e5.
	10). Li2 chhut-khi3 kap li2 e5 tui3-tek8 kau-chian3 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 chiong in kau ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, li2 ia7 liah8 in khi3;  11). hit-si5 ti7 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, na7 khoaN3-kiN3 u7 bi2-lu2, li2 ia7 loan5-bou7 i, beh chhoa7 i choe3-bou2;  12). chiu7 thang chhoa7 kau3 li2 e5 ke, i chiu7 tioh8 thi3 thau5-mng5, siu chng2-kah;  13). thng3-khi3 i siu7-liah8 e5 si5 sou2 chheng7 e5 saN, tiam3 ti7 li2 e5 ke ai-khau3 pe7-bu2 chit8-geh8-jit8; jian5-au7 li2 thang kap i tang5-pang5, li2 choe3 i e5 tiong7-hu, i choe3 li2 e5 bou2.  14). Au7-lai5 li2 na7 bo5 hoaN-hi2 i, chiu7 tioh8 hou7 i chhut-chai7 i e5 i3-su3 chhut-khi3, koat-toan3 m7-thang boe7-chiN5, ia7 m7-thang tang3-choe3 lu2-pi7 khoan2-thai7 i; in-ui7 li2 i2-keng kap i seng5-chhin.
	15). Lang5 na7 u7 nng7 e5 bou2, chit8-e5 si7 i sou2 thiaN3-e5, chit8-e5 si7 i sou2 oan3-e5, long2 u7 ka7 i siN-kiaN2, chong2-si7 toa7-kiaN2 si7 sou2 oan3 e5 bou2 siN--e5;  16). kau3 hou7 kiaN2 seng5-chiap giap8 e5 jit8, m7-thang lip8 siu7-thiaN3 e5 bou2 siN e5 kiaN2 choe3 toa7-kiaN2, poaN5-ke3 chin e5 toa7-kiaN2, chiu7-si7 siu7-oan3 e5 bou2 e5 kiaN2;  17). chong2-si7 tioh8 jin7 sou2 oan3 e5 bou2 e5 kiaN2 choe3 toa7-kiaN2, chiong sou2 u7 e5 giap8 hou7 i siang-hun7; in-ui7 i si7 i khui3-lat8 e5 khi2-thau5, toa7-kiaN2 e5 beng5-hun7 si7 i-e5.
	18). Lang5 na7 u7 ban5-phe5 ngou2-gek8 e5 kiaN2, m7-thiaN in lau7-pe7 e5 oe7, a2-si7 lau7-bu2 e5 oe7, in sui-jian5 keng2-kai3 i, i iu5-goan5 m7-thiaN in;  19). i e5 pe7 kap i e5 bu2 tioh8 liah8 i, thoa i chhut, toa3-kau3 pun2-siaN5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 hia, chiu7-si7 i pun2 sou2-chai7 e5 siaN5-mng5;  20). ka7 hit e5 siaN5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 kong2, Goan2 chit e5 kiaN2 ban5-phe5 ngou2-gek8, m7-thiaN goan2 e5 oe7, lam7-sam2 khai-chiN5, tham-chiah8, houN3-chiu2;  21). hit e5 siaN5 e5 cheng3-lang5 chiu7 tioh8 eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 hou7 i si2; an2-ni, chiu7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tu5-khi3 hit e5 phaiN2.  I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 long2 beh thiaN-kiN3 lai5 kiaN.
	22). Lang5 na7 hoan7 eng-kai si2 e5 choe7, siu7 pan7-choe7 si2, li2 na7 tiau3 i ti7 chha5--nih,  23). i e5 sin-si m7-thang tiau3 ti7 chha5--nih ke3-mi5, tek-khak tioh8 ti7 hit-jit8 bai5-chong3 i, bian2-tit phah la5-sam5 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7; in-ui7 siu7 tiau3-si2 e5 lang5 si7 siu7 Siong7-te3 sou2 chiu3-chou2 e5.

[22]	Li2 na7 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 e5 gu5, a2-si7 iuN5, kiaN5 be5-lou7, li2 m7-thang tiN3 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3, li2 tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i to3-tng2--lai5 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 hia.  2). Li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 na7 li7-khui li2 hng7, a2-si7 li2 m7-bat i, chiu7 tioh8 khan kau3 li2 e5 chhu3, lau5 ti7 li2 hia, theng3-hau7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 lai5 chhe7, li2 chiah heng5 i.  3). Li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 e5 lu5, a2-si7 i e5 saN, bo5-lun7 i sit-loh8 sim2-mih8, i sit-loh8, li2 sou2 khioh-tioh8 e5, long2 tioh8 an2-ni kiaN5, m7-thang tiN3-choe3 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3.  4). Li2 na7 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 e5 lu5, a2-si7 gu5, poah8-to2 ti7 lou7--nih, m7-thang tiN3-choe3 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3, tek-khak tioh8 pang-chan7 i, hu5 i khi2--lai5.
	5). Hu7-jin5-lang5 m7-thang chheng7 ta-pou-lang5 sou2 chheng7 e5, ta-pou-lang5 ia7 m7-thang chheng7 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 saN; in-ui7 kiN3-na7 an2-ni kiaN5 e5, si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 iam3-ouN3 e5.
	6). Li2 na7 ti7 lou7--nih tu2-tioh8 chiau2-siu7, hek8-si7 ti7 chhiu7--nih, hek8-si7 ti7 toe7--nih, lai7-bin7 u7 chiau2-a2-kiaN2, a2-si7 chiau2-nng7, chiau2-bu2 aN3 chiau2-kiaN2, a2-si7 pu7-nng7, li2 m7-thang liah8 chiau2-kiaN2 soa3 liah8 chiau2-bu2;  7). tek-khak tioh8 pang3 chiau2-bu2 khi3, chong2-si7 chiau2-a2-kiaN2 li2 thang liah8--khi3; an2-ni li2 chiu7 thang hiong2-siu7 hok-khi3 koh chiah8 tng5 he3-siu7.
	8). Li2 na7 khi2 sin chhu3, tioh8 choe3 lan5-kan ti7 chhu3-teng2, bian2-tit lang5 tui3 hia poah8--loh8-lai5; lau5-huih e5 choe7 chiu7 kui ti7 li2 e5 chhu3.
	9). M7-thang eng7 nng7-iuN7 e5 cheng2-chi2 ia7 ti7 li2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5; kiaN-liau2 choe3 chit8-e7 bo5--khi3, chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 ia7 e5 cheng2-chi2 kiat-sit8-e5, kap li2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 kiat-sit8-e5, long2 bo5 thang su-khia eng7.
	10). M7-thang eng7 gu5 kap lu5 saN-kap loe5-chhan5.  11). M7-thang chheng7 chham-chhap e5 pou3-liau7, iuN5-mng5 kap iu3-toe7 hap8-chit--e5.
	12). Li2 sou2 moa e5 saN tioh8 ti7 i e5 si3-ui5 choe3 chhiu.
	13). Lang5 na7 chhoa7-bou2, kap i tang5-pang5,  14). au7-lai5 oan3-hun7 i, hui2-pong3 i phaiN2-tai7, phah-phaiN2 i e5 mia5, kong2, Goa2 chhoa7 chit e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, kap i tang5-pang5, khoaN3 i bo5 chai7-sek-lu2 e5 pin5-ku3;  15). cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 pe7-bu2 tioh8 theh8 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chai7-sek-lu2 e5 pin5-ku3 chhut-lai5, toa3 kau3 i pun2 siaN5-mng5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 hia;  16). cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 lau7-pe7 tioh8 tui3 tiuN2-lo2 kong2, Goa2 eng7 goa2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 hou7 chit e5 lang5 choe3-bou2, i oan3-hun7 i;  17). khoaN3 ah, i hui2-pong3 i phaiN2-tai7, kong2, Goa2 khoaN3 li2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 bo5 chai7-sek-lu2 e5 pin5-ku3; ki5-sit8 chit-e5 si7 goa2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chai7-sek-lu2 e5 pin5-ku3.  Pe7-bu2 chiu7 chiong hit-e5 pou3 pai5 ti7 pun2-siaN5 tiuN2-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  18). Hit e5 siaN5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 tioh8 liah8 hit e5 lang5 lai5 chek-hoat8 i;  19). ia7 tioh8 hoat8 i chit8-pah gun5, hou7 cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 lau7-pe7; in-ui7 i u7 ka-bu5 I2-sek-liat8 chai7-sek-lu2 e5 phaiN2-mia5; cha-bou2-kiaN2 iu5-goan5 choe3 i e5 bou2, chit8-si3-lang5 m7-thang li5-chhut i.  20). Chong2-si7 chit e5 su7 na7 si7 chin-e5, cha-bou2-kiaN2 bo5 chai7-sek-lu2 e5 pin5-ku3;  21). in tioh8 liah8 hit e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kau3 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 chhu3 e5 mng5-khau2, i pun2-siaN5 e5 lang5 tioh8 eng7 chioh8-thau5 ka7 i tim3-si2; in-ui7 i ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong kiaN5 kian3-siau3 e5 su7, ti7 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke kiaN5 im5-loan7; an2-ni chiu7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tu5--khi3 hit e5 phaiN2.
	22). Na7 tu2-tioh8 u7 lang5 kap ke3 tiong7-hu e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 tang5-pang5, kan-hu kap hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 long2 tioh8 hou7 in si2; an2-ni chiu7 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiong-kan tu5--khi3 hit e5 phaiN2.
	23). Na7 u7 cha-bou2-kiaN2, si7 chai7-sek-lu2 e5, i2-keng choe3 lang5 tiaN7-tioh8, u7 lang5 ti7 siaN5-lai7 tu2-tioh8 i, kap i tang5-pang5;  24). chiu7 lin2 tioh8 liah8 chi2 nng7-lang5 chhut-khi3 kau3 hit e5 siaN5-mng5, eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3-si2 in; cha-bou2-kiaN2, in-ui7 i ti7 siaN5-lai7 iau2-ku2 bo5 hau2-kiu3; ta-pou-lang5, in-ui7 i leng5-jiok8 i e5 chhu3-piN e5 bou2; an2-ni chiu7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tu5--khi3 hit e5 phaiN2.
	25). Chong2-si7 na7 u7 lang5 ti7 chhan5-ia2 tu2-tioh8 i2-keng pheng3 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, hit-lang5 ka7 i kiong5-kan; kan-ta hit-e5 ka7 i kiong5-kan e5 lang5 tioh8 si2;  26). chong2-si7 hit e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 li2 m7-thang chaiN2-iuN7 pan7 i; in-ui7 hit e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 bo5 eng-kai si2 e5 su7; chit e5 tai7-chi3 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek i e5 chhu3-piN, thai5-si2 i chit8-iuN7;  27). in-ui7 i ti7 chhan5-ia2 tu2-tioh8 i, hit-e5 choe3-lang5 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 hau2-kiu3, ia7 bo5 lang5 kiu3 i.
	28). Na7 ta-pou-lang5 tu2-tioh8 be7 phoe3 lang5 e5 chai7-sek-lu2, khiN5 i kap i su-thong, bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3,  29). chiu7 hit-e5 kap i su-thong e5 lang5, tioh8 theh8 gou7-chap8 e5 gun5, hou7 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 e5 lau7-pe7, in-ui7 i i2-keng leng5-jiok8 i; chiu7 tioh8 chhoa7 i choe3 bou2, chit8-si3-lang5 m7-thang li5 i.
	30). Lang5 m7-thang chhoa7 lau7-pe7 e5 au7-bou2 choe3-bou2, m7-thang hian-khui i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 saN-a2-ku.

[23]	KiN3-na7 goa7-sin7 siu7-siong-e5, a2-si7 siu7 iam-koah-e5, m7-thang jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7.
	2). Su-thong lai5 siN e5 kiaN2 m7-thang jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7; sui-jian5 kau3 i e5 chap8-tai7, ia7 m7-thang jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7.
	3). A-bun5 lang5 a2-si7 Mou5-ap lang5, m7-thang jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7; sui-jian5 kau3 in e5 chap8-tai7, eng2-oan2 boe7 thang jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7;  4). in-ui7 lin2 chhut Ai-kip8 e5 si5, in bo5 eng7 chiah8-mih8 kap chui2, ti7 lou7--nih ngia5-chih lin2; koh in-ui7 in tui3-tek8 lin2, chhiaN3 Bi2-sou2-pho-tai7-bi2 e5 Pi3-toat8 lang5, Pi2-jiN2 e5 kiaN2, Pa-lan5 lai5 chiu3-chou2 lin2.  5). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 m7-thiaN Pa-lan5; Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 hou7 hit e5 chiu3-chou2 pian3-choe3 chiok-hok li2; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 thiaN3 li2.  6). Li2 chit8-si3-lang5 kau3 eng2-oan2 m7-thang ka7 in tou5-bou5 peng5-an kap hok-khi3.
	7). M7-thang oan3-hun7 I2-tong lang5, in-ui7 i si7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7; m7-thang oan3-hun7 Ai-kip8 lang5, in-ui7 lin2 bat chhut-goa7 ti7-hia;  8). in sou2 siN e5 kiaN2-sun kau3 te7-saN tai7 thang jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7.
	9). Li2 e5 kun-tui7 chhut-khi3 kong-kek li2 e5 tui3-tek8, ti7 iaN5-poaN5 tioh8 ka-ki7 kim3-kai3 it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2-su7.  10). Lin2 tiong-kan na7 u7 lang5, ti7 mi5-si5 sou2 tu2-tioh8-e5, lai5 bak bo5 chheng-khi3, i chiu7 tioh8 chhut-khi3 kau3 iaN5-goa7, m7-thang jip8 iaN5-lai7;  11). kau3 beh am3 e5 si5, i tioh8 eng7 chui2 soe2, kau3 jit8-loh8 chiah thang jip8 iaN5.  12). Li2 ti7 iaN5-goa7 keng2 chit8-ui7 thang chhut-khi3 kau3 goa7-bin7 e5 sou2-chai7;  13). ti7 li2 e5 khi3-ku7-lai7 tioh8 u7 thuh-a2; li2 ti7 goa7-bin7 chhut-kiong e5 si5, tioh8 eng7 i kut8 thou5, chiah oat8-tng2-sin, kham3 li2 sou2 pang3 e5;  14). in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 si3-koe3 kiaN5 ti7 li2 e5 iaN5-lai7, beh chin2-kiu3 li2, chiong li2 e5 tui3-tek8 kau hou7 li2; sou2-i2 li2 e5 iaN5-poaN5 eng-kai tioh8 u7 seng3-kiat; bian2-tit I khoaN3-kiN3 li2 tiong-kan u7 u3-oe3, chiu7 li7-khui li2.
	15). Na7 u7 lou5-pok8 thoat-li7 i e5 chu2-lang5, chau2 kau3 li2 hia, li2 m7-thang chiong i kau hou7 i e5 chu2-lang5;  16). i beh kap li2 tiam3, khia7 li2 tiong-kan, ti7 i sou2 keng2 li2 chit8 e5 siaN5-mng5-lai7 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 i sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5; li2 m7-thang khi-hu7 i.
	17). I2-sek-liat8 e5 lu2-chu2-tiong m7-thang u7 ki7-lu2.
	I2-sek-liat8 e5 lam5-chu2-tiong m7-thang u7 loan5-tong5.  18). Chhiong-ki sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 chiN5, a2-si7 kau2-lui7 e5 kang-chiN5, li2 m7-thang toa3 jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 tian7 lai5 sia7-goan7; in-ui7 chi2 nng7-hang7 long2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 iam3-ouN3 e5.
	19). Li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 hek8-si7 tui3 li2 chioh chiN5-gun5, a2-si7 chioh chiah8-mih8, chioh kiN3-na7 oe7 siN li7-sek e5 mih8, li2 long2 m7-thang theh8 i e5 li7-sek;  20). li2 chioh goa7-chok8 e5 lang5, thang theh8 i e5 li7-sek, chong2-si7 chioh li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 chiu7 m7-thang theh8 i e5 li7-sek; thang hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 ti7 li2 sou2 khi3 beh tit-tioh8 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7, ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, su3-hok li2.
	21). Li2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 he7-goan7, sia7 i m7-thang ian5-chhian5; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 tek-khak beh tui3 li2 tho2; li2 na7 bo5 sia7, chiu7 u7 choe7;  22). li2 na7 bo5 he7-goan7, chiu7 bo5 choe7.  23). KiN3-na7 tui3 li2 e5 chhui3 sou2 chhut e5, chiau3 li2 i2-keng he7-goan7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 lai5 kam-sim hian3 e5, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 chhui3 sou2 in2, li2 tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 i.
	24). Li2 jip8 li2 e5 chhu3-piN e5 phu5-to5-hng5, thang chhut-chai7 i3-su3 chiah8 phu5-to5 kau3 pa2; chong2-si7 m7-thang toe2 ti7 li2 e5 khi3-ku7-lai7.
	25). Li2 jip8 li2 e5 chhu3-piN iau2-be7 koah e5 ngou2-kok tiong, thang eng7 chhiu2 tiah i e5 siu7; chong2-si7 m7-thang eng7 liam5-a2 koah li2 e5 chhu3-piN e5 gou7-kak.

[24]	Lang5 na7 chhoa7-bou2, jian5-au7 khoaN3 i e5 bou2 m7 teng3-i3, in-ui7 i chai i u7 bo5 hap8-gi5 e5 su7, chiu7 thang sia2 li5-su hou7 i, kau i e5 chhiu2, chhe i li7-khui i e5 ke.  2). Hu7-jin5-lang5 li7-khui i e5 ke liau2-au7, thang khi3 ke3 pat8-lang5.  3). Na7 si7 au7 e5 tiong7-hu oan3-hun7 i, ia7 sia2 li5-su kau i e5 chhiu2, kah i li7-khui i e5 ke, a2-si7 i au7 e5 tiong7-hu chhoa7 i choe3-bou2 chiu7 si2;  4). chiu7 hit-e5 cheng5 e5 tiong7-hu i2-keng kah i khi3--e5, boe7-tit-thang ti7 i phah la5-sam5 i2-au7, koh chhoa7 i choe3-bou2; in-ui7 che si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 iam3-ouN3-e5; m7-thang hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7 lai5 hoan7-choe7.
	5). Sin chhoa7-bou2 e5 lang5 m7-thang khi3 kau-chian3, ia7 m7-thang kau-tai3 i pan7-li2 sim2-mih8 su7; thang hou7 i ti7 ke-lai7 chheng-han5 chit8-ni5, thang hou7 i sou2 chhoa7 e5 bou2 hoaN-hi2.  6). M7-thang eng7 lang5 e5 chioh8-bo7, a2-si7 chioh8-bo7 e5 teng2-tun2, choe3 chun2-tng3; in-ui7 che si7 eng7 lang5 e5 siN3-mia7 choe3 chun2-tng3.
	7). Na7 tu2-tioh8 lang5 koai2 I2-sek-liat8-tiong chit8-e5 hiaN-ti7, khoan2-thai7 i choe3 lou5-chai5, a2-si7 boe7 i, hit e5 koai2-kun3 chiu7 tioh8 hou7 i si2; an2-ni, chiu7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tu5--khi3 hit e5 phaiN2.
	8). Thai2-ko e5 phaiN2 cheng3-thau5, li2 tioh8 chin soe3-ji7; che3-si Li7-bi7 lang5 it-chhe3 sou2 ka3-si7 lin2-e5, tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni lai5 kiaN5; goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 in-e5, lin2 tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5;  9). cha2 chhut Ai-kip8 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 ti7 lou7-nih tui3 Bi2-li7-am3 sou2-kiaN5-e5, li2 tioh8 ki3-tit.
	10). Li2 bo5-lun7 eng7 sim2-mih8 chioh chhu3-piN, m7-thang jip8 i e5 ke theh8 chun2-tng3,  11). li2 tioh8 khia7 ti7 goa7-bin7, theng3-hau7 ka7 li2 chioh e5 lang5 theh8 chun2-tng3 chhut-lai5 hou7 li2;  12). hit lang5 na7 si7 song3-hiong, li2 m7-thang lau5 i e5 chun2-tng3 ke3-mi5;  13). jit8-loh8 e5 si5, tek-khak tioh8 eng7 hit e5 chun2-tng3 heng5 i, hou7 i eng7 i e5 saN kah teh khun3; i chiu7 ka7 li2 chiok-hok; che ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, beh sng3-choe3 li2 e5 gi7.
	14). Khun3-khou2 song3-hiong e5 chhiaN3-kang lang5, bo5-lun7 si7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7, a2-si7 chhut-goa7 lang5 tiam3 ti7 li2 e5 toe7, ti7 li2 e5 siaN5-mng5-lai7 e5, li2 m7-thang khi-hu7 i;  15). i e5 kang-chiN5 li2 hit-jit8 tioh8 hou7 i, m7-thang theng3-hau7 kau3 jit8-loh8-liau2; in-ui7 i song3-hiong, koa3-sim ti7 hit-e5; kiaN-liau2 i in-ui7 li2 lai5 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa au5-kio3, li2 chiu7 u7 choe7.
	16). M7-thang in-ui7 kiaN2 lai5 hou7 lau7-pe7 si2, ia7 m7-thang in-ui7 lau7-pe7 lai5 hou7 kiaN2 si2; tak8-lang5 tioh8 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 choe7 lai5 si2.
	17). Li2 sim2-phoaN3, m7-thang oan-ong2 chhut-goa7 lang5 kap bo5-pe7 e5 kiaN2, ia7 m7-thang theh8 koaN2-hu7 e5 i-chiuN5 choe3 chun2-tng3;  18). li2 tioh8 ki3-tit li2 ti7 Ai-kip8 bat choe3 lou5-chai5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kiu3-siok8 li2 tui3 hia chhut; sou2-i2 goa2 beng7-leng7 li2 tioh8 an2-ni kiaN5.
	19). Li2 ti7 chhan5--nih siu-koah gou7-kak, na7 boe7-ki3-tit chit8-sok ti7 chhan5--nih, m7-thang koh oat--khi3 theh8, tioh8 lau5 hou7 chhut-goa7 lang5 kap kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7, ti3-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, su3-hok li2.  20). Li2 phah li2 e5 kaN-na2-chhiu7 i2-au7 m7-thang koh sun5 hiah e5 chhiu7-ki; tioh8 lau5 hou7 chhut-goa7 lang5 kap kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7.  21). Li2 ban2 li2 e5 phu5-to5, sou2-chhun-e5 m7-thang koh ban2, tioh8 lau5 hou7 chhut-goa7 lang5, kap kou-ji5, koaN2-hu7;  22). li2 ia7 tioh8 ki3-tit li2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 bat choe3 lou5-chai5; sou2-i2 goa2 beng7-leng7 li2 tioh8 an2-ni kiaN5.

[25]	Lang5 na7 u7 oan-ke lai5 tui3-sin3, koaN-hu2 phoaN3-toan3 i, chiu7 tioh8 teng7 gi7-lang5 choe3-gi7, teng7 phaiN2-lang5 choe3-phaiN2.  2). PhaiN2-lang5 na7 eng-kai siu7-phah, sim2-phoaN3-koaN tioh8 hou7 i phak ti7 toe7--nih, ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, chiau3 i e5 choe7, chiau3 siau3-giah8 phah i;  3). tok8-tok8 thang phah i si3-chap8-e7, m7-thang ke3 siau3-giah8; na7 ke3 siau3-giah8, phah i khah-choe7-e7, chiu7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 hou7 li2 khoaN3-khin.
	4). Gu5 teh lun2 gou7-kak, m7-thang lang2 i e5 chhui3.
	5). HiaN-ti7 saN-kap khia7-khi2, ki5-tiong na7 chit8-e5 si2 bo5 kiaN2, si2-lang5 e5 bou2 m7-thang ke3 goa7-lang5, i tiong7-hu e5 sio2-ti7 tioh8 jip8-khi3 i hia, chhoa7 i choe3-bou2, lai5 chin7 sio2-chek e5 pun2-hun7;  6). i sou2 siN e5 toa7-kiaN2, tioh8 soa3-chiap si2 e5 hiaN e5 beng5-hun7, bian2-tit i e5 mia5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8-tiong siau-biat8.  7). Hit-lang5 na7 m7 goan7-i3 chhoa7 i e5 hiaN-so2, i e5 hiaN-so2 chiu7 tioh8 kau3 siaN5-mng5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 hia kong2, Goa2 e5 tiong7-hu e5 sio2-ti7 m7-kheng2 ti7 I2-sek-liat8-tiong ka7 i e5 hiaN thoan5 chit8 e5 mia5-ji7, bo5 beh ka7 goa2 chin7 sio2-chek e5 pun2-hun7.  8). I siaN5-lai7 e5 tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 tioh8 kio3 i lai5, ka7 i kong2; i na7 chip-i3 kong2, Goa2 bo5 beh chhoa7 i;  9). i e5 hiaN-so2 chiu7 tioh8 ti7 tiuN2-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chiu7-kun7 i, thng3 hit-lang5 kha--nih e5 oe5, phui3-noa7 ti7 i e5 bin7, kong2, KiN3-na7 bo5 beh ui7-tioh8 hiaN kian3-lip8 i e5 ke e5, tioh8 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 i;  10). ti7 I2-sek-liat8-tiong, i e5 mia5 beh chheng choe3 thng3-oe5--e5 e5 ke.
	11). Na7 u7 nng7-lang5 saN-phah, ki5-tiong chit8-lang5 e5 bou2 kun7-oa2 lai5, beh kiu3 i e5 tiong7-hu thoat-li7 phah i e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, chhun-chhiu2 khiN5-tiau5 hit-lang5 e5 e7-the2;  12). chiu7 tioh8 cham7-tng7 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 chhiu2, bak8-chiu m7-thang kho2-lin5 i.
	13). Li2 e5 te7-a2-lai7 m7-thang u7 nng7-iuN7 e5 pheng5-chi2, u7-liap8 toa7, u7-liap8 soe3;  14). chhu3-lai7 m7-thang u7 nng7-iuN7 e5 chin, tau2, u7-e5 toa7, u7-e5 soe3;  15). tioh8 eng7 chun2-chun2 kong-peng5 e5 pheng5-chi2, chun2-chun2 kong-peng5 e5 chin, tau2; thang hou7 li2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 e5 toe7 chiah8 tng5 he3-siu7;  16). in-ui7 kiN3-na7 kiaN5 chiah e5 tai7-chi3, kap kiaN5 put-gi7 e5, long2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 iam3-ouN3-e5.
	17). Li2 tioh8 ki3-tit lin2 chhut Ai-kip8 e5 si5, A-ma2-lek8 lang5 ti7 lou7--nih sou2 khoan2-thai7 li2 e5;  18). i ti7 lou7--nih tu2-tioh8 li2, tng li2 khun3-khou2 ia3-sian7 e5 si5, u7 chaiN2-iuN7 phah li2 au7-tui7, chiu7-si7 ti7 li2 au7-bin7 e5 loan2-jiok8 e5; i ia7 bo5 kiaN-ui3 Siong7-te3.  19). Sou2-i2 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 kiu3 li2 thoat-li7 si3-ui5 long2-chong2 e5 tui3-tek8, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7, tit-tioh8 peng5-an, hit-si5 li2 tioh8 chiong A-ma2-lek8 e5 mia5-ji7, tui3 thiN-e7 chhat-siau, m7-thang boe7-ki3-tit.

[26]	Li2 i2-keng kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7, seng5-chiap lai5 khia7-khi2 i,  2). chiu7 tioh8 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7, chiong sou2 siu tak8-hang7 khi2-thau5-sek8 e5 thou2-san2, theh8 tam7-poh8, he7 ti7 kheng--nih, khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh keng2 an-ti3 I e5 mia5 e5 sou2-chai7;  3). tioh8 khi3 kiN3 tng-si5 choe3 che3-si-e5, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kong2-beng5 goa2 i2-keng kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 lan2 e5 liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 siuN2-su3 lan2 e5 toe7.  4). Che3-si chiu7 tui3 li2 e5 chhiu2 chih hit-kheng, lai5 he7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 toaN5-cheng5.  5). Li2 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2, goa2 e5 chou2 si7 chit8-e5 teh-beh si2 e5 A-lan5 lang5, loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8 kia3-kha ti7-hia, lang5-giah8 chio2-chio2; ti7-hia chiaN5-choe3 chit8-kok toa7 koh kiong5, lang5-giah8 koh choe7.  6). Ai-kip8 lang5 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 goan2, khou2-chhou2 goan2, eng7 khou2-kang kah goan2 choe3;  7). tui3 hit-tiap8 goan2 ai-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa goan2 liat8-chou2 e5 Siong7-te3, Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN goan2 e5 siaN, khoaN3-kiN3 goan2 e5 khou2-chhou2, goan2 e5 tioh8-boa5, goan2 e5 ap-pek;  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, kap chhun-chhut e5 chhiu2-kut, kap toa7 thang kiaN e5 su7, kap sin5-jiah, ki5-su7, chhoa7 goan2 chhut Ai-kip8,  9). koh chhoa7 goan2 kau3 chit sou2-chai7, eng7 chit e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 goan2, chiu7-si7 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7.  10). KhoaN3 ah, chit e5 toe7 khi2-thau5-sek8 e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 sou2 siuN2-su3 goa2 e5, goa2 taN i2-keng toa3-lai5.  Au7-lai5 li2 tioh8 chiong i he7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 keng3-pai3 I.  11). Li2 kap Li7-bi7 lang5, i2-kip8 lin2 tiong-kan e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, tioh8 in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 kap li2 e5 ke-koan3 it-chhe3 e5 hok-hun7 lai5 hoaN-hi2.
	12). Tak8-pai2 kau3 te7-saN ni5, chiu7-si7 chap8-hun7 thiu chit8-hun7 e5 ni5, li2 thiu it-chhe3 e5 thou2-san2 chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7, pun hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5, kap chhut-goa7 lang5, kap kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7, hou7 in ti7 li2 e5 siaN5-mng5, thang tit-tioh8 chiah8-pa2.  13). Li2 koh tioh8 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2, Goa2 i2-keng tui3 goa2 e5 ke theh8-chhut seng3-mih8, soa3 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5 kap chhut-goa7 lang5, kap kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7, si7 chiau3 li2 sou2 beng7-leng7 goa2 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7; Li2 e5 kai3-beng7 goa2 long2 bo5 hoan7-tioh8, ia7 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit;  14). ku-song e5 si5, goa2 be7-bat chiah8 i, bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 si5, goa2 be7-bat theh8--khi2-lai5, ia7 bo5 eng7 i choe3 si2-lang5 e5 lou7-eng7; goa2 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa goa2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, long2 chiau3 Li2 it-chhe3 sou2 beng7-leng7 goa2 e5 lai5 kiaN5.  15). Kiu5 Li2 tui3 thiN--nih, tui3 Li2 khia7-khi2 e5 seng3-sou2, aN3-loh8 khoaN3, su3-hok Li2 e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8, kap Li2 sou2 siuN2-su3 goan2 e5 toe7, chiau3 Li2 sou2 tui3 goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 e5, chiu7-si7 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7.
	16). Kin-a2-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beng7-leng7 li2 kiaN5 chiah e5 lut8-le7 hoat-tou7; sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 chin7-sim chin7-seng3 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 i;  17). kin-a2-jit8 li2 seng5-jin7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 li2 e5 Siong7-te3, un2 beh kiaN5 I e5 to7-lou7, siu2 I e5 lut8-le7, kai3-beng7, hoat-tou7, thiaN-than3 I e5 oe7.  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa kin-a2-jit8 ia7 seng5-jin7 li2 choe3 I ka-ki7 tek8-piat8 e5 peh-siN3, chiau3 I sou2 eng3-un2 li2 e5, hou7 li2 siu2 I it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7;  19). koh hou7 li2 tui3 ti7 eng5-kng, mia5-siaN, chun-kui3, poaN5-ke3 I sou2 chhong3-cho7 ban7-kok e5 peh-siN3; hou7 li2 kui ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, choe3 seng3-kiat e5 peh-siN3, chiau3 I sou2 kong2 e5.

[27]	Mou5-se kap I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 tiuN2-lo2 beng7-leng7 peh-siN3 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 siu2 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7.  2). Lin2 ke3 Iok-tan3, kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7, hit-jit8 tioh8 khia7 kui2-te3 toa7-chioh8, eng7 he boah i;  3). li2 i2-keng ke3--khi3, tioh8 sia2 chit e5 lut8-hoat it-chhe3 e5 oe7 ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7, thang hou7 li2 jip8-khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 liat8-chou2 e5 Siong7-te3 sou2 eng3-un2 li2 e5.  4).  Lin2 i2-keng ke3 Iok-tan3, chiu7 tioh8 ti7 I2-pa-lou7 soaN khia7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 hiah e5 chioh8, eng7 he boah i.  5). Ti7-hia tioh8 ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5, chiu7-si7 chioh8 e5 toaN5, ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7 m7-thang tang7-tioh8 thih-khi3;  6). tioh8 eng7 bo5 ke3-phah e5 chioh8 khi2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 toaN5;  7). ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7 tioh8 hian3 sio-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3; koh tioh8 hian3 sia7-un-che3; ia7 ti7-hia chiah8, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 hoaN-hi2.  8). Li2 tioh8 chiong chit e5 lut8-hoat it-chhe3 e5 oe7, sia2-beng5 ti7 hiah e5 chioh8--nih.
	9). Mou5-se kap che3-si Li7-bi7 lang5, hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 kong2, I2-sek-liat8 ah, tioh8 cheng7-cheng7 lai5 thiaN; kin-a2-jit8 li2 chiaN5-choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 peh-siN3;  10). sou2-i2 tioh8 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, kiaN5 I e5 kai3-beng7 lut8-le7, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5.
	11). Tng hit-jit8 Mou5-se beng7-leng7 peh-siN3 kong2,  12). Lin2 ke3 Iok-tan3 liau2-au7, Se-bian7, Li7-bi7, Iu5-tai7, I2-sat-ka, Iok-sek, Pian7-nga2-bin2, chiah e5 chi-phai3, tioh8 khia7 ti7 Ki-li7-sim soaN lai5 chiok-hok peh-siN3;  13). Liu5-pian7, Ka-tek, A-siat, Se-pou3-lun5, Tan3, Na2-hut-tha-li7, chiah e5 chi-phai3, tioh8 khia7 ti7 I2-pa-lou7 soaN lai5 soan-pou3 chiu3-chou2.  14). Li7-bi7 lang5 tioh8 toa7-siaN tui3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 kong2;
	15). KiN3-na7 lang5 che3-cho7 ngou2-siong7, khek--e5, a2-si7 chu3--e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 iam3-ouN3-e5, chiu7-si7 sai-hu7 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 e5, chhai7 ti7 am3-chiN7 e5 sou2-chai7, hit-lang5 tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 in3 kong2, A-beng7.
	16). KhoaN3-khin lau7-pe7 a2-si7 lau7-bu2 e5, tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	17). I5-soa2 chhu3-piN e5 kai3-chi2 e5, tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	18). Hou7 chhiN-mi5 lang5 kiaN5 m7-tioh8 lou7 e5, tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	19). Sim2-phoaN3 lai5 oan-ong2 chhut-goa7 lang5 kap kou-ji5 koaN2-hu7 e5, tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	20). Kap lau7-pe7 e5 au7-bou2 tang5-pang5 e5 tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2, in-ui7 i u7 hian-khui i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 saN-a2-ku.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	21). Bo5-lun7 kap sim2-mih8 siu3 kau-hap8-e5 tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	22). Lang5 kap siang5-pe7 e5 chi2-be7, a2-si7 siang5-bu2 e5 chi2-be7, tang5-pang5, hit-lang5 tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	23). Kap tiuN7-m2 tang5-pang5-e5 tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2. Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	24). Am3-chiN7 phah-si2 chhu3-piN e5 tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	25). Siu7 pou3-lou7 lai5 hai7-si2 bo5-choe7 e5 lang5 e5 tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.
	26). Bo5 kian-siu2 chiah e5 lut8-hoat e5 oe7 lai5 kiaN5-e5 tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  Peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 kong2, A-beng7.

[28]	Li2 na7 ti3-i3 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, siu2 I it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7 lai5 kiaN5 i, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh hou7 li2 poaN5-ke3 thiN-e7 ban7-kok;  2). li2 na7 thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, chiu7 chiah-e5 sou2 chiok-hok-e5 beh jip li2, beh kau3 ti7 li2;  3). li2 ti7 siaN5-lai7 beh tit-tioh8 hok-khi3, ti7 chhan5--nih beh tit-tioh8 hok-khi3;  4). li2 e5 sin-khu sou2-siN-e5, li2 e5 thou2-toe7 sou2-chhut-e5, li2 e5 cheng-siN sou2-chhut-e5, i2-kip8 gu5 e5 gu5-a2-kiaN2, iuN5 e5 iuN5-a2-kiaN2, long2 beh tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  5). Li2 e5 kheng-a2 kap li2 chhiau-mi7 e5 khi3-ku7, long2 beh tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  6). Li2 jip8-lai5 beh tit-tioh8 hok-khi3; chhut-khi3 ia7 beh tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  7). Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 khi2-lai5 kong-kek li2 e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 in thai5-su ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; in tui3 chit8 tiau5 lou7 chhut-lai5 kong-kek li2, beh ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tui3 chhit tiau5 lou7 lai5 chau2.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh beng7-leng7 hok-khi3 hou7 li2, ti7 li2 e5 chhek-chhng, kap li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7; ia7 beh su3-hok li2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7.  9). Li2 na7 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 kai3-beng7, kiaN5 I e5 to7-lou7, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh siat-lip8 li2 choe3 I ka-ki7 seng3 e5 peh-siN3, chiau3 I sou2 tui3 li2 chiu3-choa7 e5;  10). thiN-e7 ban7 peh-siN3 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 siok8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5-e7, chiu7 beh kiaN-ui3 li2.  11). Li2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 toe7, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 li2 e5 seng-khu sou2-siN--e5, cheng-siN sou2-chhut e5, thou2-toe7 sou2-chhut--e5, chhiong-chiok u7 chhun.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ka7 li2 khui I thiN--nih po2-poe3 e5 khou3-pang5, loh8 kip8-si5 e5 hou7 ti7 li2 e5 toe7, ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7 su3-hok li2; li2 beh chioh hou7 choe7-choe7 kok, ia7 li2 m7-bian2 chioh.  13-14). Li2 na7 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 kai3-beng7, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 i, bo5 phian-cho2, bo5 phian-iu7, lai5 oai-chhoah8 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 chiah e5 oe7, khi3 than3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 lai5 hok8-sai7 i, Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 beh hou7 li2 choe3-thau5, bo5 choe3-be2; li2 beh tiam3 ti7 teng2-bin7, bo5 tiam3 ti7 e7-bin7.
	15). Li2 na7 bo5 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, bo5 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 I it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, lut8-le7, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5, chiah e5 chiu3-chou2 chiu7 beh jip-tioh8 li2, beh kau3 ti7 li2.  16). Ti7 siaN5-lai7 li2 beh siu7 chiu3-chou2; ti7 chhan5--nih li2 ia7 beh siu7 chiu3-chou2.  17). Li2 e5 kheng-a2 kap li2 chhiau-mi7 e5 khi3-ku7, long2 beh siu7 chiu3-chou2.  18). Li2 e5 seng-khu sou2 siN--e5, li2 e5 toe7 sou2-chhut--e5, i2-kip8 gu5 e5 gu5-a2-kiaN2, iuN5 e5 iuN5-a2-kiaN2, long2 beh siu7 chiu3-chou2.  19). Li2 jip8-lai5 beh siu7 chiu3-chou2; chhut-khi3 ia7 beh siu7 chiu3-chou2.  20). In-ui7 li2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 phaiN2 lai5 khi3-sak goa2, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, hou7 chiu3-chou2, jiau2-loan7, chek-hoat8, kau3 ti7 li2, tit8-kau3 li2 siu7 hui2-biat8, kin2-kin2 biat8-bo5.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 un-ek8 tiN5 li2, kau3 I biat8-bo5 li2 ti7 li2 sou2 jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7.  22). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh eng7 siau-san2, jiat8-piN7, hoat-iam7, tok8-jiat8, to-kiam3, kou-ta5, hiu2-noa7, kong-kek li2; chiah-e5 long2 beh tui-jip li2, kau3 li2 biat8-bo5.  23). Li2 thau5-khak-teng2 e5 thiN beh piN3-choe3 tang5, kha-e7 e5 toe7 beh piN3-choe3 thih.  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 li2 toe7-chiuN7 e5 hou7 piN3 thou5-hun2, piN3 soa; I beh tui3 thiN loh8 ti7 li2, kau3 li2 biat8-bo5.  25). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 li2 thai5-su ti7 li2 tui3-tek8 e5 bin7-cheng5; li2 tui3 chit8 tiau5 lou7 chhut-khi3 ti2-tek8 in, beh ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 tui3 chhit tiau5 lou7 lai5 to5-chau2; li2 beh ti7 thiN-e7 ban7-kok-tiong liu5-lok8.  26). Li2 e5 sin-si beh hou7 khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2 kap toe7-chiuN7 e5 chau2-siu3 choe3 chiah8-mih8, ia7 bo5 lang5 koaN2 i.  27). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh eng7 Ai-kip8 e5 iong, ti7-chhng, sian2, koe3, boe7 i--tit-e5, lai5 phah li2.  28). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh eng7 tian-kong5, chhiN-mi5, sim e5 kiaN-hiaN5 phah li2;  29). li2 beh ti7 jit8-tiong-tau3 si3-koe3 bong, chhin-chhiuN7 chhiN-mi5 e5 am3-bong-sa; li2 e5 lou7 boe7 heng-thong, siong5-siong5 tu2-tioh8 che3-ap, chhiuN2-toat8, bo5 lang5 chin2-kiu3 li2.  30). Li2 beh pheng3-tiaN7 bou2, pat8-lang5 kap i tang5-pang5; li2 beh khi2-chhu3, bo5 thang khia7 ti7 hi2 lai7-bin7; li2 beh chai-cheng3 phu5-to5-hng5, ia7 boe7 tit-tioh8 chiah8 i e5 ke2-chi2.  31). Li2 e5 gu5 thai5 ti7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu cheng5, li2 bo5 thang chiah8--tioh8; li2 e5 lu5 ti7 li2 e5 bak8-cheng5 siu7 chhiuN2-toat8, m7-heng5 li2; li2 e5 iuN5 beh kui li2 e5 tui3-tek8, bo5 lang5 thoe3 li2 kiu3 i.  32). Li2 e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 beh kau ti7 pat8-kok e5 peh-siN3, li2 e5 bak8-chiu beh khoaN3, thong-jit8 liau5-bang7 i, kau3 sit-beng5; li2 e5 chhiu2 ia7 bo5 lat8 thang choe3 sim2-mih8.  33). Li2 e5 thou2-san2, kap li2 tioh8-boa5 sou2 tit-tioh8--e5, beh hou7 li2 sou2 m7-bat e5 kok-bin5 chiah8 liau2-liau2; li2 kan-ta siu7 khi-hu7, siu7 ap-che3;  34). li2 ui7-tioh8 li2 e5 bak8-chiu sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 su7, beh ti3-kau3 tian-kong5.  35). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh eng7 boe7 i--tit e5 tok8-iong phah li2, ti7 li2 e5 kha-thau5-u, kha-thui2, tui3 li2 e5 kha-chiuN2 kau3 thau5-khak-teng2.
	36). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chhian-soa2 li2 kap li2 sou2 siat-lip8 koan2-hat li2 e5 ong5, kau3 li2 kap li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 m7-bat e5 kok, ti7-hia li2 beh hok8-sai7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, si7 chha5--e5, chioh8--e5;  37). li2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beh chhoa7 li2 kau3 e5 liat8-kok-tiong, beh hou7 lang5 gong5-ngiah8, hou7 lang5 choe3 oe7-piN3, siu7 ki-chhi3;  38). li2 beh toa3 choe7-choe7 cheng2-chi2 kau3 chhan5--nih, na7-si7 sou2 siu-e5 si7 chin-chio2; in-ui7 chhau2-meh beh chiah8 i.  39). Li2 beh chai-cheng3 phu5-to5-hng5 lai5 siu-cheng2 i, chong2-si7 bo5 thang lim-chiu2, bo5 thang ban2 ke2-chi2; in-ui7 thang5 beh chiah8 i.  40). Thong keng2-lai7 li2 beh u7 kaN-na2-chhiu7, chong2-si7 bo5 i e5 iu5 thang boah li2 e5 seng-khu; in-ui7 li2 e5 kaN-na2-chhiu7 boe7 tiau5-liap8.  41). Li2 beh siN-kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2, bo5 thang choe3 li2 e5; in-ui7 in beh hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3.  42). Li2 e5 chhiu7-bak8, kap li2 e5 thou2-san2, chhau2-meh beh it-chin7 chiah8 i.  43). Li2 tiong-kan e5 chhut-goa7 lang5 beh na2-seng na2-koaiN5, li2 beh na2-kang3 na2-ke7;  44). i beh chioh li2, ia7 li2 bo5 thang chioh i; i beh choe3-thau5, li2 beh choe3-be2.  45). Chiah e5 chiu3-chou2 beh long2 kau3 ti7 li2, beh tui li2, beh jip-tioh8 li2, kau3 li2 biat8-bo5; in-ui7 li2 bo5 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, bo5 siu2 I sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 hiah e5 kai3-beng7 lut8-le7;  46). chiah e5 chiu3-chou2 beh kau3 ti7 li2 kap li2 e5 hou7-e3, choe3 sin5-jiah ki5-su7, kau3 eng2-oan2.  47). In-ui7 li2 bo5 ui7-tioh8 li2 e5 ho2-giah8, eng7 hoaN-hi2 e5 sim khoai3-lok8 e5 i3-su3, lai5 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3;  48). sou2-i2 li2 beh tu2-tioh8 iau-go7, chhui3-ta, thng3-theh, bo5 poaN3-hang7 mih8, hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chhe lai5 kong-kek li2 e5 tui3-tek8; i beh eng7 thih-taN koa3 ti7 li2 e5 am7-kun2, kau3 biat8-bo5 li2.
	49). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh tui3 hng7-hng7, tui3 toe7-kek8, chhoa7 chit8-kok chhin-chhiuN7 eng pe--lai5 kong-kek li2; hit e5 kok e5 oe7, li2 boe7 hiau2 thiaN;  50). hit e5 kok e5 lang5 bin7 hiong5-kai3-kai3, bo5 the2-thiap lau7-lang5, ia7 bo5 lin5-bin2 gin2-na2;  51). in beh chiah8 li2 e5 cheng-siN sou2-siN-e5, kap li2 e5 thou2-san2, kau3 li2 biat8-bo5; li2 e5 ngou2-kok, chiu2, iu5, i2-kip8 gu5 e5 gu5-a2-kiaN2, iuN5 e5 iuN5-a2-kiaN2, long2 bo5 ka7 li2 lau5--teh, kau3 in biat8-bo5 li2.  52). I beh ui5-khun3 li2 ti7 li2 tak8 e5 siaN5-mng5-lai7, kau3 li2 sou2 oa2-kho3 koaiN5 koh kian-kou3 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5 long2 to2-hoai7 ti7 li2 e5 choan5-toe7; i beh ui5-khun3 li2 ti7 li2 tak8 e5 siaN5-mng5-lai7, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 choan5-toe7.  53). Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 ui5-khun3 li2, li2 ti7 khun2-pek khun3-khou2 e5 tiong-kan, beh chiah8 li2 e5 seng-khu sou2-siN-e5, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 bah.  54). Lin2 tiong-kan iu3-siu3 put-chi2 soe3-ji7 e5 lang5, bak8-chiu beh gin5 i e5 hiaN-ti7, kap i sim-hoai5-tiong e5 bou2, i2-kip8 ki5-u5 sou2 chhun e5 kiaN2-ji5;  55). ti3-kau3 i bo5 beh eng7 i sou2 chiah8 kiaN2-ji5 e5 bah, pun chit8 tiam2-a2 hou7 in tiong-kan e5 chit8-lang5; in-ui7 li2 ti7 tak8 e5 siaN5-mng5-lai7, siu7 tui3-tek8 ui5-khun3 toa7-toa7 khun2-pek li2 e5 si5, i bo5 chhun poaN3-hang7.  56). Lin2 tiong-kan iu3-siu3 soe3-ji7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, in-ui7 i e5 iu3-siu3 soe3-ji7 peng5-sou3 m7-kaN2 eng7 kha-chiuN2 tah8-toe7-e5, beh gin5 i sim-hoai5-tiong e5 tiong7-hu, kap i e5 kiaN2, i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2,  57). i2-kip8 i seng-khu sou2 chhut e5 ui, kap i sou2 siN hiah e5 kiaN2; in-ui7 ti7 li2 siu7 ui5, hou7 tui3-tek8 ti7 li2 chiah e5 siaN5-mng5-lai7 khun2-pek li2 khun3-khou2 e5 si5, i in-ui7 pah-hang7 mih8 khiam3-kheh, sou2-i2 beh thau-chiah8--i.  58). Na7 li2 bo5 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 chit pun2 chheh sou2 ki3 lut8-hoat it-chhe3 e5 oe7, bo5 keng3-ui3 u7 eng5-kng thang kiaN-ui3 e5 mia5, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3,  59). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 beh eng7 ki5-koai3 e5 chai-e7, chiu7-si7 kek8-toa7 kek8-ku2 e5 chai-e7, kap kek8-tang7 kek8-ku2 e5 piN7, kau3 ti7 li2 i2-kip8 li2 e5 hou7-e3;  60). ia7 beh hou7 li2 sou2 kiaN Ai-kip8 hiah e5 piN7-cheng3 long2 lim5-kau3 ti7 li2, ia7 beh tiN5 ti7 li2 e5 seng-khu;  61). lian5 hiah-e5 bo5 ki3 ti7 chit-pun2 lut8-hoat e5 chheh e5 chai-e7 piN7-cheng3, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 i long2 kau3 ti7 li2, kau3 li2 biat8-bo5.  62). Lin2 cheng5 sui-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 thiN-teng2 e5 chhiN hiah-choe7, chong2-si7 in-ui7 li2 bo5 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, sou2-i2 li2 sou2 chhun e5 siau3-giah8 chiu7 beh chio2-chio2.  63). Cheng5 Ia5-ho5-hoa liah8 su3-hok lin2 hou7 lin2 heng-ong7 choe3 hoaN-hi2, au7-lai5 Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 beh liah8 hui2-biat8 lin2, biat8-bo5 lin2, choe3 hoaN-hi2; lin2 ia7 beh tui3 lin2 sou2 jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7 siu7 puih8--khi2-lai5.  64). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 lin2 si3-soaN3 ti7 ban7 peh-siN3-tiong, tui3 toe7 chit e5 kek8-thau5 kau3 toe7 hit e5 kek8-thau5; li2 beh ti7-hia hok8-sai7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3, si7 li2 kap li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 m7-bat, chha5--e5, chioh8--e5.  65). Ti7 hiah e5 kok-lai7, li2 boe7 tit-tioh8 an-jian5, li2 e5 kha ia7 boe7 tit-tioh8 hioh-khun3; Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 beh hou7 li2 ti7-hia sim phok8-phok8-chheng2, bak8-chiu sit-beng5, cheng-sin5 soe-pai7;  66). li2 e5 siN3-mia7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 bo5-tiaN7 bo5-tioh8, li2 jit8-mi5 kiaN-hiaN5, li2 e5 siN3-mia7 bo5 un2-tang3.  67). Li2 in-ui7 sim-lai7 sou2 kiaN-hiaN5 e5, bak8-chiu sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5, cha2-khi2 beh kong2, khou2 boe7-tit chit-si5 am3! am3-si5 beh kong2, khou2 boe7-tit chit-si5 thiN-kng!  68). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 li2 che7-chun5 to3--khi3 Ai-kip8, tui3 hit tiau5 lou7, chiu7-si7 goa2 bat tui3 li2 kong2 li2 boe7 koh khoaN3-kiN3 e5; ti7-hia li2 beh boe7 pun2-sin hou7 tui3-tek8 choe3 lou5-pok8 lu2-pi7, chong2-si7 bo5 lang5 boe2.

[29]	Chiah-e5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ti7 Mou5-ap toe7, beng7-leng7 Mou5-se kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 lip8-iok e5 oe7, si7 I ti7 Ho5-liat8 kap in sou2 lip8 e5 iok i2-goa7--e5.
	2). Mou5-se tiau3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 lai5, ka7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7, ti7 lin2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 tui3 Hoat-lo2, kap i e5 cheng3 jin5-sin5, i2-kip8 i choan5-toe7, sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 su7 lin2 long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3,  3). chiu7-si7 li2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 toa7 chhi3-giam7, kap sin5-jiah, kap hiah e5 toa7 ki5-su7.  4). Chong2-si7 kau3 kin-a2-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa iau2 bo5 hou7 li2 oe7 hiau2-ngou7 e5 sim, oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 bak8-chiu, oe7 thiaN-kiN3 e5 hi7-khang.  5). Goa2 chhoa7 lin2 ti7 khong3-ia2 si3-chap8 ni5, lin2 seng-khu e5 saN bo5 phoa3, kha--nih e5 oe5 ia7 bo5 phoa3;  6). lin2 bo5 chiah8 piaN2, ia7 bo5 lim chheng-chiu2, kau7-chiu2; che si7 beh hou7 lin2 chai Goa2 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  7). Lin2 kau3 chit sou2-chai7, Hi-sit8-pun2 ong5 Se-hong5, Pa-san ong5 Gok8, chhut-lai5 kap lan2 kau-chian3;  8). lan2 chiu7 kong-kek in, chhu2 in e5 toe7, hou7 Liu5-pian7 e5 chi-phai3, Ka-tek e5 chi-phai3, kap Ma2-na2-se poaN3 chi-phai3 choe3-giap8;  9). sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 chit e5 iok e5 oe7, thang hou7 lin2 ti7 it-chhe3 sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7 heng-thong.
	10). Kin-a2-jit8 lin2 cheng3-lang5, lin2 e5 siu2-leng2 , lin2 e5 chi-phai3, lin2 e5 tiuN2-lo2, lin2 e5 koaN-tiuN2, I2-sek-liat8 e5 ta-pou-teng,  11). lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, lin2 e5 bou2, kap li2 iaN5-lai7 e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, tui3 lin2 e5 phoa3-chha5-e5 kau3 lin2 e5 chhiuN7-chui2-e5, long2 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5;  12). hou7 li2 jip8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 iok, ia7 jip8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 kin-a2-jit8 kap li2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5;  13). hou7 I chiau3 I sou2 bat tui3 li2 kong2-e5, koh chiau3 I tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok sou2 chiu3-choa7-e5, kin-a2-jit8 siat-lip8 li2 choe3 I e5 peh-siN3, I choe3 li2 e5 Siong7-te3.  14). Goa2 m7-na7 kap lin2 lip8 chit e5 iok, kap chit e5 chiu3-choa7,  15). ia7 si7 kap hiah-e5 kin-a2-jit8 kap lan2 tang5-khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5-e5, i2-kip8 kin-a2-jit8 bo5 kap lan2 tang5 ti7-teh e5 lang5 lip8 e5;  16). (in-ui7 lan2 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 tiam3 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7, ia7 lan2 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 keng-ke3 lin2 sou2 tui3-hia ke3 e5 liat8-kok, che si7 lin2 sou2 chai e5;  17). lin2 ia7 khoaN3-kiN3 in tiong-kan thang iam3-ouN3 e5 mih8, kap in hiah e5 chha5, chioh8, kim, gun5 e5 ngou2-siong7;)  18). kiaN-liau2 lin2 tiong-kan, ta-pou lang5, a2-si7 cha-bou2 lang5, hek8-si7 ka-chok8, hek8-si7 chi-phai3, in e5 sim kin-a2-jit8 poe7-biu7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 e5 Siong7-te3, khi3 hok8-sai7 hiah e5 kok e5 siong7-te3; koh kiaN-liau2 lin2 tiong-kan u7 phaiN2-kun siN-chhut tok8-chhau2 kap in-tin5;  19). i thiaN-kiN3 chit-e5 chiu3-chou2 e5 oe7, sim-lai7 iu5-goan5 ka-ki7 an-ui3, kong2, Goa2 sui-jian5 kiaN5 tai7-chi3, sim ngi7, chiong ta-e5, tam5-e5 long2 hui2-biat8, goa2 iau2-ku2 oe7 peng5-an;  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 beh sia3-bian2 i, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 kap tou3-khi7, beh sio hit-lang5, chiong chit pun2 chheh sou2 ki3 it-chhe3 e5 chiu3-chou2, long2 beh kau3 ti7 i e5 seng-khu; Ia5-ho5-hoa koh beh tui3 thiN-e7 chhat-biat8 i e5 mia5;  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 beh chiau3 chit e5 lut8-hoat e5 chheh sou2 ki3-chai3 e5 iok it-chhe3 e5 chiu3-chou2, tui3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3 chi-phai3 e5 tiong-kan hun-piat i, hou7 i tu2-tioh8 chai-e7.
	22). Chiu7 au7-tai7, lin2 hou7-poe3 e5 kiaN2-sun, kap hng7-hng7 lai5 e5 goa7-kok lang5, khoaN3-kiN3 hit sou2-chai7 e5 chai-e7, i2-kip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hou7 in tu2-tioh8 e5 piN7-cheng3,  23). koh khoaN3-kiN3 pian3-toe7 u7 jiu5-ng5, u7 iam5, u7 he2-sio, bo5 cheng3-choh, bo5 chhut-san2, lian5 chhau2 ia7 bo5 hoat-siN ti7-hia, chhin-chhiuN7 Sou2-to-ma2, Go5-mou5-lah8, Ap-ma2, Se2-phian e5 hui2-hoai7, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 si5 sou2 hui2-hoai7-e5 chit8-iuN7,  24). hiah e5 liat8-kok in long2 beh kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa siaN2-su7 tui3 chit e5 toe7 an2-ni kiaN5 ah? chit e5 siu7-khi3 hiah beng2-liat8 si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3 ah?  25). Lang5 beh kong2, Si7 in-ui7 in khi3-sak Ia5-ho5-hoa in liat8-chou2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 iok, si7 I chhoa7 in chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 si5 sou2 lip8 e5;  26). in khi3 than3 pat8-e5 siong7-te3 hok8-sai7 i, si7 in peng5-sou3 sou2 m7-bat e5 siong7-te3, Ia5-ho5-hoa be7-bat hun-phai3 hou7 in e5;  27). sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoat toa7 siu7-khi3 ti7 chit e5 toe7, chiong chit e5 chheh sou2 ki3 it-chhe3 e5 chiu3-chou2, long2 kang3-loh8 ti7 i;  28). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 siu7-khi3-tiong toa7 siu7-khi3, thong3-hun7 puih8 in chhut i e5 toe7, hiat in ti7 goa7-pang, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8 chit8-iuN7.  29). Pi3-bat8 e5 su7 siok8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lan2 Siong7-te3 e5; hian2-beng5 e5 su5, si7 eng2-oan2 siok8 ti7 lan2 kap lan2 e5 kiaN2-sun, beh hou7 lan2 kiaN5 chit e5 lut8-hoat it-chhe3 e5 oe7.

[30]	Chiah e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7-si7 goa2 sou2 pai5-liat8 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 e5 chiok-hok kap chiu3-chou2, chiong-lai5 kau3 ti7 li2, li2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 koaN2 li2 kau3 e5 liat8-kok-tiong,  2). li2 e5 sim ki3-tit i, li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2-sun na7 chin7-sim chin7-seng3 kui-ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, thiaN-than3 I e5 oe7, chiau3 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 it-chhe3 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5;  3). chiu7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh hou7 li2 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 to3-tng2-lai5, beh lin5-bin2 li2, beh to3-tng2-lai5 chu7-chip8 li2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 sou2 si3-soaN3 li2 kau3 e5 liat8-kok lai5.  4). Li2 siu7 koaN2-tiok8 e5, na7 u7 ti7 thiN-piN e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 ia7 beh tui3 hia chu7-chip8 li2, toa3 li2 tui3 hia to3--lai5.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh chhoa7 li2 jip8 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 seng5-chiap e5 toe7, li2 ia7 seng5-chiap i; I ia7 beh ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2, hou7 li2 e5 lang5-giah8 ke-thiN pi2 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 khah-choe7.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh ti7 li2 e5 sim, kap li2 e5 hou7-e3 e5 sim, kiaN5 kat-le2, hou7 li2 chin7-sim chin7-seng3 thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, hou7 li2 thang tit-tioh8 oah8.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh chiong che it-chhe3 e5 chiu3-chou2 he7 ti7 li2 e5  tui3-tek8, kap oan3-hun7 li2 khun2-pek li2 e5 lang5 e5 sin-chiuN7;  8). li2 beh to3-tng2 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, kiaN5 I it-chhe3 e5 kai3-beng7, chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5.  9-10). Li2 na7 thiaN-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7, chip-siu2 chit e5 lut8-hoat sou2 ki3 e5 kai3-beng7 lut8-le7, koh chin7-sim chin7-seng3 kui-ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh hou7 li2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, kap li2 e5 seng-khu sou2-siN-e5, cheng-siN sou2-chhut-e5, thou2-toe7 sou2-chhut-e5, chhiong-chiok u7 chhun; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh koh hoaN-hi2 li2, su3-hok li2, chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5 hoaN-hi2 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 chit8-iuN7.
	11). In-ui7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 beng7-leng7 li2 e5 kai3-beng7, m7-si7 li2 sou2 choe3-boe7-kau3-e5, ia7 bo5 ti7 hng7-hng7.  12). M7-si7 ti7 thiN--nih, ti3-kau3 li2 kong2, Chi7-chui7 ui7 goan2 chiuN7-thiN, toa3-lai5 goan2 chia, hou7 goan2 thiaN lai5 kiaN5 i ah?  13). Ia7 m7-si7 ti7 hai2-goa7, ti3-kau3 li2 kong2, Chi7-chui7 ui7 goan2 ke3-hai2 toa3-lai5 goan2 chia, hou7 goan2 thiaN lai5 kiaN5 i ah?  14). Chit e5 oe7 kap li2 chin kun7, chiu7-si7 ti7 li2 e5 chhui3 ti7 li2 e5 sim, hou7 li2 thang lai5 kiaN5 i.
	15). KhoaN3 ah, goa2 kin-a2-jit8 u7 eng7 oah8 kap hok-khi3, si2 kap chai-e7, pai5-liat8 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  16). chiu7-si7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 beng7-leng7 li2 thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, kiaN5 I e5 to7-lou7, siu2 I e5 kai3-beng7, lut8-le7, hoat-tou7, hou7 li2 thang oah8-teh, ke-thiN lang5-giah8, Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 chiu7 beh ti7 li2 sou2 beh jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7 su3-hok li2.  17). Siat-su2 li2 e5 sim poe7-biu7 m7 thiaN-than3, koh siu7 iu2-hek8, khi3 keng3-pai3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 hok8-sai7 i;  18). goa2 kin-a2-jit8 chiu7 beng5-beng5 ka7 lin2 kong2, lin2 tek-khak beh biat8-bo5; ti7 li2 ke3 Iok-tan3 jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7, li2 e5 jit8-chi2 boe7-oe7 ku2-tng5.  19). Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 kio3 thiN kio3 toe7 tui3 lin2 choe3 kan-cheng3, goa2 eng7 siN si2, chiok-hok chiu3-chou2, pai5-liat8 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; so2-i2 li2 tioh8 keng2 oah8-mia7, hou7 li2 kap li2 e5 hou7-e3 long2 oe7 oah8-teh;  20). lai5 thiaN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3, thiaN I e5 oe7, kiat-lian5 ti7 I; in-ui7 I si7 li2 e5 oah8-mia7, li2 e5 jit8-chi2 ku2-tng5 ia7 chai7 ti7 I; hou7 li2 thang khia7-khi2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok, chiu3-choa7 sou2 beh siuN2-su3 in e5 toe7.

[31]	Mou5-se eng7 chiah e5 oe7 khi3 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 kong2.  2). Tui3 in kong2, Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 chit8-pah ji7-chap8 he3, boe7 koh chiau3-siong5 chhut-jip8; Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 bat tui3 goa2 kong2, Li2 boe7-oe7 ke3 chit e5 Iok-tan3.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 beh chhoa7 li2 ke3--khi3, beh biat8-bo5 chiah e5 kok ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 beh seng5-chiap in.  Iok-su-a beh chhoa7 li2 ke3-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 bat kong2-e5.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh khoan2-thai7 in, chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5-jit8 khoan2-thai7 I sou2 biat8 A-mou5-li7 lang5 nng7 e5 ong5, Se-hong5 kap Gok8, i2-kip8 in e5 toe7 chit8-iuN7.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh eng7 in kau ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5; lin2 tioh8 chiau3 goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3 lin2 it-chhe3 e5 beng7-leng7 khoan2-thai7 in.  6). Lin2 tioh8 iong2-kam2 chong3-taN2, boh8-tit kiaN in, ia7 boh8-tit lun2 in; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 Siong7-te3 kap li2 khi3, I bo5 li7-khui li2, ia7 bo5 pang3-sak li2.  7). Mou5-se kio3 Iok-su-a lai5, ti7 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 tui3 i kong2, Li2 tioh8 iong2-kam2 chong3-taN2, in-ui7 li2 beh kap chit e5 peh-siN3 khi3, jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 in liat8-chou2 chiu3-choa7 beh hou7 in e5 toe7, li2 ia7 beh hou7 in tit-tioh8 i choe3-giap8.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa beh kiaN5 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; I beh kap li2 ti7-teh, I bo5 li7-khui li2, ia7 bo5 pang3-sak li2; boh8-tit kiaN, ia7 boh8-tit lun2.
	9). Mou5-se sia2 chit e5 lut8-hoat, kau-hou7 kng Ia5-ho5-hoa iok-kui7 e5 che3-si, Li7-bi7 e5 kiaN2-sun, kap I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3 tiuN2-lo2.  10). Mou5-se beng7-leng7 in kong2, Mui2 chhit-ni5 e5 lou7-be2, chiu7-si7 ti7 thau2-pang3 e5 ni5 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 ki5, tah-liau5-choeh e5 si5,  11). I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 lai5-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 I sou2 keng2 e5 sou2-chai7, hit-si5 li2 tioh8 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 thak8 chit e5 lut8-hoat hou7 in thiaN.  12). Li2 tioh8 chu7-chip8 peh-siN3, ta-pou, cha-bou2, gin2-na2, i2-kip8 li2 siaN5-mng5-lai7 e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, hou7 in thiaN, hou7 in hap8-sip8, thang keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 chit e5 lut8-hoat it-chhe3 e5 oe7;  13). ia7 hou7 in m7-chai-iaN2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 tit-tioh8 thiaN-kiN3; chiu7 ti7 lin2 ke3 Iok-tan3 sou2 seng5-chiap e5 toe7, chiau3 lin2 tiam3 ti7-hia it-chhe3 e5 jit8 thang hak8-sip8 keng3-ui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.
	14). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, KhoaN3 ah, li2 si2 e5 ki5 kun7 lah; li2 tiau3 Iok-su-a lai5, saN-kap khia7 ti7 hoe7-bou7-tiong; Goa2 beh eng7 chit-jim7 beng7-leng7 i, Mou5-se chiu7 kap Iok-su-a khi3 saN-kap khia7 ti7 hoe7-bou7-tiong.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7, hun5-thiau7 tiong, hian2-hian7; hun5-thiau7 theng5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-mng5 e5 teng2-bin7.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh tui3 Mou5-se kong2, KhoaN3 ah, li2 beh kap li2 liat8-chou2 saN-kap khun3; chit e5 peh-siN3 beh khi2-lai5, kiaN5 sia5-im5 lai5 than3 i sou2 beh khi3 tiam3 hit sou2-chai7 goa7-bin7 e5 siong7-te3, li7-khui Goa2, poe7 Goa2 kap i sou2 lip8 e5 iok.  17). Hit-si5 Goa2 beh tui3 in hoat-chhut siu7-khi3; Goa2 ia7 beh li7-khui in, ng-bin7 m7-khoaN3 in; in beh siu7 thun-biat8, tu2-tioh8 choe7-choe7 chai-e7 hoan7-lan7; hit-jit8 in beh kong2, Lan2 tu2-tioh8 chai-e7 hoan7-lan7, kiam2-m7-si7 in-ui7 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 bo5 ti7 lan2 e5 tiong-kan mah?  18). Hit-jit8 in-ui7 in phian-ng3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2, sou2-i2 Goa2 koat-toan3 ng Goa2 e5 bin7.  19). TaN lin2 ka-ki7 tioh8 sia2 chit e5 koa, eng7 hit-e5 ka3-si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 kiaN2-sun, hou7 in e5 chhui3 liam7, hou7 chit e5 koa ka7 Goa2 choe3 kan-cheng3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 kiaN2-sun.  20). In-ui7 Goa2 chhoa7 in jip8 Goa2 tui3 in e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 hit e5 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7; in tit-tioh8 chiah8 koh pa2-chiok, sin-the2 pui5, chiu7 beh phian-ng3 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 hok8-sai7 in, khoaN3-khin Goa2, poe7 Goa2 e5 iok.  21). Kau3 in tu2-tioh8 choe7-choe7 chai-e7 hoan7-lan7 e5 si5, chit e5 koa beh ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 choe3 kian3-cheng3 lai5 kan-cheng3 in; in-ui7 in e5 kiaN2-sun e5 chhui3 beh liam7, bo5 boe7-ki3-tit; in-ui7 hian7-kim Goa2 iau2-be7 chhoa7 in kau3 Goa2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 e5 toe7, in sou2 chun5 e5 liam7-thau5, Goa2 i2-keng chai.  22). Tng hit-jit8 Mou5-se chiu7 sia2 chit e5 koa, chiong i lai5 ka3-si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 kiaN2-sun.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a kong2, Li2 tioh8 iong2-kam2 chong3-taN2, in-ui7 li2 beh chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 jip8 Goa2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 hou7 in e5 toe7; Goa2 beh kap li2 saN-kap ti7-teh.
	24). Mou5-se eng7 chit e5 lut8-hoat e5 oe7 sia2 ti7 chheh--nih, it-chin7 sia2 beng5-pek8;  25). Mou5-se chiu7 hoan-hu3 kng Ia5-ho5-hoa iok-kui7 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5, kong2,  26). Chiong chit e5 lut8-hoat e5 chheh he7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 Siong7-te3 e5 iok-kui7 piN, thang ti7-hia choe3 li2 e5 kan-cheng3.  27). In-ui7 goa2 chai li2 si7 poe7-gek8--e5, si7 am7-kun2 ngi7--e5; khoaN3 ah, Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 iau2 oah8 kap lin2 ti7-teh, lin2 siong7-chhiaN2 poe7-gek8 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ho5-hong3 goa2 si2 liau2-au7 ah?  28). Tioh8 chu7-chip8 lin2 chiah e5 chi-phai3 e5 tiuN2-lo2 kap koaN-tiuN2 long2 lai5, goa2 beh kong2 chiah e5 oe7 hou7 in thiaN, ia7 beh kio3-thiN kio3-toe7 hou7 in choe3 kan-cheng3.  29). In-ui7 goa2 chai goa2 si2 liau2-au7, lin2 beh choan5-jian5 pai7-hoai7, oai-chhoah8 goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 kiaN5 e5 to7-lou7; jit8-au7 lin2 beh tu2-tioh8 chai-e7, in-ui7 lin2 beh kiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 khoaN3-choe3 phaiN2 e5 su7, eng7 lin2 e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 jia2 I e5 siu7-khi3.
	30). Mou5-se chiong chit e5 koa e5 oe7, thau5 kau3 be2 kong2 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-hoe7 thiaN.

[32]	Chiah e5 thiN ah, tioh8 aN3 hi7-khang, goa2 beh kong2-oe7; Goan7 toe7 ia7 tioh8 thiaN goa2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 e5.
2.	Goa2 e5 ka3-si7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 kang3-loh8, Goa2 e5 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 lou7-chui2 teh tih; Chhin-chhiuN7 mng-mng e5 hou7 loh8 ti7 iu3-iu3 e5 chhau2, Chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-hou7 loh8 ti7 chhai3-soe.
3.	In-ui7 goa2 beh soan-thoan5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5;  Lin2 tioh8 chun lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 choe3 toa7.
4.	Choe3 Chioh8-poaN5-e5, I sou2-choe3-e5 si7 oan5-choan5, I e5 lou7 long2 si7 kong-peng5;  Si7 chin-sit8 e5 Siong7-te3, long2 bo5 put-gi7;  I si7 kong-gi7, koh cheng3-tit8.
5.	Chit e5 koai-phiah oan-khiau e5 se3-tai7 ka-ki7 pai7-hoai7;  M7-si7 I e5 kiaN2, si7 in e5 pe7-peng7.
6.	Gu5-gong7 bu5-ti e5 peh-siN3 ah, Lin2 an2-ni po3-tap Ia5-ho5-hoa mah?  I kiam2-m7-si7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7, boe2-li2-e5 mah?  I u7 chhong3-cho7 li2, kian3-lip8 li2.
7.	Tioh8 ki3-tit kou2-cha2 e5 jit8, Siau3-liam7 lek8-tai7 e5 ni5;  Mng7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7, i beh chi2-si7 li2, Mng7 li2 e5 lau7-toa7, in beh ka7 li2 kong2.
8.	Chi3-koaiN5-e5 pun-giap8 hou7 liat8-pang.  Pun-khui se3-kan lang5 e5 si5, Chiu7 tiaN7-tioh8 peh-siN3 e5 kai3-han7, Chiau3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 siau3-giah8.
9.	Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hun7-giah8 si7 I e5 peh-siN3;  I sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 san2-giap7 si7 Nga2-kok.
10.	I tu2-tioh8 i ti7 pha-hng e5 toe7, Ti7 hong-hoe3 ia2-siu3 hau2 e5 khong3-ia2, I ui5-seh8 i, khoaN3-kou3 i, Po2-hou7 i chhin-chhiuN7 bak8-chiu-jin5.
11.	Koh chhin-chhiuN7 eng-chiau2 la7 i e5 siu7, Ti7 eng-a2 e5 teng2-bin7 iat8 i e5 sit8, Thi2-khui  sit8-kou2 lai5 sin5 i, Chai3 i ti7 i e5 sit8-kou2.
12.	Chi2-u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhoa7 i, Bo5 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 kap i ti7-teh.
13.	Chiu7 hou7 i khia5 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7, Tit-tioh8 chiah8 chhan5--nih e5 thou2-san2;  Koh hou7 i tui3 chioh8-poaN5 suh-bit8, Tui3 he2-chioh8 suh-iu5;
14.	Ia7 chiah8 gu5-lin-iu5, kap iuN5-lin, Pui5 e5 iuN5-a2-kiaN2, Pa-san sou2 chhut e5 mi5-iuN5-kang2 kap soaN-iuN5, Kap siong7-ho2 e5 sio2-beh8;  Ia7 lim phu5-to5-chiap e5 chiu2.
15.	Ia5-su-lun5 pui5 chiu7 a3-pa3, Li2 i2-keng pui5, koh toa7-liap8, bah chin-phauh;  I chiu7 li7-khui chhong3-cho7 i e5 Siong7-te3, KhoaN3-khin kiu3 i e5 Chioh8-poaN5.
16.	In eng7 pat8 e5 siong7-te3 kek I tou3-khi7, Eng7 kho2-ouN3-e5, jia2 I e5 siu7-khi3.
17.	In che3-hian3 sia5-kui2, m7-si7 chin e5 Siong7-te3, Chiu7-si7 in peng5-sou3 sou2 m7-bat e5 siong7-te3, Si7 sin--e5, kun7-lai5 chiah u7--e5, Si7 li2 e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 bo5 kiaN-ui3 e5.
18.	SiN li2 e5 Chioh8-poaN5, li2 bo5 siau3-liam7 I, SiN li2 e5 Siong7-te3, li2 boe7-ki3-tit I.
19.	Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 oan3-hun7, In-ui7 I e5 kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kek I e5 ian5-kou3.
20.	Chiu7 kong2, Goa2 beh tui3 in ng Goa2 e5 bin7, KhoaN3 in kiat-kiok8 chaiN2-iuN7;  In si7 koai-phiah e5 chok8-lui7, Bo5 sin3-sit8 e5 kiaN2-ji5.
21.	In eng7 hit-e5 m7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5, kek Goa2 e5 tou3-khi7, Eng7 in e5 hu-ke2 e5 mih8, jia2 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3;  Goa2 chiu7 eng7 m7-si7 choe3 peh-siN3 e5, kek in e5 tou3-khi7;  Eng7 gu5-gong7 e5 kok-bin5, jia2 in e5 siu7-khi3.
22.	In-ui7 ti7 Goa2 e5 siu7-khi3-tiong u7 he2 toh8--khi2-lai5, Sio kau3 im-kan kek8-chhim e5 sou2-chai7, Ia7 sio toe7 kap toe7 e5 chhut-san2, Ia7 khi2-he2 sio chiah e5 soaN e5 toe7-ki.
23.	Goa2 beh chek-chu7 chai-e7 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7, Eng7 Goa2 long2-chong2 e5 chiN3 lai5 sia7 in.
24.	In beh in-ui7 iau-go7 lai5 siau-san2, Siu7 iam7-jiat8 kap tok8-cheng3 thun-biat8;  Goa2 beh hou7 in tu2-tioh8 ia2-siu3 e5 chhui3-khi2, Kap choa5 e5 tok8.
25.	Goa7-bin7 u7 to-kiam3, Lai7-bin7 u7 kiaN-hiaN5, hou7 lang5 si2-bo5, Hou7 siau3-lian5 e5 ta-pou-lang5, kap chai7-sek-lu2, Chiah8-lin-e5, kap peh8 thau5-mng5 e5 lang5, long2 biat8-bo5,
26.	Goa2 kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 in si3-soaN3 ti7 hng7-hng7, Ti7 lang5 e5 tiong-kan tu5 in e5 mia5-ji7;
27.	Chong2-si7 Goa2 kiaN tui3-tek8 kek Goa2, KiaN-liau2 in e5 tui3-tek8 gou7-hoe7, KiaN-liau2 in beh kong2, Si7 goan2 e5 chhiu2 kiah8-koaiN5, M7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kiaN5 chiah e5 su7.
28.	In-ui7 in si7 boe7 hiau2-tit siuN7 e5 peh-siN3, Ti7 sim-lai7 bo5 chhang-mia5.
29.	Goan7 in u7 ti3-hui7, oe7 beng5-pek8 chit-e5, Oe7 siuN7 in e5 kiat-kiok8.
30.	Na7 m7-si7 in e5 Chioh8-poaN5 boe7 in, Na7 m7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiong in kau hou7 lang5, ChaiN2-iuN7 tui3-tek8 chit8-e5 oe7 koaN2 in chit8-chheng?  Nng7-e5 oe7 hou7 in chit8-ban7 to5-chau2 ah?
31.	In e5 chioh8-poaN5 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 e5 Chioh8-poaN5, Lian5 lan2 e5 tui3-tek8 ia7 an2-ni pheng5-phoaN3.
32.	In e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 si7 tui3 Sou2-to-ma2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 thoan5-e5, Ia7 tui3 Go5-mou5-lah8 e5 hng5 chhut-e5, In e5 phu5-to5 si7 tok8 e5 phu5-to5, Kui-pha long2 si7 khou2--e5;
33.	In e5 chiu2 si7 leng5 e5 tok8, Si7 ok-choa5 chan5-hai7 e5 tok8.
34.	Che kiam2-m7-si7 chek-chu7 ti7 Goa2 chia, Hong-bat8 ti7 Goa2 po2-poe3 e5 khou3-pang5 mah?
35.	Sin-oan po3-eng3 chai7-ti7 Goa2, Ti7 in e5 kha tah8-tian e5 si5;  In-ui7 in tu2-tioh8 chai-e7 e5 jit8 kun7 lah, Sou2 beh tu2-tioh8 e5 su7 oe7 kin2-kin2 kau3.
36.	Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3-kiN3 I e5 peh-siN3 khui3-lat8 i2-keng bo5--khi3, Hiah-e5 khu-sok--e5, chu7-iu5--e5, long2 bo5 lau5 chit8-e5, Chiu7 beh thoe3 in sin-oan, In-ui7 I e5 lou5-pok8 lai5 the3-hoe2.
37.	I beh kong2, In e5 siong7-te3, In sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 chioh8-poaN5;
38.	Chiu7-si7 chiah8 in che3-su7 e5 iu5, Lim in koan3-tian7 e5 chiu2 e5, taN ti7 toh-loh8?  Thang hou7 in khi2-lai5 pang-chan7 lin2, Po2-hou7 lin2.
39.	Lin2 taN tioh8 khoaN3, Goa2 , Goa2 chiu7-si7 I, Goa2 i2-goa7 bo5 u7 Siong7-te3;  Goa2 hou7 lang5 si2, Goa2 hou7 lang5 oah8, Goa2 sun2-siong--i, Goa2 i-ti7--i;  Bo5 chit8-e5 oe7 tui3 Goa2 e5 chhiu2 kiu3-chhut.
40.	Goa2 kiah8-khi2 chhiu2 ng3 thiN kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 eng2-oah8 lai5 kong2;
41.	Goa2 na7 boa5 Goa2 kng-na3-na3 e5 to, Goa2 na7 chip-heng5 sim2-phoaN3, Chiu7 beh heng5-hoat8 Goa2 e5 tui3-tek8, Po3-eng3 oan3-hun7 Goa2 e5 lang5.
42.	Goa2 beh hou7 Goa2 e5 chiN3 lim huih kau3 chui3, Goa2 e5 to beh chiah8 bah, Chiu7-si7 siu7-thai5 siu7-liah8 e5 lang5 e5 huih, Tui3-tek8 siu2-leng2 e5 thau5 e5 bah.
43.	Liat8-kok ah, long2 tioh8 kap I e5 peh-siN3 saN-kap hoaN-hi2;  In-ui7 I beh ui7 I e5 lou5-pok8 e5 huih sin-oan, Po3-eng3 I e5 tui3-tek8, Beh siok8 I e5 toe7 kap I e5 peh-siN3 e5 choe7.
	44). Mou5-se lai5, eng7 chit e5 koa it-chhe3 e5 oe7 liam7 hou7 peh-siN3 thiaN; Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a ia7 kap i ti7-teh.  45). Mou5-se tui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3-lang5 kong2 chiah e5 it-chhe3 e5 oe7 beng5-pek8, chiu7 ka7 in kong2,  46). Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 sou2 tui3 lin2 kan-cheng3 it-chhe3 e5 oe7, lin2 tioh8 khng3 ti7 sim--nih; ia7 tioh8 hoan-hu3 lin2 e5 kiaN2-sun chip-siu2 lai5 kiaN5 chit e5 lut8-hoat it-chhe3 e5 oe7;  47). in-ui7 che tui3-ti7 lin2 m7-si7 khang-khang e5 su7; si7 lin2 e5 oah8-mia7, ia7 beh in-ui7 chit e5 su7 lin2 e5 jit8-chi2 tit-tioh8 ku2-tng5, ti7 lin2 ke3 Iok-tan3 beh jip8-khi3 seng5-chiap e5 toe7.
	48). Tng jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  49). Li2 chiuN7-khi3 A-pa-lim5 soaN, Ni5-pho e5 soaN-thau5, kap Ia5-li7-ko tui3-bin7 e5 Mou5-ap toe7, khoaN3 Goa2 siuN2-su3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choe3-giap8 e5 Ka-lam5 toe7;  50). li2 beh si2 ti7 li2 sou2 chiuN7-khi3 e5 soaN, lai5 to3-chou2, chhin-chhiuN7 li2 e5 hiaN A-lun5 si2 ti7 Ho5-jiN2 soaN, lai5 to3-chou2 chit8-iuN7;  51). in-ui7 lin2 ti7 Sim5 e5 khong3-ia2, Ka-te-su e5 Bi2-li7-pa e5 chui2, ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiong tek-choe7 Goa2, in-ui7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiong bo5 chun Goa2 choe3 seng3.  52). Li2 thang tui3-bin7 khoaN3 hit e5 toe7, chong2-si7 boe7-tit-thang jip8-khi3 kau3 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 toe7.

[33]	Siong7-te3 e5 lou5-pok8 Mou5-se, ti7 i iau2-be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng, ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiok-hok; sou2 chiok-hok e5 oe7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  2). I kong2,
	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Se-nai2 lai5, Ui7-tioh8 in tui3 Se-jiN2 khi2-lai5; Tui3 Pa-lan5 e5 soaN chio3-chhut kng, Tui3 ban7-ban7 seng3-e5 hia lai5; Tui3 I e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 ui7-tioh8 in hoat-chhut liat8-he2 e5 lut8-hoat.
3.	I put-chi2 thiaN3-thang3 hiah e5 peh-siN3, I hiah e5 seng3--e5 long2 ti7 Li2 e5 chhiu2;  In che7 ti7 Li2 e5 kha-e7, ThiaN-siu7 Li2 hiah e5 oe7.
4.	Mou5-se eng7 lut8-hoat thoan5 hou7 lan2, Choe3 Nga2-kok hoe7-chiong3 e5 san2-giap8.
5.	Peh-siN3 e5 siu2-leng2, I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3 chi-phai3 saN-kap chu7-hoe7 e5 si5, I ti7 Ia5-su-lun5 choe3-ong5.
6.	Goan7 Liu5-pian7 oah8-teh bo5 si2, Goan7 i e5 lang5-giah8 bo5 chio2.
7.	I ka7 Iu5-tai7 chiok-hok, an2-ni kong2, Kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN Iu5-tai7 e5 siaN, Chhoa7 i kau3 i e5 peh-siN3 hia;  I bat eng7 i e5 chhiu2 ui7 ka-ki7 kau-chian3;  Li2 beh pang-chan7 i ti2-tng i e5 tui3-tek8.
8.	Lun7 Li7-bi7 kong2, Li2 e5 Thou2-beng5 kap Li2 e5 OU-leng5, kap Li2 seng3-kiat e5 lang5 saN-kap ti7-teh;  Li2 ti7 Ma2-sat bat chhi3 i, Ti7 Bi2-li7-pa e5 chui2 bat kap i saN-chiN.
9.	I lun7-kau3 i e5 lau7-pe7, i e5 lau7-bu2, chiu7 kong2, Goa2 m7-bat khoaN3-kiN3 i;  Ia7 bo5 seng5-jin7 i e5 hiaN-ti7;  Ia7 bo5 seng5-jin7 i e5 kiaN2-ji5;  In-ui7 in kiaN5 Li2 e5 oe7, Siu2 Li2 e5 iok.
10.	In beh eng7 Li2 e5 hoat-tou7 ka3-si7 Nga2-kok, Eng7 Li2 e5 lut8-hoat ka3-si7 I2-sek-liat8;  In beh eng7 hiuN he7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, Kap ka-nng5-chiah e5 sio-che3 ti7 Li2 e5 toaN5-teng2.
11.	Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok i e5 san2-giap8, Chiap-lap8 i e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3 e5 kang;  Hiah e5 khi2-lai5 kong-kek i kap oan3-hun7 i e5 lang5, Goan7 Li2 phah-chih8 in e5 io, hou7 in boe7 koh khi2-lai5,
12.	Lun7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 chiu7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 thiaN3 e5 beh kap I an-jian5 khia7-khi2;  Ia5-ho5-hoa thong-jit8 po2-hou7 i, I ia7 beh tiam3 ti7 i e5 keng-thau5-tiong.
13.	Lun7 Iok-sek chiu7 kong2, Goan7 i e5 toe7 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok, Tit-tioh8 thiN-teng2 e5 po2-mih8, kap lou7-chui2, I2-kip8 toe7-e7 sou2 khng3 e5 chui2-goan5;
14.	Tit-tioh8 jit8-thau5 sou2 siN e5 po2-mih8, Geh8 sou2 chhut e5 po2-mih8;
15.	Tit-tioh8 kou2-cha2 e5 soaN e5 chi3-po2, Kap eng2 se3-tai7 e5 soaN-nia2 e5 po2-mih8;
16.	Tit-tioh8 toe7 e5 po2-mih8 kap ki5-tiong sou2 chhiong-moa2--e5, I2-kip8 tiam3 ti7 chhi3-phe3-lai7--e5 e5 un-hui7;  Goan7 hiah e5 long2 kui ti7 Iok-sek e5 thau5-khak, Kui ti7 hit-e5 kap i e5 hiaN-ti7 pun-khui--e5 e5 thau5-khak-teng2.
17.	Chhin-chhiuN7 gu5 e5 thau5-chiuN7-siN-e5, eng5-kng siok8 ti7 i, I e5 kak si7 ia2-gu5 e5 kak;  Eng7 in lai5 tak ban7 peh-siN3 kau3 ti7 toe7-kek8;  Che si7 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 ban7-ban7, Ma2-na2-se e5 chheng-chheng.
18.	Lun7 Se-pou3-lun5 chiu7 kong2, Se-pou3-lun5 ah, li2 chhut-goa7 thang hoaN-hi2;  I2-sat-ka ah, ti7 li2 e5 pou3-piN5-lai7 thang khoai3-lok8.
19.	In beh tiau3 chiah e5 peh-siN3 kau3 soaN--nih, Ti7-hia beh hian3 kong-gi7 e5 che3;  In-ui7 in beh khip-siu hai2--nih e5 hong-seng7, Kap soa--nih sou2-khng3 e5 po2-poe3.
20.	Lun7 Ka-tek chiu7 kong2, Khui-khoah Ka-tek-e5 tit-tioh8 o-lo2;  I bih-teh chhin-chhiuN7 bu2 e5 sai, I thiah-lih8 chhiu2-kut kap thau5-khak.
21.	I ui7 ka-ki7 pi7-pan7 tai7-seng tit-tioh8 e5 giap8, In-ui7 ti7-hia u7 siat lut8-hoat--e5 e5 hun7-giah8 lau5--teh;  I kap peh-siN3 e5 siu2-leng2 saN-kap lai5, KiaN5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 kong-gi7, Kap I2-sek-liat8 saN-kap kiaN5 I e5 phoaN3-toan3.
22.	Lun7 Tan3 chiu7 kong2, Tan3 si7 soe3 chiah sai, Tui3 Pa-san thiau3-chhut.
23.	Lun7 Na2-hut-tha-li7 chiu7 kong2, Na2-hut-tha-li7 ah, tit-tioh8 un-hui7 chhiong-chiok;  Ia7 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-hok moa2-moa2 e5, Beh tit-tioh8 sai--si3 kap lam5--si3 choe3 giap8.
24.	Lun7 A-siat chiu7 kong2, Goan7 A-siat in-ui7 kiaN2 choe7 lai5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3, Tit-tioh8 in e5 hiaN-ti7 e5 hoaN-hi2;  Thang eng7 i e5 kha un3 ti7 iu5--nih.
25.	Li2 e5 mng5-kong5 si7 thih--e5, tang5--e5;  Li2 e5 jit8-chi2 chaiN2-iuN7, li2 e5 khui3-lat8 ia7 beh an2-ni.
26.	Ia5-su-lun5 ah, bo5 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 Siong7-te3 e5, I che7-thiN lai5 pang-chan7 li2, Ia7 che7 kiong-chhong, hian2-beng5 I e5 eng5-kng.
27.	Eng2-oah8 e5 Siong7-te3 choe3 li2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, Eng2-oan2 e5 chhiu2 ti7 li2 e5 e7-bin7;  I ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2 tui3-tek8, Koh kong2, Hui2-biat8 i.
28.	I2-sek-liat8 an-jian5 khia7-khi2, Nga2-kok e5 hou7-e3 ka-ki7 toa3 ti7 ngou2-kok kap chiu2 e5 toe7;  I e5 thiN ia7 tih-loh8 lou7-chui2.
29.	I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 u7 hok-khi3;  Chi7-chui7 chhin-chhiuN7 li2 chit-e5 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chin2-kiu3 e5 peh-siN3 ah?  I si7 li2 e5 tin5-pai5 po2-hou7 li2, Si7 li2 eng5-iau7 e5 to-kiam3;  Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 beh tau5-hang5 li2;  Li2 beh tah8 ti7 in koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7.

[34]	Mou5-se tui3 Mou5-ap piN5-iuN5 chiuN7 Ni5-pho soaN, chiuN7 hit e5 kap Ia5-li7-ko saN-tui3 e5 Pi2-su-ka soaN-thau5.  Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 i khoaN3 Ki-liat8 choan5-toe7 tit8-kau3 Tan3;  2).  Na2-hut-tha-li7 choan5-toe7, I2-hoat-lian5 Ma2-na2-se e5 toe7, Iu5-tai7 choan5-toe7 kau3 sai-hai2;  3). Lam5-hng kap kio3-choe3 cho2-chhiu7-siaN5 e5 Ia5-li7-ko soaN-kok e5 piN5-iuN5, kau3 So2-jiN2.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i kong2, Chit e5 toe7 chiu7-si7 Goa2 tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok, chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 beh siuN2-su3 li2 e5 hou7-e3 e5, taN Goa2 hou7 li2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3; chong2-si7 li2 boe7 tit-tioh8 ke3-khi3 kau3 hia.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou5-pok8 Mou5-se chiu7 si2 ti7-hia, ti7 Mou5-ap e5 toe7, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2 e5.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa bai5-chong3 i ti7 Mou5-ap toe7, Pek-pi2-jiN2 saN-tui3 e5 soaN-kok; kau3 kin-a2-jit8 bo5 lang5 chai i e5 bong7.  7). Mou5-se si2 e5 si5, chit8-pah ji7-chap8 he3, bak8-chiu bo5 hoe, cheng-lek8 bo5 soe-the3.  8). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ti7 Mou5-ap piN5-iuN5 ui7-tioh8 Mou5-se ai-khau3 saN-chap8 jit8; ui7-tioh8 Mou5-se iu-bun7 ai-khau3 e5 jit8 moa2 lah.
	9). Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a tit-tioh8 ti3-hui7 e5 sin5 chhiong-moa2; in-ui7 Mou5-se bat hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 thiaN-than3 i, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5 lai5 kiaN5.  10). Au7-lai5 I2-sek-liat8-tiong bo5 koh heng-khi2 sian-ti chhin-chhiuN7 Mou5-se, i si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7 tui3 bin7 sou2 bat e5;  11). chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe i ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7, tui3 Hoat-lo2 kap i long2-chong2 e5 jin5-sin5, i2-kip8 i e5 choan5-toe7 sou2 kiaN5 tak8-iuN7 e5 sin5-jiah ki5-su7, ia7 chiau3 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2, toa7 thang kiaN e5 su7, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se sou2 kiaN5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 e5.
